000000r 1               v_reset:
000000r 1               
000000r 1  20 rr rr         JSR     copydata
000003r 1  20 rr rr         jsr zerobss
000006r 1               
000006r 1  4C rr rr         jmp kernel_init
000009r 1               
000009r 1               
000009r 1               
000009r 1               .segment "DATA"
000000r 1               
000000r 1               .include "drivers/acia.s"
000000r 2               .segment "DATA"
000000r 2               
000000r 2               acia_init:
000000r 2  8D E1 FF         sta ACIA_STATUS        ; soft reset (value not important)
000003r 2                                           ; set specific modes and functions
000003r 2  9C rr rr         stz has_acia
000006r 2  A9 0B            lda #$0B                ; no parity, no echo, no Tx interrupt, NO Rx interrupt, enable Tx/Rx
000008r 2                   ;lda #$09               ; no parity, no echo, no Tx interrupt, Rx interrupt, enable Tx/Rx
000008r 2  8D E2 FF         sta ACIA_CMD        ; store to the command register
00000Br 2  AD E2 FF         lda ACIA_CMD        ; load command register again
00000Er 2  C9 0B            cmp #$0B                ; if not the same
000010r 2  D0 11            bne acia_absent         ; then it means the ACIA is not connected
000012r 2  AD E1 FF         lda ACIA_STATUS         ; Read the ACAI status to
000015r 2  29 60            and #$60                ; check if present or absent
000017r 2  D0 0A            bne acia_absent
000019r 2  A9 01            lda #1
00001Br 2  8D rr rr         sta has_acia           ; remember that ACIA is here
00001Er 2  A9 10            lda #$10               ; 1 stop bits, 8 bit word length, internal clock, 115.200k baud rate
000020r 2                   ;lda #$10               ; 1 stop bits, 8 bit word length, internal clock, 1200 baud rate
000020r 2  8D E3 FF         sta ACIA_CTRL          ; program the ctl register
000023r 2               
000023r 2               acia_absent:
000023r 2  A0 14                ldy #20
000025r 2               aa_loop:
000025r 2  20 rr rr             jsr delay_short
000028r 2  AD E1 FF             lda ACIA_STATUS         ; Read ACIA data a few times
00002Br 2  AD E0 FF             lda ACIA_DATA           ; to try and prevent spurious characters
00002Er 2  88                   dey
00002Fr 2  D0 F4                bne aa_loop
000031r 2               aa_end:
000031r 2  60                   rts
000032r 2               
000032r 2               acia_out:
000032r 2  48               pha
000033r 2  5A               phy
000034r 2  8D E0 FF         sta ACIA_DATA
000037r 2  A0 20            ldy #$20            ;minimal delay is $02
000039r 2  20 rr rr         jsr delay_short
00003Cr 2  7A               ply
00003Dr 2  68               pla
00003Er 2  60               rts
00003Fr 2               
00003Fr 2               acia_getc:
00003Fr 2  AD E1 FF         lda ACIA_STATUS                 ; Read the ACIA status to
000042r 2  29 08            and #$08                        ; Check if there is character in the receiver
000044r 2  F0 05            beq @no_char      ; Exit now if we don't get one.
000046r 2  AD E0 FF         lda ACIA_DATA
000049r 2  38               sec
00004Ar 2  60               rts
00004Br 2               @no_char:
00004Br 2  18               clc
00004Cr 2  60               rts
00004Dr 2               
00004Dr 1               .include "drivers/timer.s"
00004Dr 2               
00004Dr 2               
00004Dr 2               COUNTER = CLOCK_SPEED/400        ; n/s
00004Dr 2               
00004Dr 2               .segment "ZEROPAGE": zeropage
000002r 2  xx xx xx xx  time: .res 4
000006r 2               
000006r 2               .segment "DATA"
00004Dr 2               
00004Dr 2               timer_init:
00004Dr 2  AD 8E FF         lda IER
000050r 2  09 C0            ora #$C0        ;enable interrupt on timer1 timeout
000052r 2  8D 8E FF         sta IER
000055r 2  A9 40            lda #$40        ; timer one free run mode
000057r 2  8D 8B FF         sta ACR
00005Ar 2  A9 60            lda #<COUNTER     ; set timer to low byte to calculated value from defined clock speed
00005Cr 2  8D 84 FF         sta T1CL
00005Fr 2  A9 EA            lda #>COUNTER       ; set timer to high byte to calculated value from defined clock speed
000061r 2               
000061r 2  8D 85 FF         sta T1CH
000064r 2  A9 00            lda #0              ; reset time variable
000066r 2  85 rr            sta time
000068r 2  85 rr            sta time+1
00006Ar 2  85 rr            sta time+2
00006Cr 2  85 rr            sta time+3
00006Er 2  58               cli
00006Fr 2  60               rts
000070r 2               
000070r 2               
000070r 2               timer_irq:
000070r 2  E6 rr            inc time
000072r 2  F0 01            beq @inc1
000074r 2               @exit1:
000074r 2                   ; this resets the PS/2 temp variables
000074r 2                   ;jsr reset_ps2
000074r 2  60               rts
000075r 2               @inc1:
000075r 2  E6 rr            inc time+1
000077r 2  F0 02            beq @inc2
000079r 2  80 F9            bra @exit1
00007Br 2               @inc2:
00007Br 2  E6 rr            inc time+2
00007Dr 2  F0 02            beq @inc3
00007Fr 2  80 F3            bra @exit1
000081r 2               @inc3:
000081r 2  E6 rr            inc time+3
000083r 2  80 EF            bra @exit1
000085r 2  60               rts

000086r 2               ps2_init:
000086r 2  78             sei ; prevent interrupts while initializing
000087r 2               kb_conn_msg:
000087r 2  A2 00          ldx #0
000089r 2               kb_conn_loop:
000089r 2  BD rr rr       lda kb_conn_msg_text,x
00008Cr 2  F0 1A          beq kb_conn_msg_end
00008Er 2  20 rr rr       jsr kernel_putc
000091r 2  E8             inx
000092r 2  80 F5          bra kb_conn_loop
000094r 2  44 65 74 65  kb_conn_msg_text: .byte "Detecting keyboard", $0D, $00
000098r 2  63 74 69 6E  
00009Cr 2  67 20 6B 65  
0000A8r 2               kb_conn_msg_end:
0000A8r 2               
0000A8r 2  AD 8E FF       lda IER
0000ABr 2  09 88          ora #$88      ;enable interrupt on neg transition on CB2
0000ADr 2  8D 8E FF       sta IER
0000B0r 2               
0000B0r 2  A9 00          lda #0
0000B2r 2  8D 8C FF       sta PCR
0000B5r 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_TEMP
0000B8r 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_BIT
0000BBr 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_STATE
0000BEr 2  8D rr rr       sta to_send
0000C1r 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_PARITY
0000C4r 2  85 rr          sta KB_BUF_W_PTR
0000C6r 2  85 rr          sta KB_BUF_R_PTR
0000C8r 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_INIT_STATE
0000CBr 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_INIT_WAIT
0000CEr 2  8D rr rr       sta ready
0000D1r 2  8D rr rr       sta ignore_next
0000D4r 2  85 rr          sta character
0000D6r 2  20 rr rr       jsr clear_buffer
0000D9r 2               
0000D9r 2                 ; jsr kb_reset
0000D9r 2                 ; jsr kb_leds
0000D9r 2                 ; jsr kb_leds_data
0000D9r 2               
0000D9r 2                 ; jmp done_init
0000D9r 2               
0000D9r 2  A9 00          lda #KB_INIT_STATE_RESET
0000DBr 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_INIT_STATE
0000DEr 2  58             cli           ;enable interrupts
0000DFr 2               
0000DFr 2               @wait1:
0000DFr 2  A0 0A          ldy #10
0000E1r 2  20 rr rr       jsr delay
0000E4r 2  EE rr rr       inc KB_INIT_WAIT
0000E7r 2  F0 1C          beq done_init     ; nothing to show yet
0000E9r 2  AD rr rr       lda to_send
0000ECr 2  D0 F1          bne @wait1       ; do nothing while sending
0000EEr 2               
0000EEr 2                 ;jsr lcd_print
0000EEr 2               
0000EEr 2  AE rr rr       ldx KB_INIT_STATE
0000F1r 2  E0 00          cpx #KB_INIT_STATE_RESET
0000F3r 2  F0 06          beq @do_reset
0000F5r 2  E0 01          cpx #KB_INIT_STATE_RESET_ACK
0000F7r 2  F0 0C          beq done_init
0000F9r 2                 ; beq @self_test_ok  ; Wait for 256 loops with nothing. if still nothing, reset keyboard
0000F9r 2               
0000F9r 2  80 0A          bra done_init
0000FBr 2                 ;sta PORTA
0000FBr 2                 ; wait for keyboard self test (#$AA)
0000FBr 2               
0000FBr 2               @do_reset:
0000FBr 2  20 rr rr       jsr kb_reset
0000FEr 2  A9 01          lda #KB_INIT_STATE_RESET_ACK  ; next state should be an acknowledgment
000100r 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_INIT_STATE
000103r 2  80 DA          bra @wait1
000105r 2               
000105r 2               
000105r 2               done_init:
000105r 2  A9 00          lda #0
000107r 2  8D 82 FF       sta DDRB
00010Ar 2  8D 8C FF       sta PCR
00010Dr 2  8D rr rr       sta ignore_next
000110r 2  8D rr rr       sta ready
000113r 2  85 rr          sta control_keys
000115r 2  8D rr rr       sta to_send
000118r 2  8D rr rr       sta ready
00011Br 2  85 rr          sta character
00011Dr 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_TEMP
000120r 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_INIT_STATE
000123r 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_BIT
000126r 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_STATE
000129r 2  85 rr          sta KB_BUF_W_PTR
00012Br 2  85 rr          sta KB_BUF_R_PTR
00012Dr 2  58             cli ; enable interrupts again
00012Er 2  60             rts
00012Fr 2               
00012Fr 2               
00012Fr 2               kb_reset:
00012Fr 2  A9 00          lda #0
000131r 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_INIT_WAIT
000134r 2  A9 F0          lda #$F0
000136r 2  8D 81 FF       sta PORTA
000139r 2  78             sei                   ;disable interrupts
00013Ar 2  20 rr rr       jsr prepare_send
00013Dr 2  A9 FF          lda #$FF
00013Fr 2  8D rr rr       sta to_send
000142r 2  58             cli                   ; enable interrupts
000143r 2  60             rts
000144r 2               
000144r 2               no_kb_msg:
000144r 2  A2 00          ldx #0
000146r 2               no_kb_loop:
000146r 2  BD rr rr       lda no_kb_msg_text,x
000149r 2  F0 BA          beq done_init
00014Br 2  20 rr rr       jsr kernel_putc
00014Er 2  E8             inx
00014Fr 2  80 F5          bra no_kb_loop
000151r 2  4E 6F 20 6B  no_kb_msg_text: .byte "No keyboard connected", $0D, $00
000155r 2  65 79 62 6F  
000159r 2  61 72 64 20  
000168r 2               
000168r 2               
000168r 2               prepare_send:
000168r 2  48             pha
000169r 2  5A             phy
00016Ar 2                 ; ready to send, pull clock low for a while
00016Ar 2  A9 C0          lda #$C0
00016Cr 2  8D 8C FF       sta PCR       ;set CB2 low
00016Fr 2                 ;delay
00016Fr 2  A0 80          ldy #$80
000171r 2  20 rr rr       jsr delay
000174r 2                 ; delay end
000174r 2                 ; pull data low now
000174r 2  AD 80 FF       lda PORTB
000177r 2  29 7F          and #($FF^DATA)
000179r 2  8D 80 FF       sta PORTB
00017Cr 2  AD 82 FF       lda DDRB
00017Fr 2  09 80          ora #DATA   ;data as output to set it low
000181r 2  8D 82 FF       sta DDRB
000184r 2  A0 40          ldy #$40
000186r 2  20 rr rr       jsr delay
000189r 2  A9 01          lda #KB_STATE_DATA    ; no start bit when sending
00018Br 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_STATE
00018Er 2                 ; release clock
00018Er 2  A9 00          lda #0
000190r 2  8D rr rr       sta to_send
000193r 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_PARITY
000196r 2  8D 8C FF       sta PCR       ;set CB2 to negative edge input
000199r 2               
000199r 2  7A             ply
00019Ar 2  68             pla
00019Br 2  60             rts
00019Cr 2               
00019Cr 2               
00019Cr 2               reset_ps2:          ; routine called during a timer interrupt to check
00019Cr 2  48             pha
00019Dr 2                                   ; if the elasped time since the last ps2 interrupt allows us to reset it
00019Dr 2  A5 rr          lda time+3
00019Fr 2  C5 rr          cmp last_ps2_time+3
0001A1r 2  90 16          bcc @reset
0001A3r 2  A5 rr          lda time+2
0001A5r 2  C5 rr          cmp last_ps2_time+2
0001A7r 2  90 10          bcc @reset
0001A9r 2  A5 rr          lda time+1
0001ABr 2  C5 rr          cmp last_ps2_time+1
0001ADr 2  90 0A          bcc @reset
0001AFr 2  A5 rr          lda time
0001B1r 2  69 01          adc #$1
0001B3r 2  C5 rr          cmp last_ps2_time
0001B5r 2  90 02          bcc @reset
0001B7r 2               @exit2:
0001B7r 2  68             pla
0001B8r 2  60             rts
0001B9r 2               @reset:
0001B9r 2  A9 00          lda #0
0001BBr 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_TEMP
0001BEr 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_BIT
0001C1r 2  8D rr rr       sta KB_STATE
0001C4r 2  85 rr          sta KB_BUF_W_PTR
0001C6r 2  85 rr          sta KB_BUF_R_PTR
0001C8r 2  F0 ED          beq @exit2
0001CAr 2               
0001CAr 2               clear_buffer:
0001CAr 2  DA             phx
0001CBr 2  A2 FF          ldx #$ff
0001CDr 2               @clear_loop:
0001CDr 2  9E rr rr       stz KB_BUF, x
0001D0r 2  CA             dex
0001D1r 2  D0 FA          bne @clear_loop
0001D3r 2  FA             plx
0001D4r 2  60             rts
0001D5r 2               
0001D5r 2               
0001D5r 2               ps2_get_char:
0001D5r 2               
0001D5r 2  DA               phx                             ; save X
0001D6r 2  A6 rr            ldx KB_BUF_R_PTR                ; check the keyboard buffer
0001D8r 2  BD rr rr         lda KB_BUF, x
0001DBr 2  F0 0B            beq no_ps2_char_available       ; exit if nothing found
0001DDr 2  9E rr rr         stz KB_BUF, x                   ; if there was a character, reset this buffer cell
0001E0r 2  E6 rr            inc KB_BUF_R_PTR                ; and increment the read pointer
0001E2r 2               
0001E2r 2  38               sec                             ; mark character present
0001E3r 2  FA               plx                             ; restore X
0001E4r 2  20 rr rr         jsr check_ctrl_c
0001E7r 2  60               rts                             ; return
0001E8r 2               no_ps2_char_available:                  ; no keyboard char
0001E8r 2  E6 rr            inc KB_BUF_R_PTR                ; increment read pointer for next time
0001EAr 2  FA               plx                             ; restore X
0001EBr 2  18               clc
0001ECr 2  60               rts
0001EDr 2                 .include "ps2_irq.s"

0001EDr 3               
0001EDr 3               ps2_irq:
0001EDr 3  48               pha
0001EEr 3  DA               phx
0001EFr 3  AD rr rr         lda to_send
0001F2r 3  D0 25            bne @willsend
0001F4r 3  AD rr rr         lda KB_STATE            ; which state ?
0001F7r 3  C9 00            cmp #KB_STATE_START
0001F9r 3  F0 0F            beq @start        ; start bit
0001FBr 3               
0001FBr 3  C9 01            cmp #KB_STATE_DATA             ; get data bits
0001FDr 3  F0 1D            beq @data
0001FFr 3               
0001FFr 3  C9 02            cmp #KB_STATE_PARITY             ; this is the parity bit
000201r 3  F0 3A            beq @parity
000203r 3               
000203r 3  C9 03            cmp #KB_STATE_STOP      ; stop bit
000205r 3  F0 3D            beq @stop
000207r 3  4C rr rr         jmp @exit
00020Ar 3               
00020Ar 3               @start:
00020Ar 3  A9 01            lda #KB_STATE_DATA
00020Cr 3  8D rr rr         sta KB_STATE        ; next state will be to get data
00020Fr 3  A9 00            lda #0
000211r 3  8D rr rr         sta KB_TEMP
000214r 3  8D rr rr         sta KB_BIT
000217r 3  80 65            bra @exit
000219r 3               @willsend:
000219r 3  4C rr rr         jmp @sending
00021Cr 3               @data:
00021Cr 3  AD 80 FF         lda PORTB       ; get the bit of data from PORTB bit 7
00021Fr 3  29 80            and #$80
000221r 3  0D rr rr         ora KB_TEMP     ; OR it with existing temp data
000224r 3  8D rr rr         sta KB_TEMP     ; save it
000227r 3  EE rr rr         inc KB_BIT      ; prepare for next bit
00022Ar 3  AD rr rr         lda KB_BIT
00022Dr 3  C9 08            cmp #8          ; if this is the last bit, next state is parity
00022Fr 3  F0 05            beq @next_state_parity
000231r 3  4E rr rr         lsr KB_TEMP     ; if not last bit, shift KB_TEMP right to prepare for next bit
000234r 3               
000234r 3  80 48            bra @exit
000236r 3               
000236r 3               @next_state_parity:
000236r 3  A9 02            lda #KB_STATE_PARITY    ;next state is parity
000238r 3  8D rr rr         sta KB_STATE
00023Br 3  80 41            bra @exit
00023Dr 3               
00023Dr 3               @parity:
00023Dr 3  A9 03            lda #KB_STATE_STOP      ;next state is stop
00023Fr 3  8D rr rr         sta KB_STATE
000242r 3  80 3A            bra @exit
000244r 3               
000244r 3               @stop:
000244r 3  A9 00            lda #KB_STATE_START
000246r 3  8D rr rr         sta KB_STATE
000249r 3  AD rr rr         lda ignore_next
00024Cr 3  D0 45            bne @ignored
00024Er 3                   ; Save key to character buffer
00024Er 3  AE rr rr         ldx KB_TEMP
000251r 3  E0 AA            cpx #$AA
000253r 3  F0 32            beq @init
000255r 3  E0 FA            cpx #$FA
000257r 3  F0 2E            beq @init
000259r 3  E0 F0            cpx #$F0
00025Br 3  F0 2F            beq @ignore_next
00025Dr 3  E0 12            cpx #LSHIFT_KEY
00025Fr 3  F0 4F            beq @shift_pressed
000261r 3  E0 59            cpx #RSHIFT_KEY
000263r 3  F0 4B            beq @shift_pressed
000265r 3  A5 rr            lda control_keys
000267r 3  29 01            and #SHIFT
000269r 3  D0 09            bne @shifted
00026Br 3               @unshifted:
00026Br 3                   ;stx PORTA
00026Br 3  BD rr rr         lda ASCIITBL, x
00026Er 3               
00026Er 3  C9 1B            cmp #$1B             ; reset if escape pressed
000270r 3  F0 12            beq @esc
000272r 3  80 03            bra @output
000274r 3               @shifted:
000274r 3  BD rr rr         lda ASCIITBL+128, x
000277r 3               @output:
000277r 3  A6 rr            ldx KB_BUF_W_PTR
000279r 3  9D rr rr         sta KB_BUF, x
00027Cr 3                   ;sta PORTA
00027Cr 3  E6 rr            inc KB_BUF_W_PTR
00027Er 3               
00027Er 3               @exit:
00027Er 3  2C 80 FF         bit PORTB
000281r 3  FA               plx
000282r 3  68               pla
000283r 3  60               rts
000284r 3               @esc:
000284r 3  4C rr rr         jmp v_reset
000287r 3               @init:
000287r 3  8E rr rr         stx ready
00028Ar 3  80 F2            bra @exit
00028Cr 3               
00028Cr 3               @ignore_next:
00028Cr 3  A9 01            lda #1
00028Er 3  8D rr rr         sta ignore_next
000291r 3  80 EB            bra @exit
000293r 3               
000293r 3               @ignored:
000293r 3  AE rr rr         ldx KB_TEMP
000296r 3  E0 12            cpx #LSHIFT_KEY
000298r 3  F0 0B            beq @shift_released
00029Ar 3  E0 59            cpx #RSHIFT_KEY
00029Cr 3  F0 07            beq @shift_released
00029Er 3  A9 00            lda #0
0002A0r 3  8D rr rr         sta ignore_next
0002A3r 3  80 D9            bra @exit
0002A5r 3               
0002A5r 3               @shift_released:
0002A5r 3  A9 00            lda #0
0002A7r 3  8D rr rr         sta ignore_next
0002AAr 3  A9 00            lda #0
0002ACr 3  85 rr            sta control_keys
0002AEr 3  80 CE            bra @exit
0002B0r 3               
0002B0r 3               @shift_pressed:
0002B0r 3  A5 rr            lda control_keys
0002B2r 3  09 01            ora #SHIFT
0002B4r 3  85 rr            sta control_keys
0002B6r 3  80 C6            bra @exit
0002B8r 3               
0002B8r 3               @sending:
0002B8r 3                   ; lda #1
0002B8r 3                   ; sta PORTA
0002B8r 3                   ; data pin of DDRB should be set as output by prepare_send
0002B8r 3  AD rr rr         lda KB_STATE                ; which state ?
0002BBr 3  C9 01            cmp #KB_STATE_DATA          ; send data bits
0002BDr 3  F0 0A            beq @sending_data
0002BFr 3  C9 02            cmp #KB_STATE_PARITY        ; this is the parity bit
0002C1r 3  F0 33            beq @sending_parity
0002C3r 3  C9 03            cmp #KB_STATE_STOP          ; stop bit
0002C5r 3  F0 56            beq @sending_stop
0002C7r 3  80 B5            bra @exit
0002C9r 3               
0002C9r 3               
0002C9r 3               @sending_data:
0002C9r 3                   ; lda #4
0002C9r 3                   ; sta PORTA
0002C9r 3  AD rr rr         lda to_send       ; get the bit of data from memory
0002CCr 3  29 01            and #$01          ; get only bottom bit
0002CEr 3  F0 0D            beq @send_zero
0002D0r 3               
0002D0r 3               @send_one:
0002D0r 3  AD 80 FF         lda PORTB
0002D3r 3  09 80            ora #$80
0002D5r 3  8D 80 FF         sta PORTB
0002D8r 3  EE rr rr         inc KB_PARITY
0002DBr 3  80 08            bra @sending_done
0002DDr 3               @send_zero:
0002DDr 3  AD 80 FF         lda PORTB
0002E0r 3  29 7F            and #$7F
0002E2r 3  8D 80 FF         sta PORTB
0002E5r 3               @sending_done:
0002E5r 3                   ; lda #2
0002E5r 3                   ; sta PORTA
0002E5r 3  EE rr rr         inc KB_BIT      ; prepare for next bit
0002E8r 3  AD rr rr         lda KB_BIT
0002EBr 3  C9 08            cmp #8          ; if this is the last bit, next state is parity
0002EDr 3  4C rr rr         jmp @next_state_parity
0002F0r 3  4E rr rr         lsr to_send
0002F3r 3  18               clc
0002F4r 3  80 88            bra @exit
0002F6r 3               
0002F6r 3               @sending_parity:
0002F6r 3                   ; lda #5
0002F6r 3                   ; sta PORTA
0002F6r 3  AD rr rr         lda KB_PARITY
0002F9r 3  29 01            and #$01
0002FBr 3  F0 10            beq @odd_parity     ; send zero if odd parity
0002FDr 3  AD 80 FF         lda PORTB
000300r 3  09 80            ora #$80            ; send one if even
000302r 3  8D 80 FF         sta PORTB
000305r 3  A9 03            lda #KB_STATE_STOP      ;next state is stop
000307r 3  8D rr rr         sta KB_STATE
00030Ar 3  4C rr rr         jmp @exit
00030Dr 3               @odd_parity:
00030Dr 3  AD 80 FF         lda PORTB
000310r 3  29 7F            and #$7F
000312r 3  8D 80 FF         sta PORTB
000315r 3  A9 03            lda #KB_STATE_STOP      ;next state is stop
000317r 3  8D rr rr         sta KB_STATE
00031Ar 3  4C rr rr         jmp @exit
00031Dr 3               
00031Dr 3               @sending_stop:
00031Dr 3                   ; lda #6
00031Dr 3                   ; sta PORTA
00031Dr 3  A9 00            lda #KB_STATE_START     ; set it back to start in case we are receivin next
00031Fr 3  8D rr rr         sta KB_STATE
000322r 3  A9 00            lda #0
000324r 3  8D rr rr         sta to_send
000327r 3  8D rr rr         sta KB_BIT
00032Ar 3  8D rr rr         sta KB_PARITY
00032Dr 3  AD 82 FF         lda DDRB        ; set PORTB back to input
000330r 3  29 7F            and #$7F
000332r 3  8D 82 FF         sta DDRB
000335r 3  4C rr rr         jmp @exit
000338r 3               
000338r 2

000338r 2               .segment "CODE"
000000r 2               ; this routine delays by 2304 * y + 23 cycles
000000r 2               delay:
000000r 2  DA             phx       ; 3 cycles
000001r 2  5A             phy       ; 3 cycles
000002r 2               two:
000002r 2  A2 FF          ldx #$ff  ; 2 cycles
000004r 2               one:
000004r 2  EA             nop       ; 2 cycles
000005r 2  EA             nop       ; 2 cycles
000006r 2  CA             dex       ; 2 cycles
000007r 2  D0 FB          bne one   ; 3 for all cycles, 2 for last
000009r 2  88             dey       ; 2 cycles
00000Ar 2  D0 F6          bne two   ; 3 for all cycles, 2 for last
00000Cr 2  7A             ply       ; 4 cycles
00000Dr 2  FA             plx       ; 4 cycles
00000Er 2  60             rts       ; 6 cycles
00000Fr 2               
00000Fr 2               ; delay is in Y register
00000Fr 2               delay_long:
00000Fr 2  48             pha
000010r 2  5A             phy
000011r 2  DA             phx
000012r 2  98             tya
000013r 2  AA             tax
000014r 2               delay_long_loop:
000014r 2  A0 FF          ldy #$ff
000016r 2  20 rr rr       jsr delay
000019r 2  CA             dex
00001Ar 2  D0 F8          bne delay_long_loop
00001Cr 2  FA             plx
00001Dr 2  7A             ply
00001Er 2  68             pla
00001Fr 2  60             rts
000020r 2               
000020r 2               delay_short:        ; delay Y * 19 cycles
000020r 2  5A             phy
000021r 2               delay_short_loop:
000021r 2  EA             nop               ; 2 cycles
000022r 2  EA             nop               ; 2 cycles
000023r 2  EA             nop               ; 2 cycles
000024r 2  EA             nop               ; 2 cycles
000025r 2  EA             nop               ; 2 cycles
000026r 2  EA             nop               ; 2 cycles
000027r 2  EA             nop               ; 2 cycles
000028r 2               
000028r 2               
000028r 2  88             dey               ; 2 cycles
000029r 2  D0 F6          bne delay_short_loop   ; 2 or 3 cycles
00002Br 2  7A             ply
00002Cr 2  60             rts
00002Dr 2               
00002Dr 1               ; .include "drivers/4004.s"
00002Dr 1               .include "drivers/cf.s"
00002Dr 2

00002Dr 2               CF_ADDRESS = $FFD0
00002Dr 2

000338r 2               cf_wait:
000338r 2                   ; phy
000338r 2                   ; ldy #7
000338r 2               @wait_loop:
000338r 2                   ; lda (CF_ADDRESS), y
000338r 2  AD D7 FF         lda CF_ADDRESS + 7
00033Br 2  29 80            and #$80
00033Dr 2  D0 F9            bne @wait_loop
00033Fr 2                   ; ply
00033Fr 2  60               rts
000340r 2               
000340r 2               
000340r 2               cf_init:
000340r 2                   ; phy
000340r 2  A9 04            lda #$4
000342r 2                   ; ldy #7
000342r 2                   ; sta (CF_ADDRESS),y
000342r 2  8D D7 FF         sta CF_ADDRESS + 7
000345r 2  20 rr rr         jsr cf_wait
000348r 2  A9 E0            lda #$E0
00034Ar 2                   ; ldy #6
00034Ar 2                   ; sta (CF_ADDRESS),y
00034Ar 2  8D D6 FF         sta CF_ADDRESS + 6
00034Dr 2  A9 01            lda #$1
00034Fr 2                   ; ldy #1
00034Fr 2                   ; sta (CF_ADDRESS),y
00034Fr 2  8D D1 FF         sta CF_ADDRESS + 1
000352r 2  A9 EF            lda #$EF
000354r 2                   ; ldy #7
000354r 2                   ; sta (CF_ADDRESS),y
000354r 2  8D D7 FF         sta CF_ADDRESS + 7
000357r 2  20 rr rr         jsr cf_wait
00035Ar 2  20 rr rr         jsr cf_err
00035Dr 2                   ; ply
00035Dr 2  60               rts
00035Er 2               
00035Er 2               
00035Er 2               ; cf_read:
00035Er 2               ;     phy
00035Er 2               ;     ldy #0
00035Er 2               ; @readloop:
00035Er 2               ;     ; phy
00035Er 2               ;     ; ldy #7
00035Er 2               ;     ; lda (CF_ADDRESS), y
00035Er 2               ;     lda CF_ADDRESS + 7
00035Er 2               ;     and #8
00035Er 2               ;     beq @exit
00035Er 2               ;     ; jsr cf_wait
00035Er 2               ;     ; ldy #0
00035Er 2               ;     ; lda (CF_ADDRESS), y
00035Er 2               ;     lda CF_ADDRESS
00035Er 2               ;     ; ply
00035Er 2               ;     sta (CF_BUF_PTR), y
00035Er 2               ;     ; jsr cf_wait
00035Er 2               ;     iny
00035Er 2               ;     bne @readloop
00035Er 2               ;     ; if y wraps around to zero, increment buffer page
00035Er 2               ;     inc CF_BUF_PTR+1
00035Er 2               ;     bra @readloop
00035Er 2               ; @exit:
00035Er 2               ;     ; we only come here because we read an & 8 from REG 7
00035Er 2               ;     ; ply
00035Er 2               ;     dec CF_BUF_PTR+1
00035Er 2               ;     ply
00035Er 2               ;     rts
00035Er 2               
00035Er 2               ; : cfread 0 buffptr ! begin cfwait cfreg7 c@ 8 and while cfreg0 c@ cfbuffer buffptr @ + c! buffptr @ 1 + buffptr ! repeat ;
00035Er 2               
00035Er 2               cf_read:
00035Er 2  DA               phx
00035Fr 2  A2 00            ldx #0
000361r 2               @loop1:
000361r 2                   ;jsr cf_wait
000361r 2                   ; lda CF_ADDRESS + 7
000361r 2                   ; and #8
000361r 2                   ; beq @exit
000361r 2                   ; jsr cf_wait
000361r 2  AD D0 FF         lda CF_ADDRESS
000364r 2  9D rr rr         sta FAT_BUFFER, x
000367r 2  E8               inx
000368r 2  D0 F7            bne @loop1
00036Ar 2               @loop2:
00036Ar 2                   ;jsr cf_wait
00036Ar 2                   ; lda CF_ADDRESS + 7
00036Ar 2                   ; and #8
00036Ar 2                   ; beq @exit
00036Ar 2                   ; jsr cf_wait
00036Ar 2  AD D0 FF         lda CF_ADDRESS
00036Dr 2  9D rr rr         sta FAT_BUFFER+256, x
000370r 2  E8               inx
000371r 2  D0 F7            bne @loop2
000373r 2               @loop3:
000373r 2  AD D7 FF         lda CF_ADDRESS + 7
000376r 2  29 08            and #8
000378r 2  F0 06            beq @exit
00037Ar 2  AD D0 FF         lda CF_ADDRESS
00037Dr 2  E8               inx
00037Er 2  D0 F3            bne @loop3
000380r 2               @exit:
000380r 2  FA               plx
000381r 2  60               rts
000382r 2               
000382r 2               cf_set_lba:
000382r 2                   ; phy
000382r 2  AD rr rr         lda CF_LBA
000385r 2                   ; ldy #3
000385r 2                   ; sta (CF_ADDRESS),y
000385r 2  8D D3 FF         sta CF_ADDRESS + 3
000388r 2  AD rr rr         lda CF_LBA + 1
00038Br 2                   ; ldy #4
00038Br 2                   ; sta (CF_ADDRESS), y
00038Br 2  8D D4 FF         sta CF_ADDRESS + 4
00038Er 2  AD rr rr         lda CF_LBA + 2
000391r 2                   ; ldy #5
000391r 2                   ; sta (CF_ADDRESS), y
000391r 2  8D D5 FF         sta CF_ADDRESS + 5
000394r 2  AD rr rr         lda CF_LBA + 3
000397r 2  29 0F            and #$0F
000399r 2  09 E0            ora #$E0
00039Br 2                   ; ldy #6
00039Br 2                   ; sta (CF_ADDRESS), y
00039Br 2  8D D6 FF         sta CF_ADDRESS + 6
00039Er 2                   ; ply
00039Er 2  60               rts
00039Fr 2               
00039Fr 2               cf_read_sector:
00039Fr 2                   ; phy
00039Fr 2                   ; buffer should be set in CF_BUF_PTR
00039Fr 2  20 rr rr         jsr cf_set_lba
0003A2r 2  A9 01            lda #1
0003A4r 2                   ; ldy #2
0003A4r 2                   ; sta (CF_ADDRESS), y
0003A4r 2  8D D2 FF         sta CF_ADDRESS + 2
0003A7r 2  20 rr rr         jsr cf_wait
0003AAr 2  A9 20            lda #CF_READ_SECTOR_COMMAND
0003ACr 2                   ; ldy #7
0003ACr 2                   ; sta (CF_ADDRESS), y
0003ACr 2  8D D7 FF         sta CF_ADDRESS + 7
0003AFr 2  20 rr rr         jsr cf_wait
0003B2r 2  20 rr rr         jsr cf_read
0003B5r 2  20 rr rr         jsr cf_err
0003B8r 2                   ; ply
0003B8r 2  60               rts
0003B9r 2               
0003B9r 2               cf_err:
0003B9r 2                   ; phy
0003B9r 2  20 rr rr         jsr cf_wait
0003BCr 2                   ; ldy #7
0003BCr 2                   ; lda (CF_ADDRESS), y
0003BCr 2  AD D7 FF         lda CF_ADDRESS + 7
0003BFr 2  29 01            and #$01
0003C1r 2  F0 05            beq @exit
0003C3r 2               @exit_fail:
0003C3r 2  A9 21            lda #'!'
0003C5r 2  20 rr rr         jsr kernel_putc
0003C8r 2               @exit:
0003C8r 2                   ; ply
0003C8r 2  60               rts

0003C9r 3               .macro  printascii   addr
0003C9r 3               .local @loop
0003C9r 3               .local @done
0003C9r 3                   phx
0003C9r 3                   ldx #0
0003C9r 3               @loop:
0003C9r 3                   lda addr,x
0003C9r 3                   beq @done
0003C9r 3                   jsr kernel_putc
0003C9r 3                   inx
0003C9r 3                   bra @loop
0003C9r 3               @done:
0003C9r 3                   plx
0003C9r 3               .endmacro

0003C9r 3               .macro  cp16   src, dest
0003C9r 3                   lda src
0003C9r 3                   sta dest
0003C9r 3                   lda src + 1
0003C9r 3                   sta dest + 1
0003C9r 3               .endmacro
0003C9r 3               
0003C9r 3               .macro printstr addr, len
0003C9r 3               .repeat len, I
0003C9r 3               lda addr + I
0003C9r 3               jsr kernel_putc
0003C9r 3               .endrepeat
0003C9r 3               .endmacro
0003C9r 3               
0003C9r 3               .macro asl16 src
0003C9r 3                   asl src
0003C9r 3                   rol src + 1
0003C9r 3               .endmacro
0003C9r 3               
0003C9r 3               .macro lsr16 src
0003C9r 3                   lsr src + 1
0003C9r 3                   ror src
0003C9r 3               .endmacro
0003C9r 3               
0003C9r 3               .macro inc16 src
0003C9r 3                   inc src       ;Increment the LSB
0003C9r 3                   bne @done       ;If the result was not zero we're done
0003C9r 3                   inc src+1       ;Increment the MSB if LSB wrapped round
0003C9r 3               @done:
0003C9r 3               .endmacro
0003C9r 3               
0003C9r 3               .macro dec16 src
0003C9r 3                   lda src
0003C9r 3                   bne @skip
0003C9r 3                   dec src + 1
0003C9r 3               @skip:
0003C9r 3                   dec src
0003C9r 3               .endmacro
0003C9r 3               
0003C9r 3               .macro add16 first, second, result
0003C9r 3                   CLC             ;Ensure carry is clear
0003C9r 3                   LDA first+0       ;Add the two least significant bytes
0003C9r 3                   ADC second+0
0003C9r 3                   STA result+0       ;... and store the result
0003C9r 3                   LDA first+1       ;Add the two most significant bytes
0003C9r 3                   ADC second+1       ;... and any propagated carry bit
0003C9r 3                   STA result+1       ;... and store the result
0003C9r 3               .endmacro
0003C9r 3               
0003C9r 3

0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               ; Definitions for Tali Forth 2
0003C9r 2               ; Scot W. Stevenson <scot.stevenson@gmail.com>
0003C9r 2               ; First version: 01. Apr 2016 (Liara Forth)
0003C9r 2               ; This version: 29. Jan 2020
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               ; This file is included by taliforth.asm. These are the general
0003C9r 2               ; definitions; platform-specific definitions such as the
0003C9r 2               ; memory map are kept in the platform folder.
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               stack0 =    $0100   ; location of the stack
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               ; User Variables:
0003C9r 2               ; Block variables
0003C9r 2               blk_offset =  0        ; BLK : UP + 0
0003C9r 2               scr_offset =  2        ; SCR : UP + 2
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               ; Wordlists
0003C9r 2               current_offset =  4    ; CURRENT (byte) : UP + 4 (Compilation wordlist)
0003C9r 2               num_wordlists_offset =  5
0003C9r 2                                          ; #WORDLISTS (byte) : UP + 5
0003C9r 2               wordlists_offset =  6  ; WORDLISTS (cells) : UP + 6 to UP + 29
0003C9r 2                                          ;          (FORTH, EDITOR, ASSEMBLER, ROOT, +8 more)
0003C9r 2               num_order_offset =  30 ; #ORDER (byte) : UP + 30
0003C9r 2                                          ;          (Number of wordlists in search order)
0003C9r 2               search_order_offset =  31
0003C9r 2                                          ; SEARCH-ORDER (bytes) : UP + 31 to UP + 39
0003C9r 2                                          ; Allowing for 9 to keep offsets even.
0003C9r 2               max_wordlists =  12    ; Maximum number of wordlists supported
0003C9r 2                                          ; 4 Tali built-ins + 8 user wordlists
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               ; Buffer variables
0003C9r 2               blkbuffer_offset =     40   ; Address of buffer
0003C9r 2               buffblocknum_offset =  42   ; Block number current in buffer
0003C9r 2               buffstatus_offset =    44   ; Status of buffer (bit 0 = used, bit 1 = dirty)
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               ; Block I/O vectors
0003C9r 2               blockread_offset =     46   ; Vector to block reading routine
0003C9r 2               blockwrite_offset =    48   ; Vector to block writing routine
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               ; ASCII CHARACTERS
0003C9r 2               AscCC =   $03  ; break (CTRL-c)
0003C9r 2               AscBELL = $07  ; bell sound
0003C9r 2               AscBS =   $08  ; backspace
0003C9r 2               AscLF =   $0a  ; line feed
0003C9r 2               AscCR =   $0d  ; carriage return
0003C9r 2               AscESC =  $1b  ; escape
0003C9r 2               AscSP =   $20  ; space
0003C9r 2               AscDEL =  $7f  ; delete (CTRL-h)
0003C9r 2               AscCP =   $10  ; CTRL-p (used to recall previous input history)
0003C9r 2               AscCN =   $0e  ; CTRL-n (used to recall next input history)
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               ; DICTIONARY FLAGS
0003C9r 2               ; The first three bits are currently unused
0003C9r 2               CO = 1  ; Compile Only
0003C9r 2               AN = 2  ; Always Native Compile
0003C9r 2               IM = 4  ; Immediate Word
0003C9r 2               NN = 8  ; Never Native Compile
0003C9r 2               UF = 16 ; Includes Underflow Check (RESERVED)
0003C9r 2               HC = 32 ; Word has Code Field Area (CFA)
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               ; VARIOUS
0003C9r 2               MAX_LINE_LENGTH =   79      ; assumes 80 character lines
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               ; END
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               .segment "ZEROPAGE": zeropage
00000Er 2               ; ZERO PAGE ADDRESSES/VARIABLES
00000Er 2               
00000Er 2               ; These are kept at the top of Zero Page, with the most important variables at
00000Er 2               ; the top because the Data Stack grows towards this area from dsp0: If there is
00000Er 2               ; an overflow, the lower, less important variables will be clobbered first,
00000Er 2               ; giving the system a chance to recover. In other words, they are part of the
00000Er 2               ; floodplain.
00000Er 2               
00000Er 2               ; The four variables insrc, cib, ciblen, and toin must stay together in this
00000Er 2               ; sequence for the words INPUT>R and R>INPUT to work correctly.
00000Er 2               
00000Er 2  xx xx        cp: .res 2   ; Compiler Pointer
000010r 2  xx xx        dp: .res 2   ; Dictionary Pointer
000012r 2  xx xx        workword: .res 2   ; nt (not xt!) of word being compiled, except in
000014r 2                                          ; a :NONAME declared word (see status)
000014r 2  xx xx        insrc: .res 2   ; input Source for SOURCE-ID
000016r 2  xx xx        cib: .res 2   ; address of current input buffer
000018r 2  xx xx        ciblen: .res 2  ; length of current input buffer
00001Ar 2  xx xx        toin: .res 2  ; pointer to CIB (>IN in Forth)
00001Cr 2  xx xx        ip: .res 2  ; Instruction Pointer (current xt)
00001Er 2  xx xx        output: .res 2  ; vector for EMIT
000020r 2  xx xx        input: .res 2  ; vector for KEY
000022r 2  xx xx        havekey: .res 2  ; vector for KEY?
000024r 2  xx xx        state: .res 2  ; STATE: -1 compile, 0 interpret
000026r 2  xx xx        base: .res 2  ; number radix, default decimal
000028r 2  xx xx        nc_limit: .res 2  ; limit for Native Compile size
00002Ar 2  xx xx        uf_strip: .res 2  ; flag to strip underflow detection code
00002Cr 2  xx xx        up: .res 2  ; User Pointer (Address of user variables)
00002Er 2  xx xx        status: .res 2  ; internal status information
000030r 2                                          ; (used by : :NONAME ; ACCEPT)
000030r 2                                          ; Bit 7 = Redefined word message postpone
000030r 2                                          ;         When set before calling CREATE, it will
000030r 2                                          ;         not print the "redefined xxxx" message if
000030r 2                                          ;         the word exists. Instead, this bit will
000030r 2                                          ;         be reused and after CREATE has run, it will
000030r 2                                          ;         be set if the word was redefined and 0 if
000030r 2                                          ;         not. This bit should be 0 when not in use.
000030r 2                                          ; Bit 6 = 1 for normal ":" definitions
000030r 2                                          ;         WORKWORD contains nt of word being compiled
000030r 2                                          ;       = 0 for :NONAME definitions
000030r 2                                          ;         WORKWORD contains xt of word being compiled
000030r 2                                          ; Bit 5 = 1 for NUMBER returning a double word
000030r 2                                          ;       = 0 for NUMBER returning a single word
000030r 2                                          ; Bit 3 = 1 makes CTRL-n recall current history
000030r 2                                          ;       = 0 CTRL-n recalls previous history
000030r 2                                          ; Bit 2 = Current history buffer msb
000030r 2                                          ; Bit 1 = Current history buffer (0-7, wraps)
000030r 2                                          ; Bit 0 = Current history buffer lsb
000030r 2                                          ; status+1 is used by ACCEPT to hold history lengths.
000030r 2  xx xx        tmpbranch: .res 2  ; temporary storage for 0BRANCH, BRANCH only
000032r 2  xx xx        tmp1: .res 2  ; temporary storage
000034r 2  xx xx        tmp2: .res 2  ; temporary storage
000036r 2  xx xx        tmp3: .res 2  ; temporary storage (especially for print)
000038r 2  xx xx        tmpdsp: .res 2  ; temporary DSP (X) storage (two bytes)
00003Ar 2  xx xx        tmptos: .res 2  ; temporary TOS storage
00003Cr 2  xx xx        editor1: .res 2  ; temporary for editors
00003Er 2  xx xx        editor2: .res 2  ; temporary for editors
000040r 2  xx xx        editor3: .res 2  ; temporary for editors
000042r 2  xx xx        tohold: .res 2  ; pointer for formatted output
000044r 2  xx xx xx xx  scratch: .res 8  ; 8 byte scratchpad (see UM/MOD)
000048r 2  xx xx xx xx  
00004Cr 2               
00004Cr 2               .segment "DATASTACK": zeropage
000000r 2  xx xx xx xx  dsp_start: .res 127 ; reserve 128 bytes for data stack (64 16 bit cells)
000004r 2  xx xx xx xx  
000008r 2  xx xx xx xx  
00007Fr 2               dsp0:          ; first data stack location. Data stack grows down
00007Fr 2               rsp0:     ; starting stack pointer
00007Fr 2               
00007Fr 2               
00007Fr 2               
00007Fr 2               
00007Fr 2               .segment "BSS"
000089r 2  xx xx xx xx  hist_buff: .res $400
00008Dr 2  xx xx xx xx  
000091r 2  xx xx xx xx  
000489r 2  xx xx xx xx  buffer0: .res $100
00048Dr 2  xx xx xx xx  
000491r 2  xx xx xx xx  
000589r 2               
000589r 2               .segment "DICTIONARY"   ; the dictionary gets its own segment so that it uses all the space left in RAM
000000r 2  xx xx xx xx  dictionary: .res $1000
000004r 2  xx xx xx xx  
000008r 2  xx xx xx xx  
001000r 2               
001000r 2               cp_end = $7FFF          ; the dictionary ends at RAM end (everything else is before)
001000r 2               
001000r 2               cp0 = dictionary
001000r 2               bsize =     $ff
001000r 2               padoffset = $ff
001000r 2               
001000r 2               
001000r 2               .segment "DATA"
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               ; .include "fat16.s"
0003C9r 2               
0003C9r 2               forth:
0003C9r 2                   .include "native_words.s"     ; Native Forth words. Starts with COLD
0003C9r 3               ; Low-level Forth word routines
0003C9r 3               ; Tali Forth 2 for the 65c02
0003C9r 3               ; Scot W. Stevenson <scot.stevenson@gmail.com>
0003C9r 3               ; First version: 19. Jan 2014
0003C9r 3               ; This version: 03. Jan 2018
0003C9r 3               
0003C9r 3               ; This list is ordered alphabetically by the names of the words, not their
0003C9r 3               ; strings (so "!" is sorted as "STORE"). However, we start off with COLD,
0003C9r 3               ; ABORT, and QUIT as the natural start sequence. Each word has two special
0003C9r 3               ; status lines that begins with "; ## ", which allows auto-generation of the
0003C9r 3               ; WORDLIST.md file and other entries in the docs folder. Status entries are:
0003C9r 3               
0003C9r 3               ;       TBA --> fragment --> coded --> tested --> auto
0003C9r 3               
0003C9r 3               ; "Auto" means that the word is automatically tested by the test suite (good),
0003C9r 3               ; "tested" means that it was tested by hand in some way (okay), "coded" means
0003C9r 3               ; it hasn't been tested at all (bad). See the test suite for more details.
0003C9r 3               
0003C9r 3               ; ## COLD ( -- ) "Reset the Forth system"
0003C9r 3               ; ## "cold"  tested  Tali Forth
0003C9r 3               ;       """Reset the Forth system. Does not restart the kernel,
0003C9r 3               ;       use the 65c02 reset for that. Flows into ABORT.
0003C9r 3               ;       """
0003C9r 3               xt_cold:
0003C9r 3  D8                           cld
0003CAr 3               
0003CAr 3                               ; Set the OUTPUT vector to the default kernel_putc
0003CAr 3                               ; We do this really early so we can print error messages
0003CAr 3                               ; during debugging
0003CAr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<kernel_putc
0003CCr 3  85 rr                        sta output
0003CEr 3  A9 rr                        lda #>kernel_putc
0003D0r 3  85 rr                        sta output+1
0003D2r 3               
0003D2r 3                               ; Load all of the important zero page variables from ROM
0003D2r 3  A2 21                        ldx #cold_zp_table_end-cold_zp_table-1
0003D4r 3               
0003D4r 3               @load_zp_loop:
0003D4r 3                               ; This loop loads them back to front. We can use X here
0003D4r 3                               ; because Tali hasn't started using the stack yet.
0003D4r 3  BD rr rr                     lda cold_zp_table,x
0003D7r 3  95 rr                        sta cp,x
0003D9r 3  CA                           dex
0003DAr 3  D0 F8                        bne @load_zp_loop
0003DCr 3               
0003DCr 3                               ; Copy the 0th element.
0003DCr 3  AD rr rr                     lda cold_zp_table
0003DFr 3  85 rr                        sta cp
0003E1r 3                               ; Initialize 65c02 stack (Return Stack)
0003E1r 3  A2 rr                        ldx #rsp0
0003E3r 3  9A                           txs
0003E4r 3               
0003E4r 3                               ; Clear Data Stack. This is repeated in ABORT, but this way we
0003E4r 3                               ; can load high-level words with EVALUATE
0003E4r 3  A2 rr                        ldx #dsp0
0003E6r 3               
0003E6r 3               
0003E6r 3                               ; Initialize the user variables.
0003E6r 3  A0 31                        ldy #cold_user_table_end-cold_user_table-1
0003E8r 3  A9 00                        lda #0
0003EAr 3               
0003EAr 3               @load_user_vars_loop:
0003EAr 3                               ; Like the zero page variables, these are initialized
0003EAr 3                               ; back to front.
0003EAr 3  B9 rr rr                     lda cold_user_table,y
0003EDr 3  91 rr                        sta (up),y
0003EFr 3  88                           dey
0003F0r 3  D0 F8                        bne @load_user_vars_loop
0003F2r 3               
0003F2r 3                               ; Copy the 0th element.
0003F2r 3  AD rr rr                     lda cold_user_table
0003F5r 3  92 rr                        sta (up)
0003F7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
0003FAr 3               
0003FAr 3                               ; Define high-level words in forth_words.asm via EVALUATE. If
0003FAr 3                               ; you do not have any high-level words, this part can be
0003FAr 3                               ; commented out.
0003FAr 3  CA                           dex
0003FBr 3  CA                           dex
0003FCr 3  CA                           dex
0003FDr 3  CA                           dex
0003FEr 3               
0003FEr 3               
0003FEr 3                               ; start address goes NOS
0003FEr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<forth_words_start
000400r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
000402r 3  A9 rr                        lda #>forth_words_start
000404r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
000406r 3               
000406r 3                               ; length goes TOS
000406r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<forth_words_end
000408r 3  38                           sec
000409r 3  E9 rr                        sbc #<forth_words_start
00040Br 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
00040Dr 3               
00040Dr 3  A9 rr                        lda #>forth_words_end
00040Fr 3  E9 rr                        sbc #>forth_words_start
000411r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
000413r 3               
000413r 3               
000413r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_evaluate
000416r 3               
000416r 3                               ; Now define any user words via EVALUATE. If you do not have
000416r 3                               ; any user-defined words, this part can be commented out as
000416r 3                               ; well.
000416r 3  CA                           dex
000417r 3  CA                           dex
000418r 3  CA                           dex
000419r 3  CA                           dex
00041Ar 3               
00041Ar 3               
00041Ar 3                               ; start address goes NOS
00041Ar 3  A9 rr                        lda #<user_words_start
00041Cr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
00041Er 3  A9 rr                        lda #>user_words_start
000420r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
000422r 3               
000422r 3                               ; length goes TOS
000422r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<user_words_end
000424r 3  38                           sec
000425r 3  E9 rr                        sbc #<user_words_start
000427r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
000429r 3               
000429r 3  A9 rr                        lda #>user_words_end
00042Br 3  E9 rr                        sbc #>user_words_start
00042Dr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
00042Fr 3               
00042Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_evaluate
000432r 3               
000432r 3                               ; Initialize all of the history buffers by putting a zero in
000432r 3                               ; each length byte.
000432r 3  9C rr rr                     stz hist_buff
000435r 3  9C rr rr                     stz hist_buff+$80
000438r 3  9C rr rr                     stz hist_buff+$100
00043Br 3  9C rr rr                     stz hist_buff+$180
00043Er 3  9C rr rr                     stz hist_buff+$200
000441r 3  9C rr rr                     stz hist_buff+$280
000444r 3  9C rr rr                     stz hist_buff+$300
000447r 3  9C rr rr                     stz hist_buff+$380
00044Ar 3               
00044Ar 3               
00044Ar 3                               ; fall through to ABORT
00044Ar 3               
00044Ar 3               
00044Ar 3               ; ## ABORT ( -- ) "Reset the Data Stack and restart the CLI"
00044Ar 3               ; ## "abort"  tested  ANS core
00044Ar 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/ABORT
00044Ar 3                       ; Clear Data Stack and continue into QUIT. We can jump here via
00044Ar 3                       ; subroutine if we want to because we are going to reset the 65c02's
00044Ar 3                       ; stack pointer (the Return Stack) anyway during QUIT. Note we don't
00044Ar 3                       ; actually delete the stuff on the Data Stack.
00044Ar 3                       ; """
00044Ar 3               xt_abort:
00044Ar 3  A2 rr                        ldx #dsp0
00044Cr 3               
00044Cr 3                               ; fall through to QUIT
00044Cr 3               
00044Cr 3               
00044Cr 3               ; ## QUIT ( -- ) "Reset the input and get new input"
00044Cr 3               ; ## "quit"  tested  ANS core
00044Cr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/QUIT
00044Cr 3                       ; Rest the input and start command loop
00044Cr 3                       ; """
00044Cr 3               
00044Cr 3               xt_quit:
00044Cr 3                               ; Clear the Return Stack. This is a little screwed up
00044Cr 3                               ; because the 65c02 can only set the Return Stack via X,
00044Cr 3                               ; which is our Data Stack pointer. The ANS specification
00044Cr 3                               ; demands, however, that ABORT reset the Data Stack pointer
00044Cr 3  8A                           txa             ; Save the DSP that we just defined
00044Dr 3  A2 rr                        ldx #rsp0
00044Fr 3  9A                           txs
000450r 3  AA                           tax             ; Restore the DSP. Dude, seriously.
000451r 3               
000451r 3                               ; make sure instruction pointer is empty
000451r 3  64 rr                        stz ip
000453r 3  64 rr                        stz ip+1
000455r 3               
000455r 3                               ; SOURCE-ID is zero (keyboard input)
000455r 3  64 rr                        stz insrc
000457r 3  64 rr                        stz insrc+1
000459r 3               
000459r 3                               ; STATE is zero (interpret, not compile)
000459r 3  64 rr                        stz state
00045Br 3  64 rr                        stz state+1
00045Dr 3               @get_line:
00045Dr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<buffer0   ; input buffer, this is paranoid
00045Fr 3  85 rr                        sta cib
000461r 3  A9 rr                        lda #>buffer0
000463r 3  85 rr                        sta cib+1
000465r 3               
000465r 3                               ; Size of current input buffer (CIB) is zero
000465r 3  64 rr                        stz ciblen
000467r 3  64 rr                        stz ciblen+1
000469r 3               
000469r 3                               ; Accept a line from the current import source. This is how
000469r 3                               ; modern Forths to it.
000469r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_refill           ; ( -- f )
00046Cr 3               
00046Cr 3                               ; Test flag: LSB of TOS
00046Cr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
00046Er 3  D0 05                        bne @success
000470r 3               
000470r 3                               ; If REFILL returned a FALSE flag, something went wrong and we
000470r 3                               ; need to print an error message and reset the machine. We
000470r 3                               ; don't need to save TOS because we're going to clobber it
000470r 3                               ; anyway when we go back to ABORT.
000470r 3  A9 06                        lda #err_refill
000472r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp error
000475r 3               
000475r 3               @success:
000475r 3                               ; Assume we have successfully accepted a string of input from
000475r 3                               ; a source, with address cib and length of input in ciblen. We
000475r 3                               ; arrive here still with the TRUE flag from REFILL as TOS
000475r 3  E8                           inx                     ; drop
000476r 3  E8                           inx
000477r 3               
000477r 3                               ; Main compile/execute routine
000477r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr interpret
00047Ar 3               
00047Ar 3                               ; Test for Data Stack underflow. Tali Forth does not check for
00047Ar 3                               ; overflow because it is so rare
00047Ar 3  E0 rr                        cpx #dsp0
00047Cr 3  F0 05                        beq @stack_ok
00047Er 3  90 03                        bcc @stack_ok           ; DSP must always be smaller than DSP0
000480r 3               
000480r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp underflow_error
000483r 3               
000483r 3               @stack_ok:
000483r 3                               ; Display system prompt if all went well. If we're interpreting,
000483r 3                               ; this is " ok", if we're compiling, it's " compiled". Note
000483r 3                               ; space at beginning of the string.
000483r 3  A5 rr                        lda state
000485r 3  F0 02                        beq @print
000487r 3               
000487r 3  A9 01                        lda #1                  ; number for "compile" string
000489r 3               @print:
000489r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr print_string
00048Cr 3               
00048Cr 3                               ; Awesome line, everybody! Now get the next one.
00048Cr 3  80 CF                        bra @get_line
00048Er 3               
00048Er 3               z_cold:
00048Er 3               z_abort:
00048Er 3               z_quit:         ; no RTS required
00048Er 3               
00048Er 3               
00048Er 3               
00048Er 3               ; This table holds all of the initial values for the variables in zero page.
00048Er 3               ; This table is used by COLD.
00048Er 3               cold_zp_table:
00048Er 3  rr rr                .word cp0+256+1024      ; cp moved to make room for user vars and
000490r 3                                               ; block buffer
000490r 3  rr rr                .word dictionary_start  ; dp
000492r 3  00 00                .word 0                 ; workword
000494r 3  00 00                .word 0                 ; insrc (SOURCE-ID is 0 for keyboard)
000496r 3  rr rr                .word buffer0           ; cib
000498r 3  00 00                .word 0                 ; ciblen
00049Ar 3  00 00                .word 0                 ; toin
00049Cr 3  00 00                .word 0                 ; ip
00049Er 3  rr rr                .word kernel_putc       ; output
0004A0r 3  rr rr                .word kernel_getc       ; input
0004A2r 3  00 00                .word 0                 ; havekey
0004A4r 3  00 00                .word 0                 ; state (0 = interpret)
0004A6r 3  0A 00                .word 10                ; base
0004A8r 3  14 00                .word 20                ; nc-limit
0004AAr 3  00 00                .word 0                 ; uf_strip (off by default)
0004ACr 3  rr rr                .word cp0               ; up (user vars put right at beginning of
0004AEr 3                                               ; available RAM)
0004AEr 3  00 00                .word 0                 ; status
0004B0r 3               cold_zp_table_end:
0004B0r 3               
0004B0r 3               ; No further ZP variables are initialized. The variables past this point are
0004B0r 3               ; all temporaries.
0004B0r 3               
0004B0r 3               ; This table holds the inital values for the user variables. This table is
0004B0r 3               ; used by COLD.
0004B0r 3               cold_user_table:
0004B0r 3  00 00                .word 0                         ; BLK
0004B2r 3  00 00                .word 0                         ; SCR
0004B4r 3  00                   .byte 0                         ; CURRENT = FORTH-WORDLIST
0004B5r 3  04                   .byte 4                         ; #WORDLISTS (FORTH EDITOR ASSEMBLER ROOT)
0004B6r 3  rr rr                .word dictionary_start          ; FORTH-WORDLIST
0004B8r 3  rr rr                .word editor_dictionary_start   ; EDITOR-WORDLIST
0004BAr 3  rr rr                .word assembler_dictionary_start ; ASSEMBLER-WORDLIST
0004BCr 3  rr rr                .word root_dictionary_start     ; ROOT-WORDLIST
0004BEr 3  00 00 00 00          .word 0,0,0,0,0,0,0,0           ; User wordlists
0004C2r 3  00 00 00 00  
0004C6r 3  00 00 00 00  
0004CEr 3  01                   .byte 1                         ; #ORDER
0004CFr 3  00 00 00 00          .byte 0,0,0,0,0,0,0,0,0         ; search-order
0004D3r 3  00 00 00 00  
0004D7r 3  00           
0004D8r 3  rr rr                .word cp0+256                   ; Address of buffer (right after USER vars)
0004DAr 3  00 00                .word 0                         ; block in buffer
0004DCr 3  00 00                .word 0                         ; buffer status (not in use)
0004DEr 3  rr rr                .word xt_block_word_error       ; block-read vector
0004E0r 3  rr rr                .word xt_block_word_error       ; block-write vector
0004E2r 3               cold_user_table_end:
0004E2r 3               
0004E2r 3               
0004E2r 3               ; ## ABORT_QUOTE ( "string" -- ) "If flag TOS is true, ABORT with message"
0004E2r 3               ; ## "abort""  tested  ANS core
0004E2r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/ABORTq
0004E2r 3                       ; Abort and print a string.
0004E2r 3                       ; """
0004E2r 3               
0004E2r 3               xt_abort_quote:
0004E2r 3                               ; save the string
0004E2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_s_quote          ; S"
0004E5r 3               
0004E5r 3                               ; compile run-time part
0004E5r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>abort_quote_runtime
0004E7r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<abort_quote_runtime
0004E9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine     ; may not be JMP as JSR/RTS
0004ECr 3               
0004ECr 3  60           z_abort_quote:  rts
0004EDr 3               
0004EDr 3               
0004EDr 3               abort_quote_runtime:
0004EDr 3                       ; """Runtime aspect of ABORT_QUOTE"""
0004EDr 3               
0004EDr 3                               ; We arrive here with ( f addr u )
0004EDr 3  B5 04                        lda 4,x
0004EFr 3  15 05                        ora 5,x
0004F1r 3  F0 09                        beq @done       ; if FALSE, we're done
0004F3r 3               
0004F3r 3                               ; We're true, so print string and ABORT. We follow Gforth
0004F3r 3                               ; in going to a new line after the string
0004F3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
0004F6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
0004F9r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp xt_abort    ; not JSR, so never come back
0004FCr 3               @done:
0004FCr 3                               ; Drop three entries from the Data Stack
0004FCr 3  8A                           txa
0004FDr 3  18                           clc
0004FEr 3  69 06                        adc #6
000500r 3  AA                           tax
000501r 3               
000501r 3  60                           rts
000502r 3               
000502r 3               
000502r 3               
000502r 3               ; ## ABS ( n -- u ) "Return absolute value of a number"
000502r 3               ; ## "abs"  auto  ANS core
000502r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/ABS
000502r 3                       ; Return the absolute value of a number.
000502r 3                       ; """
000502r 3               
000502r 3               xt_abs:
000502r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
000505r 3               
000505r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
000507r 3  10 0D                        bpl @done       ; positive number, easy money!
000509r 3               
000509r 3                               ; negative: calculate 0 - n
000509r 3  38                           sec
00050Ar 3  A9 00                        lda #0
00050Cr 3  F5 00                        sbc 0,x         ; LSB
00050Er 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
000510r 3               
000510r 3  A9 00                        lda #0          ; MSB
000512r 3  F5 01                        sbc 1,x
000514r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
000516r 3               
000516r 3               @done:
000516r 3  60           z_abs:          rts
000517r 3               
000517r 3               
000517r 3               
000517r 3               ; ## ACCEPT ( addr n -- n ) "Receive a string of characters from the keyboard"
000517r 3               ; ## "accept"  auto  ANS core
000517r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/ACCEPT
000517r 3                       ; Receive a string of at most n1 characters, placing them at
000517r 3                       ; addr. Return the actual number of characters as n2. Characters
000517r 3                       ; are echoed as they are received. ACCEPT is called by REFILL in
000517r 3                       ; modern Forths.
000517r 3                       ; """
000517r 3               
000517r 3               xt_accept:
000517r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
00051Ar 3               
00051Ar 3                               ; Abort if we were asked to receive 0 chars
00051Ar 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
00051Cr 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
00051Er 3  D0 09                        bne @not_zero
000520r 3               
000520r 3  E8                           inx
000521r 3  E8                           inx
000522r 3  74 00                        stz 0,x
000524r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
000526r 3               
000526r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp accept_done
000529r 3               
000529r 3               @not_zero:
000529r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; number of chars to get in tmp2 ...
00052Br 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2
00052Dr 3  64 rr                        stz tmp2+1      ; ... but we only accept max 255 chars
00052Fr 3               
00052Fr 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; address of buffer is NOS, to tmp1
000531r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
000533r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
000535r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
000537r 3               
000537r 3  E8                           inx
000538r 3  E8                           inx
000539r 3               
000539r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
00053Br 3               
00053Br 3                               ; Select the next history buffer. Clear bit 3 first (so overflow
00053Br 3                               ; from bit 2 to 3 is OK)
00053Br 3  A5 rr                        lda status
00053Dr 3  29 F7                        and #$f7
00053Fr 3               
00053Fr 3                               ; Increment the buffer number (overflow from 7 to 0 OK)
00053Fr 3  1A                           inc
000540r 3               
000540r 3                               ; Set bit 3 for detecting if CTRL-n has been pressed the first
000540r 3                               ; time. This bit will be cleared on the first CTRL-n or CTRL-p
000540r 3                               ; received and won't be used to calculate the history buffer
000540r 3                               ; offset.
000540r 3  09 08                        ora #$08
000542r 3  85 rr                        sta status
000544r 3               
000544r 3               accept_loop:
000544r 3                               ; Out of the box, py65mon catches some CTRL sequences such as
000544r 3                               ; CTRL-c. We also don't need to check for CTRL-l because a
000544r 3                               ; vt100 terminal clears the screen automatically.
000544r 3               
000544r 3                               ; This is the internal version of KEY without all the mucking
000544r 3                               ; about with the Data Stack while still using the input vector
000544r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr key_a
000547r 3               
000547r 3                               ; We quit on both line feed and carriage return
000547r 3  C9 0A                        cmp #AscLF
000549r 3  F0 20                        beq @eol
00054Br 3  C9 0D                        cmp #AscCR
00054Dr 3  F0 1C                        beq @eol
00054Fr 3               
00054Fr 3                               ; BACKSPACE and DEL do the same thing for the moment
00054Fr 3  C9 08                        cmp #AscBS
000551r 3  F0 22                        beq @backspace
000553r 3  C9 7F                        cmp #AscDEL     ; (CTRL-h)
000555r 3  F0 1E                        beq @backspace
000557r 3               
000557r 3                               ; Check for CTRL-p and CTRL-n to recall input history
000557r 3  C9 10                        cmp #AscCP
000559r 3  F0 36                        beq @ctrl_p
00055Br 3  C9 0E                        cmp #AscCN
00055Dr 3  F0 44                        beq @ctrl_n
00055Fr 3               
00055Fr 3                               ; That's enough for now. Save and echo character.
00055Fr 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000561r 3  C8                           iny
000562r 3               
000562r 3                               ; EMIT_A sidesteps all the fooling around with the Data Stack
000562r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
000565r 3               
000565r 3  C4 rr                        cpy tmp2        ; reached character limit?
000567r 3  D0 DB                        bne accept_loop       ; fall through if buffer limit reached
000569r 3  80 03                        bra @buffer_full
00056Br 3               
00056Br 3               @eol:
00056Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space    ; print final space
00056Er 3               
00056Er 3               @buffer_full:
00056Er 3                               ; REFILL updates ciblen and toin, we don't need to do it here
00056Er 3  94 00                        sty 0,x         ; Y contains number of chars accepted already
000570r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x         ; we only accept 256 chars
000572r 3               
000572r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp accept_done
000575r 3               
000575r 3               @backspace:
000575r 3                               ; Handle backspace and delete kex, which currently do the same
000575r 3                               ; thing
000575r 3  C0 00                        cpy #0          ; buffer empty?
000577r 3  D0 06                        bne @1
000579r 3               
000579r 3  A9 07                        lda #AscBELL    ; complain and don't delete beyond the start of line
00057Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
00057Er 3  C8                           iny
00057Fr 3               @1:
00057Fr 3  88                           dey
000580r 3  A9 08                        lda #AscBS      ; move back one
000582r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
000585r 3  A9 20                        lda #AscSP      ; print a space (rubout)
000587r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
00058Ar 3  A9 08                        lda #AscBS      ; move back over space
00058Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
00058Fr 3               
00058Fr 3  80 B3                        bra accept_loop
000591r 3               
000591r 3               @ctrl_p:
000591r 3                               ; CTRL-p was pressed. Recall the previous input buffer.
000591r 3               
000591r 3                               ; Select the previous buffer
000591r 3  A5 rr                        lda status
000593r 3               
000593r 3                               ; Check for 0 (need to wrap back to 7)
000593r 3  29 07                        and #7
000595r 3  D0 08                        bne @ctrl_p_dec
000597r 3               
000597r 3                               ; We need to wrap back to 7.
000597r 3  A5 rr                        lda status
000599r 3  09 07                        ora #7
00059Br 3  85 rr                        sta status
00059Dr 3  80 11                        bra @recall_history
00059Fr 3               
00059Fr 3               @ctrl_p_dec:
00059Fr 3                               ; It's safe to decrement the buffer index directly.
00059Fr 3  C6 rr                        dec status
0005A1r 3  80 0D                        bra @recall_history
0005A3r 3               
0005A3r 3               @ctrl_n:
0005A3r 3                               ; CTRL-n was pressed. Recall the next input buffer. Select
0005A3r 3                               ; the next buffer Check bit 3. If it's set, this is the first
0005A3r 3                               ; time CTRL-n has been pressed and we should select the CURRENT
0005A3r 3                               ; history buffer.
0005A3r 3  A9 08                        lda #$8
0005A5r 3  24 rr                        bit status
0005A7r 3  D0 07                        bne @recall_history
0005A9r 3               
0005A9r 3                               ; This isn't the first time CTRL-n has been pressed, select the
0005A9r 3                               ; next history buffer. Clear bit 3 first (so overflow is OK)
0005A9r 3  A5 rr                        lda status
0005ABr 3  29 F7                        and #$f7
0005ADr 3               
0005ADr 3                               ; Increment the buffer number (overflow from 7 to 0 OK)
0005ADr 3  1A                           inc
0005AEr 3               
0005AEr 3                               ; Bit 3 (if it got set by going from buffer 7 to 0) will
0005AEr 3                               ; be cleared below.
0005AEr 3  85 rr                        sta status
0005B0r 3               
0005B0r 3                               ; Falls through to @recall_history
0005B0r 3               
0005B0r 3               @recall_history:
0005B0r 3                               ; Clear bit 3 (first time ctrl-n recall) bit in status
0005B0r 3  A9 08                        lda #%00001000
0005B2r 3  14 rr                        trb status
0005B4r 3               
0005B4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr total_recall
0005B7r 3               
0005B7r 3                               ; tmp3 now has the address of the previous history buffer.
0005B7r 3                               ; First byte of buffer is length. Clear the line by sending
0005B7r 3                               ; CR, Y spaces, then CR.
0005B7r 3  A9 0D                        lda #AscCR
0005B9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
0005BCr 3               
0005BCr 3               input_clear:
0005BCr 3  C0 00                        cpy #0
0005BEr 3  F0 08                        beq input_cleared
0005C0r 3               
0005C0r 3  A9 20                        lda #AscSP
0005C2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
0005C5r 3  88                           dey
0005C6r 3  80 F4                        bra input_clear
0005C8r 3               
0005C8r 3               input_cleared:
0005C8r 3  A9 0D                        lda #AscCR
0005CAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
0005CDr 3               
0005CDr 3                               ; Save the history length byte into histinfo+1
0005CDr 3                               ; ldy #0        ; Y is already 0 by clearing the line.
0005CDr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp3),y
0005CFr 3  85 rr                        sta status+1
0005D1r 3               
0005D1r 3                               ; Increment the tmp3 pointer so we can use ,y addressing
0005D1r 3                               ; on both tmp1 (the input buffer) and tmp3 (the history
0005D1r 3                               ; buffer)
0005D1r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp3
0005D3r 3  D0 02                        bne @2           ; Increment the upper byte on carry.
0005D5r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp3+1
0005D7r 3               @2:
0005D7r 3                               ; Copy the history buffer into the input buffer,
0005D7r 3                               ; sending the characters to the output as we go.
0005D7r 3  A9 0D                        lda #AscCR
0005D9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
0005DCr 3               
0005DCr 3               @history_loop:
0005DCr 3                               ; See if we have reached the end of the history buffer.
0005DCr 3  C4 rr                        cpy status+1
0005DEr 3  D0 03                        bne @3
0005E0r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp accept_loop       ; Needs a long jump
0005E3r 3               @3:
0005E3r 3                               ; See if we have reached the end of the input buffer.
0005E3r 3                               ; (only comparing to lower byte as we currently limit
0005E3r 3                               ; to 255 characters max)
0005E3r 3  C4 rr                        cpy tmp2
0005E5r 3  F0 0A                        beq @hist_filled_buffer
0005E7r 3               
0005E7r 3                               ; Copy a character and echo.
0005E7r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp3),y
0005E9r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
0005EBr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
0005EEr 3               
0005EEr 3                               ; Move to the next character.
0005EEr 3  C8                           iny
0005EFr 3  80 EB                        bra @history_loop
0005F1r 3               
0005F1r 3               @hist_filled_buffer:
0005F1r 3                               ; We don't want a history recall to EOL our buffer,
0005F1r 3                               ; so back up one character and return to editing.
0005F1r 3  88                           dey
0005F2r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp accept_loop
0005F5r 3               accept_done:
0005F5r 3               @done:
0005F5r 3                               ; Copy the input buffer into the currently
0005F5r 3                               ; selected history buffer.
0005F5r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr total_recall
0005F8r 3  85 rr                        sta status+1
0005FAr 3               
0005FAr 3                               ; Also save it in the first buffer byte.
0005FAr 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
0005FCr 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp3),y
0005FEr 3               
0005FEr 3                               ; Move path the count to the data bytes
0005FEr 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp3
000600r 3  D0 02                        bne @4           ; Increment the upper byte on carry.
000602r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp3+1
000604r 3               @4:
