000BCDr 3  29 02                        and #AN                 ; mask all but Always Native (AN) bit
000BCFr 3  F0 0D                        beq @compile_check
000BD1r 3               
000BD1r 3                               ; We're natively compiling no matter what. Get length and
000BD1r 3                               ; compile in code. Get the original nt back
000BD1r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmptos
000BD3r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
000BD5r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmptos+1
000BD7r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
000BD9r 3               
000BD9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_wordsize         ; ( nt -- u )
000BDCr 3               
000BDCr 3  80 27                        bra @compile_as_code
000BDEr 3               
000BDEr 3               @compile_check:
000BDEr 3                               ; See if Native Compile is even alowed by checking the NN
000BDEr 3                               ; flag
000BDEr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp3
000BE0r 3  29 08                        and #NN
000BE2r 3  F0 03                        beq @check_size_limit
000BE4r 3               
000BE4r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp @compile_as_jump    ; too far for BRA
000BE7r 3               
000BE7r 3               @check_size_limit:
000BE7r 3                               ; Native compile is a legal option, but we need to see what
000BE7r 3                               ; limit the user set for size (in nc_limit)
000BE7r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmptos
000BE9r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
000BEBr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmptos+1
000BEDr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
000BEFr 3               
000BEFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_wordsize         ; ( nt -- u )
000BF2r 3               
000BF2r 3                               ; Check the wordsize MSB against the user-defined limit.
000BF2r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
000BF4r 3  C5 rr                        cmp nc_limit+1
000BF6r 3  90 0D                        bcc @compile_as_code    ; user-defined limit MSB
000BF8r 3  D0 08                        bne @jumpto_compile_as_jump
000BFAr 3               
000BFAr 3                               ; Check the wordsize LSB against the user-defined limit.
000BFAr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
000BFCr 3  C5 rr                        cmp nc_limit            ; user-defined limit LSB
000BFEr 3  90 05                        bcc @compile_as_code    ; Allow native compiling for less
000C00r 3  F0 03                        beq @compile_as_code    ; than or equal to the limit.
000C02r 3               
000C02r 3               @jumpto_compile_as_jump:
000C02r 3                               ; If the wordsize is greater than the user-defined
000C02r 3                               ; limit, it will be compiled as a subroutine jump.
000C02r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp @compile_as_jump    ; too far for BRA
000C05r 3               
000C05r 3               @compile_as_code:
000C05r 3                               ; We arrive here with the length of the word's code TOS and
000C05r 3                               ; xt on top of the Return Stack. MOVE will need ( xt cp u )
000C05r 3                               ; on the data stack
000C05r 3  CA                           dex
000C06r 3  CA                           dex                     ; ( -- u ? )
000C07r 3  CA                           dex
000C08r 3  CA                           dex                     ; ( -- u ? ? )
000C09r 3               
000C09r 3  B5 04                        lda 4,x
000C0Br 3  95 00                        sta 0,x                 ; LSB of u
000C0Dr 3  B5 05                        lda 5,x
000C0Fr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x                 ; ( -- u ? u )
000C11r 3               
000C11r 3  68                           pla
000C12r 3  95 04                        sta 4,x                 ; LSB of xt
000C14r 3  68                           pla
000C15r 3  95 05                        sta 5,x                 ; ( -- xt ? u )
000C17r 3               
000C17r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp                  ; LSB of cp
000C19r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
000C1Br 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
000C1Dr 3  95 03                        sta 3,x                 ; ( -- xt cp u )
000C1Fr 3               
000C1Fr 3                               ; --- SPECIAL CASE 1: PREVENT RETURN STACK THRASHINIG ---
000C1Fr 3               
000C1Fr 3                               ; Native compiling allows us to strip the stack antics off
000C1Fr 3                               ; a number of words that use the Return Stack such as >R, R>,
000C1Fr 3                               ; 2>R and 2R> (but not 2R@ in this version). We compare the
000C1Fr 3                               ; xt with the contents of the table
000C1Fr 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
000C21r 3               
000C21r 3               @strip_loop:
000C21r 3  B9 rr rr                     lda @strip_table,y      ; LSB of first word
000C24r 3  D5 04                        cmp 4,x                 ; LSB of xt
000C26r 3  D0 07                        bne @next_entry
000C28r 3               
000C28r 3                               ; LSB is the same, test MSB
000C28r 3  B9 rr rr                     lda @strip_table+1,y
000C2Br 3  D5 05                        cmp 5,x
000C2Dr 3  F0 0C                        beq @found_entry
000C2Fr 3               
000C2Fr 3                               ; MSB is not equal. Pretend though that we've come from LSB
000C2Fr 3                               ; so we can use the next step for both cases
000C2Fr 3               @next_entry:
000C2Fr 3                               ; Not a word that needs stripping, so check next entry in table
000C2Fr 3                               ; Let's see if we're done with the table (marked by zero entry)
000C2Fr 3  B9 rr rr                     lda @strip_table,y      ; pointing to LSB
000C32r 3  19 rr rr                     ora @strip_table+1,y    ; get MSB
000C35r 3  F0 22                        beq @underflow_strip    ; table done, let's get out of here
000C37r 3               
000C37r 3  C8                           iny
000C38r 3  C8                           iny
000C39r 3  80 E6                        bra @strip_loop
000C3Br 3               @found_entry:
000C3Br 3                               ; This word is one of the ones that needs to have its size
000C3Br 3                               ; adjusted during native compile. We find the values in the
000C3Br 3                               ; next table with the same index, which is Y. However, Y is
000C3Br 3                               ; pointing to the MSB, so we need to go back to the LSB and
000C3Br 3                               ; halve the index before we can use it.
000C3Br 3  98                           tya
000C3Cr 3  4A                           lsr
000C3Dr 3  A8                           tay
000C3Er 3               
000C3Er 3                               ; Get the adjustment out of the size table. We were clever
000C3Er 3                               ; enough to make sure the cut on both ends of the code is
000C3Er 3                               ; is the same size.
000C3Er 3  B9 rr rr                     lda @strip_size,y
000C41r 3  85 rr                        sta tmptos              ; save a copy
000C43r 3               
000C43r 3                               ; Adjust xt: Start later
000C43r 3  18                           clc
000C44r 3  75 04                        adc 4,x
000C46r 3  95 04                        sta 4,x
000C48r 3  90 02                        bcc @2
000C4Ar 3  F6 05                        inc 5,x                 ; we just care about the carry
000C4Cr 3               @2:
000C4Cr 3               
000C4Cr 3                               ; Adjust u: Quit earlier. Since we cut off the top and the
000C4Cr 3                               ; bottom of the code, we have to double the value
000C4Cr 3  06 rr                        asl tmptos
000C4Er 3               
000C4Er 3  38                           sec
000C4Fr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
000C51r 3  E5 rr                        sbc tmptos
000C53r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
000C55r 3  B0 02                        bcs @3
000C57r 3  D6 01                        dec 1,x                 ; we just care about the borrow
000C59r 3               @3:
000C59r 3                               ; drop through to underflow check stripping
000C59r 3               
000C59r 3               @underflow_strip:
000C59r 3                               ; --- SPECIAL CASE 2: REMOVE UNDERFLOW CHECKING ---
000C59r 3               
000C59r 3                               ; The user can choose to remove the unterflow testing in those
000C59r 3                               ; words that have the UF flag. This shortens the word by
000C59r 3                               ; 3 bytes if there is no underflow.
000C59r 3               
000C59r 3                               ; See if the user wants underflow stripping turned on
000C59r 3  A5 rr                        lda uf_strip
000C5Br 3  05 rr                        ora uf_strip+1
000C5Dr 3  F0 1C                        beq @specials_done
000C5Fr 3               
000C5Fr 3                               ; See if this word even contains underflow checking
000C5Fr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp3
000C61r 3  29 10                        and #UF
000C63r 3  F0 16                        beq @specials_done
000C65r 3               
000C65r 3                               ; If we arrived here, underflow has to go. It's always 3 bytes
000C65r 3                               ; long. Note hat PICK is a special case.
000C65r 3               
000C65r 3                               ; Adjust xt: Start later
000C65r 3  18                           clc
000C66r 3  B5 04                        lda 4,x
000C68r 3  69 03                        adc #3
000C6Ar 3  95 04                        sta 4,x
000C6Cr 3  90 02                        bcc @4
000C6Er 3  F6 05                        inc 5,x                  ; we just care about the carry
000C70r 3               @4:
000C70r 3                               ; Adjust u: End earlier
000C70r 3  38                           sec
000C71r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
000C73r 3  E9 03                        sbc #3
000C75r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
000C77r 3  B0 02                        bcs @5
000C79r 3  D6 01                        dec 1,x                  ; we just care about the borrow
000C7Br 3               @5:
000C7Br 3               
000C7Br 3                               ; --- END OF SPECIAL CASES ---
000C7Br 3               @specials_done:
000C7Br 3                               ; Store size of area to be copied for calculation of
000C7Br 3                               ; new CP. We have to do this after all of the special cases
000C7Br 3                               ; because they might change the size
000C7Br 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x                 ; MSB
000C7Dr 3  48                           pha
000C7Er 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x                 ; LSB
000C80r 3  48                           pha
000C81r 3               
000C81r 3                               ; Enough of this, let's move those bytes already! We have
000C81r 3                               ; ( xt cp u ) on the stack at this point
000C81r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_move
000C84r 3               
000C84r 3                               ; Update CP
000C84r 3  18                           clc
000C85r 3  68                           pla                     ; LSB
000C86r 3  65 rr                        adc cp
000C88r 3  85 rr                        sta cp
000C8Ar 3               
000C8Ar 3  68                           pla                     ; MSB
000C8Br 3  65 rr                        adc cp+1
000C8Dr 3  85 rr                        sta cp+1
000C8Fr 3               
000C8Fr 3  80 2C                        bra @done
000C91r 3               
000C91r 3               @strip_table:
000C91r 3                              ; List of words we strip the Return Stack antics from
000C91r 3                              ; during native compile, zero terminated. The index here
000C91r 3                              ; must be the same as for the sizes
000C91r 3  rr rr rr rr                  .word xt_r_from, xt_r_fetch, xt_to_r    ; R>, R@, >R
000C95r 3  rr rr        
000C97r 3  rr rr rr rr                  .word xt_two_to_r, xt_two_r_from, 0000  ; 2>R, 2R>, EOL
000C9Br 3  00 00        
000C9Dr 3               
000C9Dr 3               @strip_size:
000C9Dr 3                               ; List of bytes to be stripped from the words that get their
000C9Dr 3                               ; Return Stack antics removed during native compile. Index must
000C9Dr 3                               ; be the same as for the xts. Zero terminated.
000C9Dr 3  04 04 04 06                  .byte 4, 4, 4, 6, 6, 0          ; R>, R@, >R, 2>R, 2R>, EOL
000CA1r 3  06 00        
000CA3r 3               
000CA3r 3               @compile_as_jump:
000CA3r 3                               ; Compile xt as a subroutine jump
000CA3r 3  A9 20                        lda #$20
000CA5r 3  92 rr                        sta (cp)
000CA7r 3               
000CA7r 3  A0 01                        ldy #1
000CA9r 3  68                           pla             ; LSB
000CAAr 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
000CACr 3  C8                           iny
000CADr 3  68                           pla             ; MSB
000CAEr 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
000CB0r 3               
000CB0r 3                               ; allot space we just used
000CB0r 3  A9 03                        lda #3
000CB2r 3  18                           clc
000CB3r 3  65 rr                        adc cp
000CB5r 3  85 rr                        sta cp
000CB7r 3  90 02                        bcc @6
000CB9r 3  E6 rr                        inc cp+1
000CBBr 3               @6:
000CBBr 3  E8                           inx             ; drop xt
000CBCr 3  E8                           inx
000CBDr 3               @done:
000CBDr 3               z_compile_comma:
000CBDr 3  60                           rts
000CBEr 3               
000CBEr 3               
000CBEr 3               
000CBEr 3               ; ## COMPILE_ONLY ( -- ) "Mark most recent word as COMPILE-ONLY"
000CBEr 3               ; ## "compile-only"  tested  Tali Forth
000CBEr 3                       ; """Set the Compile Only flag (CO) of the most recently defined
000CBEr 3                       ; word.
000CBEr 3                       ;
000CBEr 3                       ; The alternative way to do this is to define a word
000CBEr 3                       ; ?COMPILE that makes sure  we're in compile mode
000CBEr 3                       ; """
000CBEr 3               
000CBEr 3               xt_compile_only:
000CBEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr current_to_dp
000CC1r 3  A0 01                        ldy #1          ; offset for status byte
000CC3r 3  B1 rr                        lda (dp),y
000CC5r 3  09 01                        ora #CO        ; make sure bit 7 is set
000CC7r 3  91 rr                        sta (dp),y
000CC9r 3               
000CC9r 3  60           z_compile_only: rts
000CCAr 3               
000CCAr 3               
000CCAr 3               
000CCAr 3               ; ## CONSTANT ( n "name" -- ) "Define a constant"
000CCAr 3               ; ## "constant"  auto  ANS core
000CCAr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/CONSTANT
000CCAr 3                       ;
000CCAr 3                       ; Forth equivalent is  CREATE , DOES> @  but we do
000CCAr 3                       ; more in assembler and let CREATE do the heavy lifting.
000CCAr 3                       ; See http://www.bradrodriguez.com/papers/moving3.htm for
000CCAr 3                       ; a primer on how this works in various Forths. This is the
000CCAr 3                       ; same code as VALUE in our case.
000CCAr 3                       ; """
000CCAr 3               xt_value:
000CCAr 3               xt_constant:
000CCAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
000CCDr 3               
000CCDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_create
000CD0r 3               
000CD0r 3                           	; CREATE by default installs a subroutine jump to DOVAR,
000CD0r 3                               ; but we want DOCONST for constants. Go back two bytes and
000CD0r 3                               ; replace the subroutine jump target
000CD0r 3  38                           sec
000CD1r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
000CD3r 3  E9 02                        sbc #2
000CD5r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
000CD7r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
000CD9r 3  E9 00                        sbc #0
000CDBr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
000CDDr 3               
000CDDr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<doconst           ; LSB of DOCONST
000CDFr 3  92 rr                        sta (tmp1)
000CE1r 3  A0 01                        ldy #1
000CE3r 3  A9 rr                        lda #>doconst           ; MSB of DOCONST
000CE5r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000CE7r 3               
000CE7r 3                               ; Now we save the constant number itself in the next cell
000CE7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_comma            ; drop through to adjust_z
000CEAr 3               
000CEAr 3               adjust_z:
000CEAr 3                               ; Now the length of the complete word (z_word) has increased by
000CEAr 3                               ; two. We need to update that number or else words such as SEE
000CEAr 3                               ; will ignore the PFA. We use this same routine for VARIABLE,
000CEAr 3                               ; VALUE and DEFER
000CEAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_latestnt         ; gives us ( -- nt )
000CEDr 3               
000CEDr 3                               ; z_word is six bytes further down
000CEDr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
000CEFr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
000CF1r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
000CF3r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
000CF5r 3               
000CF5r 3  A0 06                        ldy #6
000CF7r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
000CF9r 3  18                           clc
000CFAr 3  69 02                        adc #2
000CFCr 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000CFEr 3  C8                           iny
000CFFr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
000D01r 3  69 00                        adc #0                  ; only need carry
000D03r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000D05r 3               
000D05r 3  E8                           inx
000D06r 3  E8                           inx
000D07r 3               
000D07r 3               z_value:
000D07r 3  60           z_constant:     rts
000D08r 3               
000D08r 3               
000D08r 3               ; ## COUNT ( c-addr -- addr u ) "Convert character string to normal format"
000D08r 3               ; ## "count"  auto  ANS core
000D08r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/COUNT
000D08r 3                       ; Convert old-style character string to address-length pair. Note
000D08r 3                       ; that the length of the string c-addr is stored in character length
000D08r 3                       ; (8 bit), not cell length (16 bit). This is rarely used these days,
000D08r 3                       ; though COUNT can also be used to step through a string character by
000D08r 3                       ; character.
000D08r 3                       ; """
000D08r 3               xt_count:
000D08r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
000D0Br 3               
000D0Br 3  A1 00                        lda (0,x)       ; Get number of characters (255 max)
000D0Dr 3  A8                           tay
000D0Er 3               
000D0Er 3                               ; move start address up by one
000D0Er 3  F6 00                        inc 0,x         ; LSB
000D10r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
000D12r 3  F6 01                        inc 1,x         ; MSB
000D14r 3               
000D14r 3                               ; save number of characters to stack
000D14r 3               @1:
000D14r 3  98                           tya
000D15r 3  CA                           dex
000D16r 3  CA                           dex
000D17r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x         ; LSB
000D19r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x         ; MSB, always zero
000D1Br 3               
000D1Br 3  60           z_count:        rts
000D1Cr 3               
000D1Cr 3               
000D1Cr 3               ; ## CR ( -- ) "Print a line feed"
000D1Cr 3               ; ## "cr"  auto  ANS core
000D1Cr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/CR"""
000D1Cr 3               xt_cr:
000D1Cr 3  A9 0A                        lda #AscLF
000D1Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
000D21r 3  60           z_cr:           rts
000D22r 3               
000D22r 3               
000D22r 3               ; ## CREATE ( "name" -- ) "Create Dictionary entry for 'name'"
000D22r 3               ; ## "create"  auto  ANS core
000D22r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/CREATE
000D22r 3                       ;
000D22r 3                       ; See the drawing in headers.asm for details on the header
000D22r 3                       ; """
000D22r 3               
000D22r 3               xt_create:
000D22r 3                               ; get string
000D22r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_parse_name       ; ( addr u )
000D25r 3               
000D25r 3                               ; if we were given an empty string, we complain and quit
000D25r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
000D27r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
000D29r 3  D0 05                        bne @got_name
000D2Br 3               
000D2Br 3  A9 05                        lda #err_noname
000D2Dr 3  4C rr rr                     jmp error
000D30r 3               
000D30r 3               @got_name:
000D30r 3                               ; Enforce maximal length of string by overwriting the MSB of
000D30r 3                               ; the length. There is a possible error here: If the string
000D30r 3                               ; is exactly 255 chars long, then a lot of the following
000D30r 3                               ; additions will fail because of wrapping
000D30r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
000D32r 3               
000D32r 3                               ; Check to see if this name already exists.
000D32r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_two_dup          ; ( addr u addr u )
000D35r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_find_name        ; ( addr u flag ) (non-zero nt as flag)
000D38r 3               
000D38r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
000D3Ar 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
000D3Cr 3  F0 1E                        beq @new_name           ; We haven't seen this one before.
000D3Er 3               
000D3Er 3                               ; This name already exists.  See if we are supposed to print
000D3Er 3                               ; the message for it.
000D3Er 3  E8                           inx                     ; Drop flag (nt) from find-name.
000D3Fr 3  E8                           inx
000D40r 3               
000D40r 3                               ; Check bit 7
000D40r 3  24 rr                        bit status
000D42r 3  10 08                        bpl @redefined_name     ; Bit 7 is zero, so print the message.
000D44r 3               
000D44r 3                               ; We aren't supposed to print the redefined message ourselves,
000D44r 3                               ; but we should indicate that it is redefined (for ; to print
000D44r 3                               ; later).
000D44r 3  A9 80                        lda #$80                ; Set bit 7 to indicate dup
000D46r 3  05 rr                        ora status
000D48r 3  85 rr                        sta status
000D4Ar 3  80 18                        bra @process_name
000D4Cr 3               
000D4Cr 3               @redefined_name:
000D4Cr 3                               ; Print the message that the name is redefined.
000D4Cr 3  A9 02                        lda #str_redefined
000D4Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr print_string_no_lf
000D51r 3               
000D51r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_two_dup           ; ( addr u addr u )
000D54r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
000D57r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
000D5Ar 3               
000D5Ar 3  80 08                        bra @process_name
000D5Cr 3               
000D5Cr 3               @new_name:
000D5Cr 3  E8                           inx                     ; Drop flag (0) from find-name.
000D5Dr 3  E8                           inx
000D5Er 3  A9 7F                        lda #$7F                ; Clear bit 0 of status to indicate new word.
000D60r 3  25 rr                        and status
000D62r 3  85 rr                        sta status
000D64r 3               
000D64r 3               @process_name:
000D64r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
000D66r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2                ; store length of string in tmp2
000D68r 3               
000D68r 3                               ; remember the first free byte of memory as the start of
000D68r 3                               ; the new word
000D68r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
000D6Ar 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
000D6Cr 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
000D6Er 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
000D70r 3               
000D70r 3                               ; We need 8 bytes plus the length of the string for our new header.
000D70r 3                               ; This is also the offset for the start of the code field (the
000D70r 3                               ; xt_ label) so we need to remember it. Otherwise, we could
000D70r 3                               ; just allot the space afterwards
000D70r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
000D72r 3  18                           clc
000D73r 3  69 08                        adc #8
000D75r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3                ; total header length
000D77r 3               
000D77r 3                               ; We need three more bytes for for the hardcoded code field
000D77r 3                               ; area (CFA), the "payload" of the word which by default will
000D77r 3                               ; be a subroutine jump to DOVAR
000D77r 3  18                           clc
000D78r 3  69 03                        adc #3
000D7Ar 3               
000D7Ar 3                               ; We overwrite the length of the string returned by PARSE-NAME
000D7Ar 3                               ; and then call ALLOT
000D7Ar 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
000D7Cr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x         ; max header size is 255 chars
000D7Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_allot    ; ( addr )
000D81r 3               
000D81r 3                               ; Get the CURRENT dictionary pointer.
000D81r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr current_to_dp
000D84r 3               
000D84r 3                               ; Now we walk through the header with Y as the index, adding
000D84r 3                               ; information byte-by-byte
000D84r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
000D86r 3               
000D86r 3                               ; HEADER BYTE 0: Length of string
000D86r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
000D88r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000D8Ar 3               
000D8Ar 3                               ; HEADER BYTE 1: Status byte. By default, we set all new words
000D8Ar 3                               ; to "never native", user will have to decide if they should
000D8Ar 3                               ; be inlined
000D8Ar 3  A9 08                        lda #NN
000D8Cr 3               
000D8Cr 3                               ; Also, words defined by CREATE are marked in the header has
000D8Cr 3                               ; having a Code Field Area (CFA), which is a bit tricky for
000D8Cr 3                               ; Subroutine Threaded Code (STC). We do this so >BODY works
000D8Cr 3                               ; correctly with DOES> and CREATE. See the discussion at
000D8Cr 3                               ; http://forum.6502.org/viewtopic.php?f=9&t=5182 for details
000D8Cr 3  09 20                        ora #HC
000D8Er 3  C8                           iny
000D8Fr 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000D91r 3  C8                           iny
000D92r 3               
000D92r 3                               ; HEADER BYTE 2,3: Next header. This is the current last word
000D92r 3                               ; in the Dictionary
000D92r 3  A5 rr                        lda dp
000D94r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000D96r 3  C8                           iny
000D97r 3  A5 rr                        lda dp+1
000D99r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000D9Br 3  C8                           iny
000D9Cr 3               
000D9Cr 3                               ; Interlude: Make old CP new DP (new start of Dictionary)
000D9Cr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
000D9Er 3  85 rr                        sta dp+1
000DA0r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
000DA2r 3  85 rr                        sta dp
000DA4r 3               
000DA4r 3                               ; HEADER BYTE 4,5: Start of the code field ("xt_" of this word).
000DA4r 3                               ; This begins after the header so we take the length of the
000DA4r 3                               ; header, which we cleverly saved in tmp3, and use it as an
000DA4r 3                               ; offset to the address of the start of the word. We come here
000DA4r 3                               ; with tmp1 in A
000DA4r 3  18                           clc
000DA5r 3  65 rr                        adc tmp3        ; add total header length
000DA7r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000DA9r 3  48                           pha             ; we need this in the next step
000DAAr 3  C8                           iny
000DABr 3               
000DABr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
000DADr 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; only need the carry
000DAFr 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000DB1r 3  C8                           iny
000DB2r 3               
000DB2r 3                               ; HEADER BYTE 6,7: End of code ("z_" of this word). By default,
000DB2r 3                               ; we execute a jump to the DOVAR routine, so we need to move three
000DB2r 3                               ; bytes down, and then one more byte so that the z_ label points
000DB2r 3                               ; to the (still fictional) RTS instruction for correct compilation
000DB2r 3  68                           pla             ; LSB of "z_" address
000DB3r 3  18                           clc
000DB4r 3  69 03                        adc #3
000DB6r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000DB8r 3               
000DB8r 3  88                           dey             ; get the MSB of xt back
000DB9r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
000DBBr 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; only need the carry
000DBDr 3  C8                           iny
000DBEr 3  C8                           iny
000DBFr 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000DC1r 3  C8                           iny
000DC2r 3               
000DC2r 3                               ; HEADER BYTE 8: Start of name string. The address is TOS, the
000DC2r 3                               ; length in tmp2. We subtract 8 from the address so we can
000DC2r 3                               ; use the same loop index, which is already 8 byte ahead at
000DC2r 3                               ; this point
000DC2r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
000DC4r 3  38                           sec
000DC5r 3  E9 08                        sbc #8
000DC7r 3  85 rr                        sta tmptos
000DC9r 3               
000DC9r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
000DCBr 3  E9 00                        sbc #0          ; only need carry
000DCDr 3  85 rr                        sta tmptos+1
000DCFr 3               
000DCFr 3               @name_loop:
000DCFr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmptos),y
000DD1r 3               
000DD1r 3                               ; Make sure it goes into the dictionary in lower case.
000DD1r 3  C9 5B                        cmp #$5B         ; ASCII '[' (one past Z)
000DD3r 3  B0 07                        bcs @store_name
000DD5r 3  C9 41                        cmp #$41        ; ASCII 'A'
000DD7r 3  90 03                        bcc @store_name
000DD9r 3               
000DD9r 3                               ; An uppercase letter has been located. Make it
000DD9r 3                               ; lowercase.
000DD9r 3  18                           clc
000DDAr 3  69 20                        adc #$20
000DDCr 3               
000DDCr 3                               ; Fall into @store_name.
000DDCr 3               
000DDCr 3               @store_name:
000DDCr 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000DDEr 3  C8                           iny
000DDFr 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp2
000DE1r 3  D0 EC                        bne @name_loop
000DE3r 3               
000DE3r 3                               ; After thename string comes the code field, starting at the
000DE3r 3                               ; current xt of this word, which is initially a jump to the
000DE3r 3                               ; subroutine to DOVAR. We code this jump by hand
000DE3r 3  A9 20                        lda #$20        ; opcode of JSR
000DE5r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000DE7r 3  C8                           iny
000DE8r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<dovar
000DEAr 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000DECr 3  C8                           iny
000DEDr 3  A9 rr                        lda #>dovar
000DEFr 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000DF1r 3               
000DF1r 3                               ; Update the CURRENT wordlist with the new DP.
000DF1r 3                               ; We do this down here because this routine uses Y.
000DF1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr dp_to_current
000DF4r 3               
000DF4r 3                               ; And we're done. Restore stack
000DF4r 3  E8                           inx
000DF5r 3  E8                           inx
000DF6r 3               
000DF6r 3  60           z_create:       rts
000DF7r 3               
000DF7r 3               
000DF7r 3               
000DF7r 3               ; ## D_MINUS ( d d -- d ) "Subtract two double-celled numbers"
000DF7r 3               ; ## "d-"  auto  ANS double
000DF7r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/double/DMinus"""
000DF7r 3               
000DF7r 3               xt_d_minus:
000DF7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_4 ; two double numbers
000DFAr 3               
000DFAr 3  38                           sec
000DFBr 3               
000DFBr 3  B5 06                        lda 6,x         ; LSB of lower word
000DFDr 3  F5 02                        sbc 2,x
000DFFr 3  95 06                        sta 6,x
000E01r 3               
000E01r 3  B5 07                        lda 7,x         ; MSB of lower word
000E03r 3  F5 03                        sbc 3,x
000E05r 3  95 07                        sta 7,x
000E07r 3               
000E07r 3  B5 04                        lda 4,x         ; LSB of upper word
000E09r 3  F5 00                        sbc 0,x
000E0Br 3  95 04                        sta 4,x
000E0Dr 3               
000E0Dr 3  B5 05                        lda 5,x         ; MSB of upper word
000E0Fr 3  F5 01                        sbc 1,x
000E11r 3  95 05                        sta 5,x
000E13r 3               
000E13r 3  E8                           inx
000E14r 3  E8                           inx
000E15r 3  E8                           inx
000E16r 3  E8                           inx
000E17r 3               
000E17r 3  60           z_d_minus:      rts
000E18r 3               
000E18r 3               
000E18r 3               
000E18r 3               ; ## D_PLUS ( d d -- d ) "Add two double-celled numbers"
000E18r 3               ; ## "d+"  auto  ANS double
000E18r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/double/DPlus"""
000E18r 3               
000E18r 3               xt_d_plus:
000E18r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_4 ; two double numbers
000E1Br 3               
000E1Br 3  18                           clc
000E1Cr 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; LSB of lower word
000E1Er 3  75 06                        adc 6,x
000E20r 3  95 06                        sta 6,x
000E22r 3               
000E22r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x         ; MSB of lower word
000E24r 3  75 07                        adc 7,x
000E26r 3  95 07                        sta 7,x
000E28r 3               
000E28r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB of upper word
000E2Ar 3  75 04                        adc 4,x
000E2Cr 3  95 04                        sta 4,x
000E2Er 3               
000E2Er 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB of upper word
000E30r 3  75 05                        adc 5,x
000E32r 3  95 05                        sta 5,x
000E34r 3               
000E34r 3  E8                           inx
000E35r 3  E8                           inx
000E36r 3  E8                           inx
000E37r 3  E8                           inx
000E38r 3               
000E38r 3  60           z_d_plus:       rts
000E39r 3               
000E39r 3               
000E39r 3               
000E39r 3               ; ## D_TO_S ( d -- n ) "Convert a double number to single"
000E39r 3               ; ## "d>s"  auto  ANS double
000E39r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/double/DtoS
000E39r 3                       ; Though this is basically just DROP, we keep it
000E39r 3                       ; separate so we can test for underflow
000E39r 3                       ; """
000E39r 3               
000E39r 3               xt_d_to_s:
000E39r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
000E3Cr 3               
000E3Cr 3  E8                           inx
000E3Dr 3  E8                           inx
000E3Er 3               
000E3Er 3  60           z_d_to_s:       rts
000E3Fr 3               
000E3Fr 3               
000E3Fr 3               
000E3Fr 3               ; ## DABS ( d -- d ) "Return the absolute value of a double"
000E3Fr 3               ; ## "dabs"  auto  ANS double
000E3Fr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/double/DABS"""
000E3Fr 3               
000E3Fr 3               xt_dabs:
000E3Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2 ; double number
000E42r 3               
000E42r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB of high cell
000E44r 3  10 17                        bpl @done       ; positive, we get off light
000E46r 3               
000E46r 3                               ; negative, calculate 0 - d
000E46r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
000E48r 3  38                           sec
000E49r 3               
000E49r 3  98                           tya
000E4Ar 3  F5 02                        sbc 2,x         ; LSB of low cell
000E4Cr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
000E4Er 3               
000E4Er 3  98                           tya
000E4Fr 3  F5 03                        sbc 3,x         ; MSB of low cell
000E51r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
000E53r 3               
000E53r 3  98                           tya
000E54r 3  F5 00                        sbc 0,x         ; LSB of high cell
000E56r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
000E58r 3               
000E58r 3  98                           tya
000E59r 3  F5 01                        sbc 1,x         ; MSB of high cell
000E5Br 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
000E5Dr 3               @done:
000E5Dr 3  60           z_dabs:         rts
000E5Er 3               
000E5Er 3               
000E5Er 3               
000E5Er 3               ; ## DECIMAL ( -- ) "Change radix base to decimal"
000E5Er 3               ; ## "decimal"  auto  ANS core
000E5Er 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/DECIMAL"""
000E5Er 3               xt_decimal:
000E5Er 3  A9 0A                        lda #10
000E60r 3  85 rr                        sta base
000E62r 3  64 rr                        stz base+1              ; paranoid
000E64r 3               
000E64r 3  60           z_decimal:      rts
000E65r 3               
000E65r 3               
000E65r 3               ; ## DEFER ( "name" -- ) "Create a placeholder for words by name"
000E65r 3               ; ## "defer"  auto  ANS core ext
000E65r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/DEFER
000E65r 3                       ; Reserve an name that can be linked to various xt by IS.
000E65r 3                       ;
000E65r 3                       ; The ANS reference implementation is
000E65r 3                       ;       CREATE ['] ABORT , DOES> @ EXECUTE ;
000E65r 3                       ; But we use this routine as a low-level word so things go faster
000E65r 3               
000E65r 3               xt_defer:
000E65r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_create
000E68r 3               
000E68r 3                               ; CREATE by default installs a subroutine jump to DOVAR,
000E68r 3                               ; but we actually want DODEFER this time. Go back two
000E68r 3                               ; bytes and repace the subroutine jump target
000E68r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp          ; LSB
000E6Ar 3  38                           sec
000E6Br 3  E9 02                        sbc #2
000E6Dr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
000E6Fr 3               
000E6Fr 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1        ; MSB
000E71r 3  E9 00                        sbc #0          ; we only care about the borrow
000E73r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
000E75r 3               
000E75r 3                               ; Save the target address
000E75r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
000E77r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<dodefer   ; LSB
000E79r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000E7Br 3  C8                           iny
000E7Cr 3  A9 rr                        lda #>dodefer   ; MSB
000E7Er 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
000E80r 3               
000E80r 3               
000E80r 3                               ; DODEFER executes the next address it finds after
000E80r 3                               ; its call. As default, we include the error
000E80r 3                               ; "Defer not defined"
000E80r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<defer_error
000E82r 3  92 rr                        sta (cp)
000E84r 3  E6 rr                        inc cp
000E86r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
000E88r 3  E6 rr                        inc cp+1
000E8Ar 3               @1:
000E8Ar 3  A9 rr                        lda #>defer_error
000E8Cr 3  92 rr                        sta (cp)
000E8Er 3  E6 rr                        inc cp
000E90r 3  D0 02                        bne @2
000E92r 3  E6 rr                        inc cp+1
000E94r 3               @2:
000E94r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr adjust_z    ; adjust header to correct length
000E97r 3               
000E97r 3  60           z_defer:        rts
000E98r 3               
000E98r 3               
000E98r 3               
000E98r 3               ; ## DEFER_FETCH ( xt1 -- xt2 ) "Get the current XT for a deferred word"
000E98r 3               ; ## "defer@"  auto  ANS core ext
000E98r 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/DEFERFetch"""
000E98r 3               
000E98r 3               xt_defer_fetch:
000E98r 3                               ; No underflow checking as >BODY does it.
000E98r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_body
000E9Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_fetch
000E9Er 3  60           z_defer_fetch:  rts
000E9Fr 3               
000E9Fr 3               
000E9Fr 3               
000E9Fr 3               ; ## DEFER_STORE ( xt2 x1 -- ) "Set xt1 to execute xt2"
000E9Fr 3               ; ## "defer!"  auto  ANS core ext
000E9Fr 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/DEFERStore"""
000E9Fr 3               
000E9Fr 3               xt_defer_store:
000E9Fr 3                               ; No underflow checking as >BODY and ! do it.
000E9Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_body
000EA2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_store
000EA5r 3  60           z_defer_store:  rts
000EA6r 3               
000EA6r 3               
000EA6r 3               
000EA6r 3               ; ## DEFINITIONS ( -- ) "Make first wordlist in search order the current wordlist"
000EA6r 3               ; ## "definitions" auto ANS search
000EA6r 3               xt_definitions:
000EA6r 3  A0 1F                        ldy #search_order_offset    ; Transfer byte variable
000EA8r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y                  ; SEARCH_ORDER[0] to
000EAAr 3  A0 04                        ldy #current_offset         ; byte variable CURRENT.
000EACr 3  91 rr                        sta (up),y
000EAEr 3  60           z_definitions:  rts
000EAFr 3               
000EAFr 3               
000EAFr 3               ; ## DEPTH ( -- u ) "Get number of cells (not bytes) used by stack"
000EAFr 3               ; ## "depth"  auto  ANS core
000EAFr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/DEPTH"""
000EAFr 3               xt_depth:
000EAFr 3  A9 rr                        lda #dsp0
000EB1r 3  86 rr                        stx tmpdsp
000EB3r 3  38                           sec
000EB4r 3  E5 rr                        sbc tmpdsp
000EB6r 3               
000EB6r 3                               ; divide by two because each cell is two bytes
000EB6r 3  4A                           lsr
000EB7r 3               
000EB7r 3  CA                           dex
000EB8r 3  CA                           dex
000EB9r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
000EBBr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
000EBDr 3               
000EBDr 3  60           z_depth:        rts
000EBEr 3               
000EBEr 3               
000EBEr 3               ; ## DIGIT_QUESTION ( char -- u f | char f ) "Convert ASCII char to number"
000EBEr 3               ; ## "digit?"  auto  Tali Forth
000EBEr 3                       ; """Inspired by the pForth instruction DIGIT, see
000EBEr 3                       ; https://github.com/philburk/pforth/blob/master/fth/numberio.fth
000EBEr 3                       ; Rewritten from DIGIT>NUMBER in Tali Forth. Note in contrast to
000EBEr 3                       ; pForth, we get the base (radix) ourselves instead of having the
000EBEr 3                       ; user provide it. There is no standard name for this routine, which
000EBEr 3                       ; itself is not ANS; we use DIGIT? following pForth and Gforth.
000EBEr 3                       ; """
000EBEr 3               
000EBEr 3               xt_digit_question:
000EBEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
000EC1r 3               
000EC1r 3                               ; one way or another, we're going to need room for the
000EC1r 3                               ; flag on the stack
000EC1r 3  CA                           dex
000EC2r 3  CA                           dex
000EC3r 3  74 00                        stz 0,x                 ; default flag is failure
000EC5r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
000EC7r 3  74 03                        stz 3,x                 ; paranoid
000EC9r 3               
000EC9r 3                               ; Check the character, now in the LSB of NOS. First, make
000EC9r 3                               ; sure we're not below the ASCII code for "0"
000EC9r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
000ECBr 3  C9 30                        cmp #'0'
000ECDr 3  90 23                        bcc @done               ; failure flag already set
000ECFr 3               
000ECFr 3                               ; Next, see if we are below "9", because that would make
000ECFr 3                               ; this a normal number
000ECFr 3  C9 3A                        cmp #'9'+1               ; this is actually ":"
000ED1r 3  90 12                        bcc @checkbase
000ED3r 3               
000ED3r 3                               ; Well, then let's see if this is the gap between "9" and "A"
000ED3r 3                               ; so we can treat the whole range as a number
000ED3r 3  C9 41                        cmp #'A'
000ED5r 3  90 1B                        bcc @done               ; failure flag is already set
000ED7r 3               
000ED7r 3                               ; probably a letter, so we make sure it is uppercase
000ED7r 3  C9 61                        cmp #'a'
000ED9r 3  90 07                        bcc @case_done          ; not lower case, too low
000EDBr 3  C9 7B                        cmp #'z'+1
000EDDr 3  B0 03                        bcs @case_done          ; not lower case, too high
000EDFr 3               
000EDFr 3  18                           clc                     ; just right
000EE0r 3  69 E0                        adc #$e0                ; offset to upper case (wraps)
000EE2r 3               
000EE2r 3               @case_done:
000EE2r 3                               ; get rid of the gap between "9" and "A" so we can treat
000EE2r 3                               ; the whole range as one number
000EE2r 3  38                           sec
000EE3r 3  E9 07                        sbc #7                  ; fall through to @checkbase
000EE5r 3               
000EE5r 3               @checkbase:
000EE5r 3                               ; we have a number, now see if it falls inside the range
000EE5r 3                               ; provided by BASE
000EE5r 3  38                           sec
000EE6r 3  E9 30                        sbc #'0'                 ; this is also the conversion step
000EE8r 3  C5 rr                        cmp base
000EEAr 3  B0 06                        bcs @done               ; already have false flag
000EECr 3               
000EECr 3                               ; Found a legal number
000EECr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x                 ; put number in NOS
000EEEr 3  D6 00                        dec 0,x                 ; set success flag
000EF0r 3  D6 01                        dec 1,x
000EF2r 3               
000EF2r 3               @done:
000EF2r 3               z_digit_question:
000EF2r 3  60                           rts
000EF3r 3               
000EF3r 3               
000EF3r 3               ; ## DISASM ( addr u -- ) "Disassemble a block of memory"
000EF3r 3               ; ## "disasm"  tested  Tali Forth
000EF3r 3                       ; """Convert a segment of memory to assembler output. This
000EF3r 3                       ; word is vectored so people can add their own disassembler.
000EF3r 3                       ; Natively, this produces Simpler Assembly Notation (SAN)
000EF3r 3                       ; code, see the section on The Disassembler in the manual and
000EF3r 3                       ; the file disassembler.asm for more details.
000EF3r 3                       ; """
000EF3r 3               xt_disasm:
000EF3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
000EF6r 3                           .ifdef disassembler
000EF6r 3                               jsr disassembler
000EF6r 3                           .endif
000EF6r 3               
000EF6r 3  60           z_disasm:       rts
000EF7r 3               
000EF7r 3               
000EF7r 3               ; ## DNEGATE ( d -- d ) "Negate double cell number"
000EF7r 3               ; ## "dnegate"  auto  ANS double
000EF7r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/double/DNEGATE"""
000EF7r 3               xt_dnegate:
000EF7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2 ; double number
000EFAr 3               
000EFAr 3  A0 00             		ldy #0
000EFCr 3  38                           sec
000EFDr 3               
000EFDr 3  98                           tya
000EFEr 3  F5 02                        sbc 2,x         ; LSB of low cell
000F00r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
000F02r 3               
000F02r 3  98                           tya
000F03r 3  F5 03                        sbc 3,x         ; MSB of low cell
000F05r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
000F07r 3               
000F07r 3  98                           tya
000F08r 3  F5 00                        sbc 0,x         ; LSB of high cell
000F0Ar 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
000F0Cr 3               
000F0Cr 3  98                           tya
000F0Dr 3  F5 01                        sbc 1,x         ; MSB of high cell
000F0Fr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
000F11r 3               
000F11r 3  60           z_dnegate:      rts
000F12r 3               
000F12r 3               
000F12r 3               ; ## QUESTION_DO ( limit start -- )(R: -- limit start) "Conditional loop start"
000F12r 3               ; ## "?do"  auto  ANS core ext
000F12r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/qDO"""
000F12r 3               xt_question_do:
000F12r 3                               ; ?DO shares most of its code with DO. We use the tmp1 flag
000F12r 3                               ; to mark which is which
000F12r 3  A9 FF                        lda #$ff                ; -1 is ?DO, jump to common code
000F14r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
000F16r 3  80 02                        bra do_common           ; skip flag for DO
000F18r 3               
000F18r 3               ; ## DO ( limit start -- )(R: -- limit start)  "Start a loop"
000F18r 3               ; ## "do"  auto  ANS core
000F18r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/DO
000F18r 3                       ;
000F18r 3                       ; Compile-time part of DO. Could be realized in Forth as
000F18r 3                       ;       : DO POSTPONE (DO) HERE ; IMMEDIATE COMPILE-ONLY
000F18r 3                       ; but we do it in assembler for speed. To work with LEAVE, we compile
000F18r 3                       ; a routine that pushes the end address to the Return Stack at run
000F18r 3                       ; time. This is based on a suggestion by Garth Wilson, see
000F18r 3                       ; the Control Flow section of the manual for details.
000F18r 3                       ;
000F18r 3                       ; This may not be native compile. Don't check for a stack underflow
000F18r 3                       ; """
000F18r 3               
000F18r 3               xt_do:
000F18r 3                               ; DO and ?DO share most of their code, use tmp1 as a flag.
000F18r 3  64 rr                        stz tmp1                ; 0 is DO, drop through to DO_COMMON
000F1Ar 3               do_common:
000F1Ar 3                               ; We push HERE to the Data Stack so LOOP/+LOOP knows where to
000F1Ar 3                               ; compile the address we need to LDA at runtime
000F1Ar 3  CA                           dex
000F1Br 3  CA                           dex
000F1Cr 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
000F1Er 3  95 00                        sta 0,x                 ; LSB
000F20r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
000F22r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x                 ; MSB   ( limit start here )
000F24r 3               
000F24r 3                               ; now we compile six dummy bytes that LOOP/+LOOP will
000F24r 3                               ; replace by the actual LDA/PHA instructions
000F24r 3  A9 05                        lda #5                  ; we don't really care about the value,
000F26r 3  A8                           tay                     ; so we use 5 to be tricky
000F27r 3               @loop:
000F27r 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
000F29r 3  88                           dey
000F2Ar 3  10 FB                        bpl @loop
000F2Cr 3               
000F2Cr 3                               ; update CP
000F2Cr 3  1A                           inc             ; we used 5 as a dummy value, this is why
000F2Dr 3  18                           clc
000F2Er 3  65 rr                        adc cp
000F30r 3  85 rr                        sta cp
000F32r 3  90 02                        bcc @1
000F34r 3  E6 rr                        inc cp+1
000F36r 3               @1:
000F36r 3                               ; compile the (?DO) portion of ?DO if appropriate
000F36r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
000F38r 3  F0 17                        beq @compile_do
000F3Ar 3               
000F3Ar 3                               ; We came from ?DO, so compile its runtime first. We do
000F3Ar 3                               ; this with a quick loop because we know it has to be
000F3Ar 3                               ; Always Native anyway
000F3Ar 3  A0 14                        ldy #question_do_runtime_end-question_do_runtime
000F3Cr 3  5A                           phy             ; save counter to calculate new CP
000F3Dr 3               @2:
000F3Dr 3  B9 rr rr                     lda question_do_runtime,y
000F40r 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
000F42r 3  88                           dey
000F43r 3  10 F8                        bpl @2
000F45r 3               
000F45r 3                               ; adjust CP
000F45r 3  68                           pla             ; retrieve counter
000F46r 3  18                           clc
000F47r 3  65 rr                        adc cp
000F49r 3  85 rr                        sta cp
000F4Br 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
000F4Dr 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; only care about carry
000F4Fr 3  85 rr                        sta cp+1        ; fall through to @compile_do
000F51r 3               
000F51r 3               @compile_do:
000F51r 3                               ; compile runtime part of DO.
000F51r 3  A0 24                        ldy #do_runtime_end-do_runtime  ; counter
000F53r 3  5A                           phy             ; save counter to calculate new CP
000F54r 3               @3:
000F54r 3  B9 rr rr                     lda do_runtime,y
000F57r 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
000F59r 3  88                           dey
000F5Ar 3  10 F8                        bpl @3
000F5Cr 3               
000F5Cr 3                               ; adjust CP
000F5Cr 3  68                           pla             ; retrieve counter
000F5Dr 3  18                           clc
000F5Er 3  65 rr                        adc cp
000F60r 3  85 rr                        sta cp
000F62r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
000F64r 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; only care about carry
000F66r 3  85 rr                        sta cp+1
000F68r 3               
000F68r 3                               ; HERE, hardcoded for speed. We put it on the Data Stack
000F68r 3                               ; where LOOP/+LOOP takes it from. Note this has nothing to
000F68r 3                               ; do with the HERE we're saving for LEAVE
000F68r 3  CA                           dex
000F69r 3  CA                           dex
000F6Ar 3  A5 rr                        lda cp          ; LSB
000F6Cr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
000F6Er 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1        ; MSB
000F70r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
000F72r 3               z_question_do:
000F72r 3  60           z_do:           rts
000F73r 3               
000F73r 3               
000F73r 3               do_runtime:
000F73r 3                       ; """Runtime routine for DO loop. Note that ANS loops quit when the
000F73r 3                       ; boundry of limit-1 and limit is reached, a different mechanism than
000F73r 3                       ; the FIG Forth loop (you can see which version you have by running
000F73r 3                       ; a loop with start and limit as the same value, for instance
000F73r 3                       ; 0 0 DO -- these will walk through the number space). We use a
000F73r 3                       ; "fudge factor" for the limit that makes the Overflow Flag trip when
000F73r 3                       ; it is reached; see http://forum.6502.org/viewtopic.php?f=9&t=2026
000F73r 3                       ; for further discussion of this. The source given there for
000F73r 3                       ; this idea is Laxen & Perry F83. -- This routine is called (DO)
000F73r 3                       ; in some Forths. Usually, we would define this as a separate word
000F73r 3                       ; and compile it with COMPILE, and the Always Native (AN) flag.
000F73r 3                       ; However, we can do it faster if we just copy the bytes
000F73r 3                       ; of this routine with a simple loop in DO.
000F73r 3                       ; """
000F73r 3                               ; First step: create fudge factor (FUFA) by subtracting the
000F73r 3                               ; limit from $8000, the number that will trip the overflow
000F73r 3                               ; flag
000F73r 3  38                           sec
000F74r 3  A9 00                        lda #0
000F76r 3  F5 02                        sbc 2,x         ; LSB of limit
000F78r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x         ; save FUFA for later use
000F7Ar 3               
000F7Ar 3  A9 80                        lda #$80
000F7Cr 3  F5 03                        sbc 3,x         ; MSB of limit
000F7Er 3  95 03                        sta 3,x         ; save FUFA for later use
000F80r 3  48                           pha             ; FUFA replaces limit on R stack
000F81r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; LSB of limit
000F83r 3  48                           pha
000F84r 3               
000F84r 3                               ; Second step: index is FUFA plus original index
000F84r 3  18                           clc
000F85r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB of original index
000F87r 3  75 02                        adc 2,x         ; add LSB of FUFA
000F89r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
000F8Br 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB of orginal index
000F8Dr 3  75 03                        adc 3,x         ; add MSB of FUFA
000F8Fr 3  48                           pha
000F90r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB of index
000F92r 3  48                           pha
000F93r 3               
000F93r 3                               ; we've saved the FUFA on the NOS of the R stack, so we can
000F93r 3                               ; use it later. Clean the Data Stack
000F93r 3  E8                           inx
000F94r 3  E8                           inx
000F95r 3  E8                           inx
000F96r 3  E8                           inx             ; no RTS because this is copied into code
000F97r 3               do_runtime_end:
000F97r 3               
000F97r 3               question_do_runtime:
000F97r 3               
000F97r 3                       ; """This is called (?DO) in some Forths. See the explanation at
000F97r 3                       ; do_runtime for the background on this design
000F97r 3                       ; """
000F97r 3                               ; see if TOS and NOS are equal. Change this to assembler
000F97r 3                               ; for speed
000F97r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_two_dup          ; ( n1 n2 n1 n2 )
000F9Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_equal            ; ( -- n1 n2 f )
000F9Dr 3               
000F9Dr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
000F9Fr 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
000FA1r 3  F0 06                        beq @do_do
000FA3r 3               
000FA3r 3                               ; We're equal, so dump everything and jump beyond the loop.
000FA3r 3                               ; But first, dump six entries off of the Data Stack
000FA3r 3  8A                           txa
000FA4r 3  18                           clc
000FA5r 3  69 06                        adc #6
000FA7r 3  AA                           tax
000FA8r 3               
000FA8r 3                               ; Then abort the whole loop
000FA8r 3  60                           rts
000FA9r 3               @do_do:
000FA9r 3  E8                           inx             ; clear flag from EQUAL off stack
000FAAr 3  E8                           inx             ; no RTS because this is copied into code
000FABr 3               question_do_runtime_end:
000FABr 3               
000FABr 3               
000FABr 3               
000FABr 3               ; ## DOES ( -- ) "Add payload when defining new words"
000FABr 3               ; ## "does>"  auto  ANS core
000FABr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/DOES
000FABr 3                       ; Create the payload for defining new defining words. See
000FABr 3                       ; http://www.bradrodriguez.com/papers/moving3.htm and
000FABr 3                       ; the Developer Guide in the manual for a discussion of
000FABr 3                       ; DOES>'s internal workings. This uses tmp1 and tmp2.
000FABr 3                       ; """
000FABr 3               
000FABr 3               xt_does:
000FABr 3                               ; compile a subroutine jump to runtime of DOES>
000FABr 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>does_runtime
000FADr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<does_runtime
000FAFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
000FB2r 3               
000FB2r 3                               ; compile a subroutine jump to DODOES. In traditional
000FB2r 3                               ; terms, this is the Code Field Area (CFA) of the new
000FB2r 3                               ; word
000FB2r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>dodoes
000FB4r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<dodoes
000FB6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
000FB9r 3               
000FB9r 3  60           z_does:         rts
000FBAr 3               
000FBAr 3               
000FBAr 3               does_runtime:
000FBAr 3                       ; """Runtime portion of DOES>. This replaces the subroutine jump
000FBAr 3                       ; to DOVAR that CREATE automatically encodes by a jump to the
000FBAr 3                       ; address that contains a subroutine jump to DODOES. We don't
000FBAr 3                       ; jump to DODOES directly because we need to work our magic with
000FBAr 3                       ; the return addresses. This routine is also known as "(DOES)" in
000FBAr 3                       ; other Forths
000FBAr 3                       ; """
000FBAr 3               
000FBAr 3  7A                           ply             ; LSB
000FBBr 3  68                           pla             ; MSB
000FBCr 3               
000FBCr 3  C8                           iny
000FBDr 3  D0 01                        bne @1
000FBFr 3  1A                           inc
000FC0r 3               @1:
000FC0r 3  84 rr                        sty tmp1
000FC2r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
000FC4r 3               
000FC4r 3                               ; CREATE has also already modified the DP to point to the new
000FC4r 3                               ; word. We have no idea which instructions followed the CREATE
000FC4r 3                               ; command if there is a DOES> so the CP could point anywhere
000FC4r 3                               ; by now. The address of the word's xt is four bytes down.
000FC4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr current_to_dp   ; Grab the DP from the CURRENT wordlist.
000FC7r 3  A5 rr                        lda dp
000FC9r 3  18                           clc
000FCAr 3  69 04                        adc #4
000FCCr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2
000FCEr 3  A5 rr                        lda dp+1
000FD0r 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; we only care about the carry
000FD2r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1
000FD4r 3               
000FD4r 3                               ; Now we get that address and add one byte to skip over the JSR
000FD4r 3                               ; opcode
000FD4r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp2)
000FD6r 3  18                           clc
000FD7r 3  69 01                        adc #1
000FD9r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3
000FDBr 3  A0 01                        ldy #1
000FDDr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp2),y
000FDFr 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; we only care about the carry
000FE1r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3+1
000FE3r 3               
000FE3r 3                               ; Replace the DOVAR address with our own
000FE3r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1        ; LSB
000FE5r 3  92 rr                        sta (tmp3)
000FE7r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
000FE9r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp3),y    ; Y is still 1
000FEBr 3               
000FEBr 3                               ; Since we removed the return address that brought us here, we
000FEBr 3                               ; go back to whatever the main routine was. Otherwise, we we
000FEBr 3                               ; smash into the subroutine jump to DODOES.
000FEBr 3  60                           rts
000FECr 3               
000FECr 3               
000FECr 3               
000FECr 3               ; ## DOT ( u -- ) "Print TOS"
000FECr 3               ; ## "."  auto  ANS core
000FECr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/d"""
000FECr 3               
000FECr 3               xt_dot:
000FECr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
000FEFr 3               
000FEFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup                      ; ( n n )
000FF2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_abs                      ; ( n u )
000FF5r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero                     ; ( n u 0 )
000FF8r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_less_number_sign         ; ( n u 0 )
000FFBr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_s            ; ( n ud )
000FFEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_rot                      ; ( ud n )
001001r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_sign                     ; ( ud )
001004r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_greater      ; ( addr u )
001007r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
00100Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
00100Dr 3               
00100Dr 3  60           z_dot:          rts
00100Er 3               
00100Er 3               
00100Er 3               
00100Er 3               ; ## DOT_PAREN ( -- ) "Print input up to close paren .( comment )"
00100Er 3               ; ## ".("  auto  ANS core
00100Er 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Dotp"""
00100Er 3               
00100Er 3               xt_dot_paren:
00100Er 3                               ; Put a right paren on the stack.
00100Er 3  CA                           dex
00100Fr 3  CA                           dex
001010r 3  A9 29                        lda #41     ; Right parenthesis
001012r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001014r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001016r 3               
001016r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_parse
001019r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
00101Cr 3               
00101Cr 3  60           z_dot_paren:    rts
00101Dr 3               
00101Dr 3               
00101Dr 3               
00101Dr 3               ; ## DOT_QUOTE ( "string" -- ) "Print string from compiled word"
00101Dr 3               ; ## ".""  auto  ANS core ext
00101Dr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Dotq
00101Dr 3                       ; Compile string that is printed during run time. ANS Forth wants
00101Dr 3                       ; this to be compile-only, even though everybody and their friend
00101Dr 3                       ; uses it for everything. We follow the book here, and recommend
00101Dr 3                       ; `.(` for general printing.
00101Dr 3                       ; """
00101Dr 3               
00101Dr 3               xt_dot_quote:
00101Dr 3                               ; we let S" do the heavy lifting. Since we're in
00101Dr 3                               ; compile mode, it will save the string and reproduce it
00101Dr 3                               ; during runtime
00101Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_s_quote
001020r 3               
001020r 3                               ; We then let TYPE do the actual printing
001020r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>xt_type
001022r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<xt_type
001024r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
001027r 3               
001027r 3  60           z_dot_quote:    rts
001028r 3               
001028r 3               
001028r 3               
001028r 3               ; ## DOT_R ( n u -- ) "Print NOS as unsigned number with TOS with"
001028r 3               ; ## ".r"  tested  ANS core ext
001028r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/DotR
001028r 3                       ;
001028r 3                       ; Based on the Forth code
001028r 3                       ;  : .R  >R DUP ABS 0 <# #S ROT SIGN #> R> OVER - SPACES TYPE ;
001028r 3                       ; """
001028r 3               
001028r 3               xt_dot_r:
001028r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
00102Br 3               
00102Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_r
00102Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup
001031r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_abs
001034r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero
001037r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_less_number_sign
00103Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_s
00103Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_rot
001040r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_sign
001043r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_greater
001046r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_from
001049r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_over
00104Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_minus
00104Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_spaces
001052r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
001055r 3               
001055r 3  60           z_dot_r:        rts
001056r 3               
001056r 3               
001056r 3               
001056r 3               ; ## DOT_S ( -- ) "Print content of Data Stack"
001056r 3               ; ## ".s"  tested  ANS tools
001056r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/tools/DotS
001056r 3                       ; Print content of Data Stack non-distructively. We follow the format
001056r 3                       ; of Gforth and print the number of elements first in brackets,
001056r 3                       ; followed by the Data Stack content (if any).
001056r 3                       ;
001056r 3                       ; Since this is for humans, we don't have to worry about speed.
001056r 3                       ; """
001056r 3               
001056r 3               xt_dot_s:
001056r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_depth    ; ( -- u )
001059r 3               
001059r 3                               ; Print stack depth in brackets
001059r 3  A9 3C                        lda #$3c        ; ASCII for "<"
00105Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
00105Er 3               
00105Er 3                               ; We keep a copy of the number of the things on the stack
00105Er 3                               ; to use as a counter later down. This assumes that there
00105Er 3                               ; are less than 255 elements on the stack
00105Er 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001060r 3  48                           pha
001061r 3               
001061r 3                               ; print unsigned number without the trailing space
001061r 3  CA                           dex             ; DUP
001062r 3  CA                           dex
001063r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001065r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001067r 3               
001067r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr print_u
00106Ar 3               
00106Ar 3  A9 3E                        lda #$3e        ; ASCII for ">"
00106Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
00106Fr 3  A9 20                        lda #AscSP      ; ASCII for SPACE
001071r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001074r 3               
001074r 3  E8                           inx
001075r 3  E8                           inx
001076r 3               
001076r 3                               ; There will be lots of cases where the stack is empty. If that
001076r 3                               ; is so, get out of here quickly
001076r 3  E0 rr                        cpx #dsp0
001078r 3  F0 1E                        beq @done
00107Ar 3               
00107Ar 3               @have_stack:
00107Ar 3                               ; We have at least one element on the stack. The depth of the
00107Ar 3                               ; stack is on the stack, we can use it as a counter. We go
00107Ar 3                               ; from bottom to top
00107Ar 3  7A                           ply
00107Br 3               
00107Br 3  A9 rr                        lda #dsp0-1     ; go up one to avoid garbage
00107Dr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3
00107Fr 3  64 rr                        stz tmp3+1      ; must be zero page on the 65c02
001081r 3               @loop:
001081r 3  CA                           dex
001082r 3  CA                           dex
001083r 3               
001083r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp3)
001085r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001087r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp3
001089r 3               
001089r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp3)
00108Br 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
00108Dr 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp3
00108Fr 3  5A                           phy
001090r 3               
001090r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dot
001093r 3               
001093r 3  7A                           ply
001094r 3  88                           dey
001095r 3  D0 EA                        bne @loop
001097r 3               
001097r 3  48                           pha             ; dummy to balance stack
001098r 3               @done:
001098r 3  68                           pla
001099r 3  60           z_dot_s:        rts
00109Ar 3               
00109Ar 3               
00109Ar 3               
00109Ar 3               ; ## D_DOT ( d -- ) "Print double"
00109Ar 3               ; ## "d."  tested  ANS double
00109Ar 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/double/Dd"""
00109Ar 3                       ;
00109Ar 3                       ; From the Forth code:
00109Ar 3                       ; : D. TUCK DABS <# #S ROT SIGN #> TYPE SPACE ;
00109Ar 3                       ; """
00109Ar 3               
00109Ar 3               xt_d_dot:
00109Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
00109Dr 3
