00154Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero
00154Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero
001552r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_two_r_from       ; ( addr1 u1 0 0 addr3 u3 ) ( R: addr2 addr2 )
001555r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_number        ; ( addr1 u1 n n addr4 u4 ) ( R: addr2 addr2 )
001558r 3               
001558r 3                               ; If u4 is not zero, we have leftover chars and have to do
001558r 3                               ; things differently
001558r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
00155Ar 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
00155Cr 3  D0 17                        bne @have_chars_left
00155Er 3               
00155Er 3                               ; Normal case, this number is all done
00155Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_two_drop         ; ( addr1 u1 n n ) ( R: addr2 addr2 )
001561r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_d_to_s           ; ( addr1 u1 n ) ( R: addr2 addr2 )
001564r 3               
001564r 3                               ; Store the new value
001564r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_fetch          ; ( addr1 u1 n addr2 ) ( R: addr2 addr2 )
001567r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_c_store          ; ( addr1 u1 ) ( R: addr2 addr2 )
00156Ar 3               
00156Ar 3                               ; Increase counter
00156Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_from           ; R>
00156Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_one_plus         ; 1+
001570r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_r             ; >R ( addr1 u1 ) ( R: addr2+1 addr2 )
001573r 3  80 CB                        bra @loop
001575r 3               
001575r 3               @have_chars_left:
001575r 3                               ; Pathological case: Drop the rest of this number off the stack
001575r 3                               ; and continue with the next word. Doesn't print a warning. We
001575r 3                               ; need to drop four cells, that is, eight bytes
001575r 3  8A                           txa
001576r 3  18                           clc
001577r 3  69 08                        adc #8
001579r 3  AA                           tax
00157Ar 3  80 C4                        bra @loop
00157Cr 3               
00157Cr 3               @done:
00157Cr 3                               ; Clean up return stack and calculate number of chars stored
00157Cr 3  E8                           inx
00157Dr 3  E8                           inx
00157Er 3  E8                           inx
00157Fr 3  E8                           inx                     ; 2DROP
001580r 3               
001580r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_two_r_from       ; ( addr2+n addr2 )
001583r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_swap
001586r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_minus            ; ( n )
001589r 3               
001589r 3  60           z_hexstore:     rts
00158Ar 3               
00158Ar 3               
00158Ar 3               
00158Ar 3               ; ## HOLD ( char -- ) "Insert character at current output"
00158Ar 3               ; ## "hold"  auto  ANS core
00158Ar 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/HOLD
00158Ar 3                       ; Insert a character at the current position of a pictured numeric
00158Ar 3                       ; output string on
00158Ar 3                       ; https://github.com/philburk/pforth/blob/master/fth/numberio.fth
00158Ar 3                       ;
00158Ar 3                       ; Forth code is : HOLD  -1 HLD +!  HLD @ C! ;  We use the the internal
00158Ar 3                       ; variable tohold instead of HLD.
00158Ar 3                       ; """
00158Ar 3               xt_hold:
00158Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
00158Dr 3               
00158Dr 3  A5 rr                        lda tohold
00158Fr 3  D0 02                        bne @1
001591r 3  C6 rr                        dec tohold+1
001593r 3               @1:
001593r 3  C6 rr                        dec tohold
001595r 3               
001595r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001597r 3  92 rr                        sta (tohold)
001599r 3  E8                           inx
00159Ar 3  E8                           inx
00159Br 3               
00159Br 3  60           z_hold:         rts
00159Cr 3               
00159Cr 3               
00159Cr 3               ; ## I ( -- n )(R: n -- n)  "Copy loop counter to stack"
00159Cr 3               ; ## "i"  auto  ANS core
00159Cr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/I
00159Cr 3                       ; Note that this is not the same as R@ because we use a fudge
00159Cr 3                       ; factor for loop control; see the Control Flow section of the
00159Cr 3                       ; manual for details.
00159Cr 3                       ;
00159Cr 3                       ; We should make this native compile for speed.
00159Cr 3                       ; """
00159Cr 3               
00159Cr 3               xt_i:
00159Cr 3  CA                           dex
00159Dr 3  CA                           dex
00159Er 3               
00159Er 3                               ; Get the fudged index off of the top of the stack. It's
00159Er 3                               ; easier to do math on the stack directly than to pop and
00159Er 3                               ; push stuff around
00159Er 3  86 rr                        stx tmpdsp
0015A0r 3  BA                           tsx
0015A1r 3               
0015A1r 3  38                           sec
0015A2r 3  BD 01 01                     lda $0101,x     ; LSB
0015A5r 3  FD 03 01                     sbc $0103,x
0015A8r 3  A8                           tay
0015A9r 3               
0015A9r 3  BD 02 01                     lda $0102,x     ; MSB
0015ACr 3  FD 04 01                     sbc $0104,x
0015AFr 3               
0015AFr 3  A6 rr                        ldx tmpdsp
0015B1r 3               
0015B1r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x         ; MSB of de-fudged index
0015B3r 3  94 00                        sty 0,x         ; LSB of de-fudged index
0015B5r 3               
0015B5r 3  60           z_i:            rts
0015B6r 3               
0015B6r 3               
0015B6r 3               
0015B6r 3               ; ## IF (C: -- orig) (flag -- ) "Conditional flow control"
0015B6r 3               ; ## "if"  auto  ANS core
0015B6r 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/IF"""
0015B6r 3               
0015B6r 3               xt_if:
0015B6r 3                               ; Compile a 0BRANCH
0015B6r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>zero_branch_runtime
0015B8r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<zero_branch_runtime
0015BAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
0015BDr 3               
0015BDr 3                               ; Put the origination address on the stack for else/then
0015BDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_here
0015C0r 3               
0015C0r 3                               ; Stuff zero in for the branch address right now.
0015C0r 3                               ; THEN or ELSE will fix it later.
0015C0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero
0015C3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_comma
0015C6r 3  60           z_if:           rts
0015C7r 3               
0015C7r 3               
0015C7r 3               zero_branch_runtime:
0015C7r 3                       ; """In some Forths, this is called (0BRANCH). Tali Forth originally
0015C7r 3                       ; included 0BRANCH as a high-level word that inserted this code at
0015C7r 3                       ; runtime.
0015C7r 3                       ; """
0015C7r 3               
0015C7r 3                               ; We use the return value on the 65c02 stack to determine
0015C7r 3                               ; where we want to return to.
0015C7r 3  68                           pla
0015C8r 3  85 rr                        sta tmpbranch
0015CAr 3  68                           pla
0015CBr 3  85 rr                        sta tmpbranch+1
0015CDr 3               
0015CDr 3                               ; See if the flag is zero, which is the whole purpose of
0015CDr 3                               ; this all
0015CDr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0015CFr 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
0015D1r 3  F0 0F                        beq @zero
0015D3r 3               
0015D3r 3                               ; Flag is TRUE, so we skip over the next two bytes. This is
0015D3r 3                               ; the part between IF and THEN
0015D3r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmpbranch   ; LSB
0015D5r 3  18                           clc
0015D6r 3  69 02                        adc #2
0015D8r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
0015DAr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmpbranch+1 ; MSB
0015DCr 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; For carry
0015DEr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
0015E0r 3               
0015E0r 3  80 13                        bra @done
0015E2r 3               
0015E2r 3               @zero:
0015E2r 3                               ; Flag is FALSE (0) so we take the jump to the address given in
0015E2r 3                               ; the next two bytes. However, the address points to the last
0015E2r 3                               ; byte of the JSR instruction, not to the next byte afterwards
0015E2r 3  A0 01                        ldy #1
0015E4r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmpbranch),y
0015E6r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
0015E8r 3  C8                           iny
0015E9r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmpbranch),y
0015EBr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
0015EDr 3               
0015EDr 3                               ; Now we have to subtract one byte from the address
0015EDr 3                               ; given because of the way the 6502 calculates RTS
0015EDr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
0015EFr 3  D0 02                        bne @1
0015F1r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1+1
0015F3r 3               @1:
0015F3r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1
0015F5r 3               
0015F5r 3               @done:
0015F5r 3                               ; However we got here, tmp1 has the value we push to jump
0015F5r 3                               ; to
0015F5r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
0015F7r 3  48                           pha             ; MSB first
0015F8r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
0015FAr 3  48                           pha
0015FBr 3               
0015FBr 3                               ; clean up the stack and jump
0015FBr 3  E8                           inx
0015FCr 3  E8                           inx
0015FDr 3               
0015FDr 3  60                           rts
0015FEr 3               
0015FEr 3               
0015FEr 3               
0015FEr 3               ; ## IMMEDIATE ( -- ) "Mark most recent word as IMMEDIATE"
0015FEr 3               ; ## "immediate"  auto  ANS core
0015FEr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/IMMEDIATE
0015FEr 3                       ; Make sure the most recently defined word is immediate. Will only
0015FEr 3                       ; affect the last word in the dictionary. Note that if the word is
0015FEr 3                       ; defined in ROM, this will have no affect, but will not produce an
0015FEr 3                       ; error message.
0015FEr 3                       ; """
0015FEr 3               xt_immediate:
0015FEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr current_to_dp
001601r 3  A0 01                        ldy #1          ; offset for status byte
001603r 3  B1 rr                        lda (dp),y
001605r 3  09 04                        ora #IM        ; make sure bit 7 is set
001607r 3  91 rr                        sta (dp),y
001609r 3               
001609r 3  60           z_immediate:    rts
00160Ar 3               
00160Ar 3               
00160Ar 3               ; ## INPUT ( -- addr ) "Return address of input vector"
00160Ar 3               ; ## "input" tested Tali Forth
00160Ar 3               
00160Ar 3               xt_input:
00160Ar 3  CA                           dex
00160Br 3  CA                           dex
00160Cr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<input
00160Er 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001610r 3  A9 rr                        lda #>input
001612r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001614r 3               
001614r 3  60           z_input:        rts
001615r 3               
001615r 3               
001615r 3               
001615r 3               ; ## INPUT_TO_R ( -- ) ( R: -- n n n n ) "Save input state to the Return Stack"
001615r 3               ; ## "input>r"  tested  Tali Forth
001615r 3                  	; """Save the current input state as defined by insrc, cib, ciblen, and
001615r 3                       ; toin to the Return Stack. Used by EVALUTE.
001615r 3                       ;
001615r 3                       ; The naive way of doing
001615r 3                       ; this is to push each two-byte variable to the stack in the form of
001615r 3                       ;
001615r 3                       ;       lda insrc
001615r 3                       ;       pha
001615r 3                       ;       lda insrc+1
001615r 3                       ;       pha
001615r 3                       ;
001615r 3                       ; for a total of 24 byte of instruction in one direction and later
001615r 3                       ; a further 24 bytes to reverse the process. We shorten this at the
001615r 3                       ; cost of some speed by assuming the four variables are grouped
001615r 3                       ; together on the Zero Page and start with insrc (see definitions.asm
001615r 3                       ; for details). The reverse operation is r_to_input. These words must
001615r 3                       ; be flagged as Never Native. Uses tmp1
001615r 3                       ; """
001615r 3               
001615r 3               xt_input_to_r:
001615r 3                               ; We arrive here with the return address on the top of the
001615r 3                               ; 65c02's stack. We need to move it out of the way first
001615r 3  68                           pla
001616r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001618r 3  68                           pla
001619r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
00161Br 3               
00161Br 3                               ; This assumes that insrc is the first of eight bytes and
00161Br 3                               ; toin+1 the last in the sequence we want to save from the Zero
00161Br 3                               ; Page.
00161Br 3  A0 07                        ldy #7
00161Dr 3               @loop:
00161Dr 3  B9 rr rr                     lda insrc,y     ; insrc+7 is toin+1
001620r 3  48                           pha
001621r 3  88                           dey
001622r 3  10 F9                        bpl @loop
001624r 3               
001624r 3                               ; Restore address for return jump
001624r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
001626r 3  48                           pha
001627r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
001629r 3  48                           pha
00162Ar 3               
00162Ar 3  60           z_input_to_r: 	rts
00162Br 3               
00162Br 3               
00162Br 3               
00162Br 3               ; ## INT_TO_NAME ( xt -- nt ) "Get name token from execution token"
00162Br 3               ; ## "int>name"  auto  Tali Forth
00162Br 3                       ; """www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Name-token.html
00162Br 3                       ; This is called >NAME in Gforth, but we change it to
00162Br 3                       ; INT>NAME to match NAME>INT
00162Br 3                       ; """
00162Br 3               
00162Br 3               xt_int_to_name:
00162Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
00162Er 3               
00162Er 3                               ; Unfortunately, to find the header, we have to walk through
00162Er 3                               ; all of the wordlists. We are running out of tmp variables.
00162Er 3                               ; (I'm assuming there is a reason this is avoiding tmp1) so
00162Er 3                               ; hold the current wordlist on the data stack. This searches
00162Er 3                               ; all of the wordlists in id order.
00162Er 3  CA                           dex
00162Fr 3  CA                           dex
001630r 3  74 00                        stz 0,x
001632r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001634r 3               
001634r 3               @wordlist_loop:
001634r 3                               ; A needs to have the current wordlist id in it at
001634r 3                               ; the top of this loop.
001634r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x                 ; Get the current wordlist.
001636r 3               
001636r 3                               ; Get the DP for that wordlist.
001636r 3  0A                           asl                     ; Turn offset into cells offset.
001637r 3  18                           clc
001638r 3  69 06                        adc #wordlists_offset
00163Ar 3  A8                           tay
00163Br 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y              ; Save the DP for this wordlist
00163Dr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2                ; into tmp2
00163Fr 3  C8                           iny
001640r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
001642r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1
001644r 3               
001644r 3                               ; Check for an empty wordlist (DP will be 0)
001644r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
001646r 3  05 rr                        ora tmp2+1
001648r 3  F0 38                        beq @next_wordlist
00164Ar 3               
00164Ar 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; Target xt is now behind wordlist id.
00164Cr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3        ; Save target xt in tmp3
00164Er 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
001650r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3+1
001652r 3               
001652r 3               @loop:
001652r 3  A0 04                        ldy #4          ; xt is four bytes down
001654r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp2),y    ; LSB of xt of current nt
001656r 3  C5 rr                        cmp tmp3
001658r 3  D0 07                        bne @no_match
00165Ar 3               
00165Ar 3                               ; LSB is the same, now check MSB
00165Ar 3  C8                           iny
00165Br 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp2),y    ; MSB of xt of current nt
00165Dr 3  C5 rr                        cmp tmp3+1
00165Fr 3  F0 32                        beq @match
001661r 3               
001661r 3               @no_match:
001661r 3                               ; no match, so we need to get the next word. Next nt is two
001661r 3                               ; bytes down
001661r 3  18                           clc
001662r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
001664r 3  69 02                        adc #2
001666r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2
001668r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1
00166Ar 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; only care about carry
00166Cr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1
00166Er 3               
00166Er 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
001670r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp2),y
001672r 3  48                           pha
001673r 3  C8                           iny
001674r 3  11 rr                        ora (tmp2),y
001676r 3  F0 09                        beq @zero
001678r 3               
001678r 3                               ; Not zero continue
001678r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp2),y
00167Ar 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1
00167Cr 3  68                           pla
00167Dr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2
00167Fr 3  80 D1                        bra @loop
001681r 3               
001681r 3               @zero:
001681r 3                               ; if next word is zero, the xt has no nt in this wordlist
001681r 3  68                           pla             ; Leftover from above loop
001682r 3               
001682r 3               @next_wordlist:
001682r 3                               ; Move on to the next wordlist.
001682r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001684r 3  1A                           inc
001685r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001687r 3  C9 0C                        cmp #max_wordlists
001689r 3  D0 A9                        bne @wordlist_loop
00168Br 3               
00168Br 3                               ; We didn't find it in any of the wordlists.
00168Br 3                               ; Remove the wordlist id from the stack.
00168Br 3  E8                           inx
00168Cr 3  E8                           inx
00168Dr 3               
00168Dr 3                               ; We return a zero to indicate that we didn't find it.
00168Dr 3  74 00                        stz 0,x
00168Fr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001691r 3  80 0A                        bra z_int_to_name
001693r 3               
001693r 3               @match:
001693r 3                               ; We found it. Remove wordlist id from stack.
001693r 3  E8                           inx
001694r 3  E8                           inx
001695r 3               
001695r 3                               ; It's a match! Replace TOS with nt
001695r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
001697r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001699r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1
00169Br 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
00169Dr 3               
00169Dr 3  60           z_int_to_name:  rts
00169Er 3               
00169Er 3               
00169Er 3               
00169Er 3               ; ## INVERT ( n -- n ) "Complement of TOS"
00169Er 3               ; ## "invert"  auto  ANS core
00169Er 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/INVERT"""
00169Er 3               xt_invert:
00169Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
0016A1r 3               
0016A1r 3  A9 FF                        lda #$FF
0016A3r 3  55 00                        eor 0,x         ; LSB
0016A5r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0016A7r 3               
0016A7r 3  A9 FF                        lda #$FF
0016A9r 3  55 01                        eor 1,x         ; MSB
0016ABr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0016ADr 3               
0016ADr 3  60           z_invert:       rts
0016AEr 3               
0016AEr 3               
0016AEr 3               ; ## IS ( xt "name" -- ) "Set named word to execute xt"
0016AEr 3               ; ## "is"  auto  ANS core ext
0016AEr 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/IS"""
0016AEr 3               
0016AEr 3               xt_is:
0016AEr 3                               ; This is a state aware word with differet behavior
0016AEr 3                               ; when used while compiling vs interpreting.
0016AEr 3                               ; Check STATE
0016AEr 3  A5 rr                        lda state
0016B0r 3  05 rr                        ora state+1
0016B2r 3  F0 0C                        beq @interpreting
0016B4r 3               
0016B4r 3               @compiling:
0016B4r 3                               ; Run ['] to compile the xt of the next word as a literal.
0016B4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_bracket_tick
0016B7r 3               
0016B7r 3                               ; Postpone DEFER! by compiling a JSR to it.
0016B7r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>xt_defer_store
0016B9r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<xt_defer_store
0016BBr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
0016BEr 3               
0016BEr 3  80 06                        bra @done
0016C0r 3               
0016C0r 3               @interpreting:
0016C0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_tick
0016C3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_defer_store
0016C6r 3               @done:
0016C6r 3  60           z_is:           rts
0016C7r 3               
0016C7r 3               
0016C7r 3               
0016C7r 3               ; ## J ( -- n ) (R: n -- n ) "Copy second loop counter to stack"
0016C7r 3               ; ## "j"  auto  ANS core
0016C7r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/J
0016C7r 3                       ; Copy second loop counter from Return Stack to stack. Note we use
0016C7r 3                       ; a fudge factor for loop control; see the Control Flow section of
0016C7r 3                       ; the manual for more details.
0016C7r 3                       ; At this point, we have the "I" counter/limit and the LEAVE address
0016C7r 3                       ; on the stack above this (three entries), whereas the ideal Forth
0016C7r 3                       ; implementation would just have two.
0016C7r 3                       ;
0016C7r 3                       ; Make this native compiled for speed
0016C7r 3                       ; """
0016C7r 3               
0016C7r 3               xt_j:
0016C7r 3  CA                           dex
0016C8r 3  CA                           dex
0016C9r 3               
0016C9r 3                               ; Get the fudged index off from the stack. It's easier to
0016C9r 3                               ; do math on the stack directly than to pop and push stuff
0016C9r 3                               ; around
0016C9r 3  86 rr                        stx tmpdsp
0016CBr 3  BA                           tsx
0016CCr 3               
0016CCr 3  38                           sec
0016CDr 3  BD 07 01                     lda $0107,x     ; LSB
0016D0r 3  FD 09 01                     sbc $0109,x
0016D3r 3  A8                           tay
0016D4r 3               
0016D4r 3  BD 08 01                     lda $0108,x     ; MSB
0016D7r 3  FD 0A 01                     sbc $010A,x
0016DAr 3               
0016DAr 3  A6 rr                        ldx tmpdsp
0016DCr 3               
0016DCr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x         ; MSB of de-fudged index
0016DEr 3  94 00                        sty 0,x         ; LSB of de-fudged index
0016E0r 3               
0016E0r 3  60           z_j:            rts
0016E1r 3               
0016E1r 3               
0016E1r 3               
0016E1r 3               ; ## KEY ( -- char ) "Get one character from the input"
0016E1r 3               ; ## "key"  tested  ANS core
0016E1r 3               xt_key:
0016E1r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/KEY
0016E1r 3                       ; Get a single character of input from the vectored
0016E1r 3                       ; input without echoing.
0016E1r 3                       ; """
0016E1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr key_a               ; returns char in A
0016E4r 3               
0016E4r 3  CA                           dex
0016E5r 3  CA                           dex
0016E6r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0016E8r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
0016EAr 3               
0016EAr 3  60           z_key:          rts
0016EBr 3               
0016EBr 3               key_a:
0016EBr 3                       ; The 65c02 doesn't have a JSR (ADDR,X) instruction like the
0016EBr 3                       ; 65816, so we have to fake the indirect jump to vector it.
0016EBr 3                       ; This is depressingly slow. We use this routine internally
0016EBr 3                       ; to avoid manipulating the Data Stack when we just want a
0016EBr 3                       ; character
0016EBr 3  6C rr rr                     jmp (input)             ; JSR/RTS
0016EEr 3               
0016EEr 3               
0016EEr 3               ; ## LATESTNT ( -- nt ) "Push most recent nt to the stack"
0016EEr 3               ; ## "latestnt"  auto  Tali Forth
0016EEr 3                       ; """www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Name-token.html
0016EEr 3                       ; The Gforth version of this word is called LATEST
0016EEr 3                       ; """
0016EEr 3               xt_latestnt:
0016EEr 3  CA                           dex
0016EFr 3  CA                           dex
0016F0r 3               
0016F0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr current_to_dp
0016F3r 3               
0016F3r 3  A5 rr                        lda dp
0016F5r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0016F7r 3  A5 rr                        lda dp+1
0016F9r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0016FBr 3               
0016FBr 3  60           z_latestnt:     rts
0016FCr 3               
0016FCr 3               
0016FCr 3               ; ## LATESTXT ( -- xt ) "Push most recent xt to the stack"
0016FCr 3               ; ## "latestxt"  auto  Gforth
0016FCr 3                       ; """http://www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Anonymous-Definitions.html"""
0016FCr 3               xt_latestxt:
0016FCr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_latestnt         ; ( nt )
0016FFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_name_to_int      ; ( xt )
001702r 3               
001702r 3  60           z_latestxt:     rts
001703r 3               
001703r 3               
001703r 3               ; ## LEAVE ( -- ) "Leave DO/LOOP construct"
001703r 3               ; ## "leave"  auto  ANS core
001703r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/LEAVE
001703r 3                       ; Note that this does not work with anything but a DO/LOOP in
001703r 3                       ; contrast to other versions such as discussed at
001703r 3                       ; http://blogs.msdn.com/b/ashleyf/archive/2011/02/06/loopty-do-i-loop.aspx
001703r 3                       ;
001703r 3                       ;       : LEAVE POSTPONE BRANCH HERE SWAP 0 , ; IMMEDIATE COMPILE-ONLY
001703r 3                       ; See the Control Flow section in the manual for details of how this works.
001703r 3                       ; This must be native compile and not IMMEDIATE
001703r 3                       ; """
001703r 3               
001703r 3               xt_leave:
001703r 3                               ; We dump the limit/start entries off the Return Stack
001703r 3                               ; (four bytes)
001703r 3  68                           pla
001704r 3  68                           pla
001705r 3  68                           pla
001706r 3  68                           pla
001707r 3               
001707r 3  60                           rts             ; this must be compiled, so keep before z_leave
001708r 3               z_leave:                        ; not reached, not compiled
001708r 3               
001708r 3               
001708r 3               
001708r 3               ; ## LEFT_BRACKET ( -- ) "Enter interpretation state"
001708r 3               ; ## "["  auto  ANS core
001708r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Bracket
001708r 3                       ; This is an immediate and compile-only word
001708r 3                       ; """
001708r 3               xt_left_bracket:
001708r 3  64 rr                        stz state
00170Ar 3  64 rr                        stz state+1
00170Cr 3               
00170Cr 3  60           z_left_bracket: rts
00170Dr 3               
00170Dr 3               
00170Dr 3               ; ## LESS_NUMBER_SIGN ( -- ) "Start number conversion"
00170Dr 3               ; ## "<#"  auto  ANS core
00170Dr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/num-start
00170Dr 3                       ; Start the process to create pictured numeric output.
00170Dr 3                       ;
00170Dr 3                       ; The new
00170Dr 3                       ; string is constructed from back to front, saving the new character
00170Dr 3                       ; at the beginning of the output string. Since we use PAD as a
00170Dr 3                       ; starting address and work backward (!), the string is constructed
00170Dr 3                       ; in the space between the end of the Dictionary (as defined by CP)
00170Dr 3                       ; and the PAD. This allows us to satisfy the ANS Forth condition that
00170Dr 3                       ; programs don't fool around with the PAD but still use its address.
00170Dr 3                       ; Based on pForth
00170Dr 3                       ; http://pforth.googlecode.com/svn/trunk/fth/numberio.fth
00170Dr 3                       ; pForth is in the pubic domain. Forth is : <# PAD HLD ! ; we use the
00170Dr 3                       ; internal variable tohold instead of HLD.
00170Dr 3                       ; """
00170Dr 3               xt_less_number_sign:
00170Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_pad      ; ( addr )
001710r 3               
001710r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001712r 3  85 rr                        sta tohold
001714r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
001716r 3  85 rr                        sta tohold+1
001718r 3               
001718r 3  E8                           inx
001719r 3  E8                           inx
00171Ar 3               
00171Ar 3               z_less_number_sign:
00171Ar 3  60                           rts
00171Br 3               
00171Br 3               ; ## LESS_THAN ( n m -- f ) "Return true if NOS < TOS"
00171Br 3               ; ## "<"  auto  ANS core
00171Br 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/less"""
00171Br 3               
00171Br 3               xt_less_than:
00171Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
00171Er 3               
00171Er 3  A0 00                        ldy #0          ; default false
001720r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr compare_16bit
001723r 3               
001723r 3                               ; for signed numbers, NOS < TOS if Z=0 and N=0
001723r 3  F0 03                        beq @false
001725r 3  30 01                        bmi @false
001727r 3               
001727r 3                               ; true
001727r 3  88                           dey
001728r 3               @false:
001728r 3  98                           tya
001729r 3               
001729r 3  E8                           inx
00172Ar 3  E8                           inx
00172Br 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
00172Dr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
00172Fr 3               
00172Fr 3  60           z_less_than:    rts
001730r 3               
001730r 3               
001730r 3               
001730r 3               ; ## LIST ( scr# -- ) "List the given screen"
001730r 3               ; ## "list"  tested  ANS block ext
001730r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/block/LIST"""
001730r 3               
001730r 3               xt_list:
001730r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
001733r 3               
001733r 3                               ; Save the screen number in SCR
001733r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_scr
001736r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_store
001739r 3               
001739r 3                               ; Use L from the editor-wordlist to display the screen.
001739r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_editor_l
00173Cr 3               
00173Cr 3  60           z_list:         rts
00173Dr 3               
00173Dr 3               
00173Dr 3               
00173Dr 3               ; ## LITERAL ( n -- ) "Store TOS to be push on stack during runtime"
00173Dr 3               ; ## "literal"  auto  ANS core
00173Dr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/LITERAL
00173Dr 3                       ; Compile-only word to store TOS so that it is pushed on stack
00173Dr 3                       ; during runtime. This is a immediate, compile-only word. At runtime,
00173Dr 3                       ; it works by calling literal_runtime by compling JSR LITERAL_RT.
00173Dr 3                       ;
00173Dr 3                       ; Note the cmpl_ routines use TMPTOS
00173Dr 3                       ; """
00173Dr 3               xt_literal:
00173Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
001740r 3               
001740r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>literal_runtime
001742r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<literal_runtime
001744r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
001747r 3               
001747r 3                               ; Compile the value that is to be pushed on the Stack during
001747r 3                               ; runtime
001747r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_comma
00174Ar 3               
00174Ar 3  60           z_literal:      rts
00174Br 3               
00174Br 3               literal_runtime:
00174Br 3               
00174Br 3                               ; During runtime, we push the value following this word back
00174Br 3                               ; on the Data Stack. The subroutine jump that brought us
00174Br 3                               ; here put the address to return to on the Return Stack -
00174Br 3                               ; this points to the data we need to get. This routine is
00174Br 3                               ; also called (LITERAL) in some Forths
00174Br 3  CA                           dex
00174Cr 3  CA                           dex
00174Dr 3               
00174Dr 3                           	; The 65c02 stores <RETURN-ADDRESS>-1 on the Return Stack,
00174Dr 3                               ; so we are actually popping the address-1 of the literal
00174Dr 3  68                           pla             ; LSB
00174Er 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001750r 3  68                           pla             ; MSB
001751r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001753r 3               
001753r 3                               ; Fetch the actual literal value and push it on Data stack
001753r 3  A0 01                        ldy #1
001755r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y    ; LSB
001757r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001759r 3  C8                           iny
00175Ar 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y    ; MSB
00175Cr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
00175Er 3               
00175Er 3                               ; Adjust return address and push back on the Return Stack
00175Er 3  98                           tya
00175Fr 3  18                           clc
001760r 3  65 rr                        adc tmp1
001762r 3  A8                           tay
001763r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
001765r 3  69 00                        adc #0
001767r 3  48                           pha
001768r 3  5A                           phy
001769r 3               
001769r 3  60                           rts
00176Ar 3               
00176Ar 3               
00176Ar 3               
00176Ar 3               ; ## LOAD ( scr# -- ) "Load the Forth code in a screen/block"
00176Ar 3               ; ## "load"  auto  ANS block
00176Ar 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/block/LOAD
00176Ar 3                       ;
00176Ar 3                       ; Note: LOAD current works because there is only one buffer.
00176Ar 3                       ; If/when multiple buffers are supported, we'll have to deal
00176Ar 3                       ; with the fact that it might re-load the old block into a
00176Ar 3                       ; different buffer.
00176Ar 3                       ; """
00176Ar 3               
00176Ar 3               xt_load:
00176Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
00176Dr 3               
00176Dr 3                               ; Save the current value of BLK on the return stack.
00176Dr 3  A0 01                        ldy #blk_offset+1
00176Fr 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
001771r 3  48                           pha
001772r 3  88                           dey
001773r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
001775r 3  48                           pha
001776r 3               
001776r 3                               ; Set BLK to the given block/screen number.
001776r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001778r 3  91 rr                        sta (up),y
00177Ar 3  C8                           iny
00177Br 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
00177Dr 3  91 rr                        sta (up),y
00177Fr 3               
00177Fr 3                               ; Load that block into a buffer
00177Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_block
001782r 3               
001782r 3                               ; Put 1024 on the stack for the screen length.
001782r 3  CA                           dex
001783r 3  CA                           dex
001784r 3  A9 04                        lda #4
001786r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001788r 3  74 00                        stz 0,x
00178Ar 3               
00178Ar 3                               ; Jump to a special evluate target. This bypasses the underflow
00178Ar 3                               ; check and skips the zeroing of BLK.
00178Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr load_evaluate
00178Dr 3               
00178Dr 3                               ; Restore the value of BLK from before the LOAD command.
00178Dr 3  A0 00                        ldy #blk_offset
00178Fr 3  68                           pla
001790r 3  91 rr                        sta (up),y
001792r 3  C8                           iny
001793r 3  68                           pla
001794r 3  91 rr                        sta (up),y
001796r 3               
001796r 3                               ; If BLK is not zero, read it back into the buffer.
001796r 3                               ; A still has MSB
001796r 3  88                           dey
001797r 3  11 rr                        ora (up),y
001799r 3  F0 12                        beq @done
00179Br 3               
00179Br 3                               ; The block needs to be read back into the buffer.
00179Br 3  CA                           dex
00179Cr 3  CA                           dex
00179Dr 3  A0 00                        ldy #blk_offset
00179Fr 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
0017A1r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0017A3r 3  C8                           iny
0017A4r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
0017A6r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0017A8r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_block
0017ABr 3               
0017ABr 3                               ; Drop the buffer address.
0017ABr 3  E8                           inx
0017ACr 3  E8                           inx
0017ADr 3               
0017ADr 3               @done:
0017ADr 3  60           z_load:         rts
0017AEr 3               
0017AEr 3               
0017AEr 3               
0017AEr 3               ; ## LOOP ( -- ) "Finish loop construct"
0017AEr 3               ; ## "loop"  auto  ANS core
0017AEr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/LOOP
0017AEr 3                       ; Compile-time part of LOOP. This does nothing more but push 1 on
0017AEr 3                       ; the stack and then call +LOOP.
0017AEr 3                       ;
0017AEr 3                       ; In Forth, this is
0017AEr 3                       ;       : LOOP  POSTPONE 1 POSTPONE (+LOOP) , POSTPONE UNLOOP ;
0017AEr 3                       ;       IMMEDIATE ; COMPILE-ONLY
0017AEr 3                       ; """
0017AEr 3               xt_loop:
0017AEr 3                               ; Have the finished word push 1 on the stack
0017AEr 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>xt_one
0017B0r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<xt_one
0017B2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine     ; drop through to +LOOP
0017B5r 3               
0017B5r 3               
0017B5r 3               ; ## PLUS_LOOP ( -- ) "Finish loop construct"
0017B5r 3               ; ## "+loop"  auto  ANS core
0017B5r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/PlusLOOP
0017B5r 3                       ;
0017B5r 3                       ; Compile-time part of +LOOP, also used for LOOP. Is usually
0017B5r 3                       ;       : +LOOP POSTPONE (+LOOP) , POSTPONE UNLOOP ; IMMEDIATE
0017B5r 3                       ;       COMPILE-ONLY
0017B5r 3                       ; in Forth. LOOP uses this routine as well. We jump here with the
0017B5r 3                       ; address for looping as TOS and the address for aborting the loop
0017B5r 3                       ; (LEAVE) as the second double-byte entry on the Return Stack (see
0017B5r 3                       ; DO and the Control Flow section of the manual for details).
0017B5r 3                       ; """
0017B5r 3               
0017B5r 3               xt_plus_loop:
0017B5r 3                               ; Compile the run-time part. We do this with a short loop
0017B5r 3                               ; and not a call to COMPILE, because it has to be natively
0017B5r 3                               ; coded anyway.
0017B5r 3  A0 11                        ldy #plus_loop_runtime_end-plus_loop_runtime
0017B7r 3  5A                           phy             ; save counter to adjust CP
0017B8r 3               @1:
0017B8r 3  B9 rr rr                     lda plus_loop_runtime,y
0017BBr 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
0017BDr 3  88                           dey
0017BEr 3  10 F8                        bpl @1
0017C0r 3               
0017C0r 3                               ; Adjust CP
0017C0r 3  68                           pla
0017C1r 3  18                           clc
0017C2r 3  65 rr                        adc cp
0017C4r 3  85 rr                        sta cp
0017C6r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
0017C8r 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; only need carry
0017CAr 3  85 rr                        sta cp+1
0017CCr 3               
0017CCr 3                               ; The address we need to loop back to is TOS. Store it so
0017CCr 3                               ; the runtime part of +LOOP jumps back up there
0017CCr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_comma
0017CFr 3               
0017CFr 3                               ; Compile an UNLOOP for when we're all done. This is a series
0017CFr 3                               ; of six PLA, so we just do it here instead jumping around
0017CFr 3                               ; all over the place
0017CFr 3  A9 68                        lda #$68                ; opcode for PLA
0017D1r 3  A0 06                        ldy #6
0017D3r 3               @2:
0017D3r 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
0017D5r 3  88                           dey
0017D6r 3  10 FB                        bpl @2
0017D8r 3               
0017D8r 3                               ; Adjust CP
0017D8r 3  A9 06                        lda #6
0017DAr 3  18                           clc
0017DBr 3  65 rr                        adc cp
0017DDr 3  85 rr                        sta cp
0017DFr 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
0017E1r 3  69 00                        adc #0                  ; only need carry
0017E3r 3  85 rr                        sta cp+1
0017E5r 3               
0017E5r 3                               ; Complete compile of DO/?DO by replacing the six
0017E5r 3                               ; dummy bytes by PHA instructions. The address where
0017E5r 3                               ; they are located is on the Data Stack
0017E5r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0017E7r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
0017E9r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
0017EBr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
0017EDr 3  E8                           inx
0017EEr 3  E8                           inx
0017EFr 3               
0017EFr 3                               ; Because of the way that CP works, we don't have to save
0017EFr 3                               ; CP, but CP-1
0017EFr 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
0017F1r 3  38                           sec
0017F2r 3  E9 01                        sbc #1
0017F4r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2
0017F6r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
0017F8r 3  E9 00                        sbc #0
0017FAr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1
0017FCr 3               
0017FCr 3                               ; now compile this in the DO/?DO routine
0017FCr 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
0017FEr 3               
0017FEr 3  A9 A9                        lda #$A9        ; opcode for LDA immediate
001800r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
001802r 3  C8                           iny
001803r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1      ; MSB
001805r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
001807r 3  C8                           iny
001808r 3  A9 48                        lda #$48        ; Opcode for PHA
00180Ar 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
00180Cr 3  C8                           iny
00180Dr 3               
00180Dr 3  A9 A9                        lda #$A9        ; opcode for LDA immediate
00180Fr 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
001811r 3  C8                           iny
001812r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2        ; LSB
001814r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
001816r 3  C8                           iny
001817r 3  A9 48                        lda #$48        ; Opcode for PHA
001819r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
00181Br 3               z_loop:
00181Br 3  60           z_plus_loop:    rts
00181Cr 3               
00181Cr 3               
00181Cr 3               plus_loop_runtime:
00181Cr 3                       ; """Runtime compile for loop control. This is used for both +LOOP and
00181Cr 3                       ; LOOP which are defined at high level. Note we use a fudge factor for
00181Cr 3                       ; loop control so we can test with the Overflow Flag. See
00181Cr 3                       ; the Control Flow section of the manual for details.
00181Cr 3                       ; The step value is TOS in the loop. This
00181Cr 3                       ; must always be native compiled. In some Forths, this is a separate
00181Cr 3                       ; word called (+LOOP) or (LOOP)
00181Cr 3                       ; """
00181Cr 3               
00181Cr 3  18                           clc
00181Dr 3  68                           pla             ; LSB of index
00181Er 3  75 00                        adc 0,x         ; LSB of step
001820r 3  A8                           tay             ; temporary storage of LSB
001821r 3               
001821r 3  B8                           clv
001822r 3  68                           pla             ; MSB of index
001823r 3  75 01                        adc 1,x         ; MSB of step
001825r 3  48                           pha             ; put MSB of index back on stack
001826r 3               
001826r 3  98                           tya             ; put LSB of index back on stack
001827r 3  48                           pha
001828r 3               
001828r 3  E8                           inx             ; dump step from TOS
001829r 3  E8                           inx
00182Ar 3               
00182Ar 3                               ; If V flag is set, we're done looping and continue
00182Ar 3                               ; after the +LOOP instruction
00182Ar 3  70 03                        bvs @hack+3     ; skip over JMP instruction
00182Cr 3               
00182Cr 3               @hack:          ; This is why this routine must be natively compiled: We
00182Cr 3                               ; compile the opcode for JMP here without an address to
00182Cr 3                               ; go to, which is added by the next next instruction of
00182Cr 3                               ; LOOP/+LOOP during compile time
00182Cr 3  4C                           .byte $4C
00182Dr 3               
00182Dr 3               plus_loop_runtime_end:
00182Dr 3               
00182Dr 3               
00182Dr 3               ; ## LSHIFT ( x u -- u ) "Shift TOS left"
00182Dr 3               ; ## "lshift"  auto  ANS core
00182Dr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/LSHIFT"""
00182Dr 3               
00182Dr 3               xt_lshift:
00182Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001830r 3               
001830r 3                               ; max shift 16 times
001830r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001832r 3  29 0F                        and #%00001111
001834r 3  F0 08                        beq @done
001836r 3               
001836r 3  A8                           tay
001837r 3               
001837r 3               @loop:
001837r 3  16 02                        asl 2,x
001839r 3  36 03                        rol 3,x
00183Br 3  88                           dey
00183Cr 3  D0 F9                        bne @loop
00183Er 3               
00183Er 3               @done:
00183Er 3  E8                           inx
00183Fr 3  E8                           inx
001840r 3               
001840r 3  60           z_lshift:       rts
001841r 3               
001841r 3               
001841r 3               
001841r 3               ; ## M_STAR ( n n -- d ) "16 * 16 --> 32"
001841r 3               ; ## "m*"  auto  ANS core
001841r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/MTimes
001841r 3                       ; Multiply two 16 bit numbers, producing a 32 bit result. All
001841r 3                       ; values are signed. Adapted from FIG Forth for Tali Forth.
001841r 3                       ;
001841r 3                       ; The original Forth is : M* OVER OVER XOR >R ABS SWAP ABS UM* R> D+- ;
001841r 3                       ; with  : D+- O< IF DNEGATE THEN ;
001841r 3                       ; """
001841r 3               
001841r 3               xt_m_star:
001841r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001844r 3               
001844r 3                               ; figure out the sign
001844r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB of n1
001846r 3  55 03                        eor 3,x         ; MSB of n2
001848r 3               
001848r 3                               ; UM* uses all kinds of temporary variables so we don't
001848r 3                               ; risk a conflict but just take the cycle hit and push
001848r 3                               ; this to the stack
001848r 3  48                           pha
001849r 3               
001849r 3                               ; get the absolute value of both numbers so we can feed
001849r 3                               ; them to UM*, which does the real work
001849r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_abs
00184Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_swap
00184Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_abs
001852r 3               
001852r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_um_star          ; ( d )
001855r 3               
001855r 3                               ; handle the sign
001855r 3  68                           pla
001856r 3  10 03                        bpl @done
001858r 3               
001858r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dnegate
00185Br 3               @done:
00185Br 3  60           z_m_star:       rts
00185Cr 3               
00185Cr 3               
00185Cr 3               
00185Cr 3               ; ## MARKER ( "name" -- ) "Create a deletion boundry"
00185Cr 3               ; ## "marker"  auto  ANS core ext
00185Cr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/MARKER
00185Cr 3                       ; This word replaces FORGET in earlier Forths. Old entries are not
00185Cr 3                       ; actually deleted, but merely overwritten by restoring CP and DP.
00185Cr 3                       ; Run the named word at a later time to restore all of the wordlists
00185Cr 3                       ; to their state when the word was created with marker.  Any words
00185Cr 3                       ; created after the marker (including the marker) will be forgotten.
00185Cr 3                       ;
00185Cr 3                       ; To do this, we want to end up with something that jumps to a
00185Cr 3                       ; run-time component with a link to the original CP and DP values:
00185Cr 3                       ;
00185Cr 3                       ;       jsr marker_runtime
00185Cr 3                       ;       <Original CP MSB>
00185Cr 3                       ;       <Original CP LSB>
00185Cr 3                       ;       <Original DP MSB> ( for CURRENT wordlist )
00185Cr 3                       ;       <Original DP LSB>
00185Cr 3                       ;       < USER variables from offset 4 to 39 >
00185Cr 3                       ;
00185Cr 3                       ;       The user variables include:
00185Cr 3                       ;       CURRENT (byte variable)
00185Cr 3                       ;       <All wordlists> (currently 12) (cell array)
00185Cr 3                       ;       <#ORDER> (byte variable)
00185Cr 3                       ;       <All search order> (currently 9) (byte array)
00185Cr 3                       ;
00185Cr 3                       ; This code uses tmp1 and tmp2
00185Cr 3                       ; """
00185Cr 3               
00185Cr 3               xt_marker:
00185Cr 3                               ; Before we do anything, we need to save CP, which
00185Cr 3                               ; after all is the whole point of this operation. CREATE
00185Cr 3                               ; uses tmp1 and tmp2, so we take the speed hit and push stuff
00185Cr 3                               ; to the stack
00185Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr current_to_dp
00185Fr 3               
00185Fr 3  A5 rr                        lda dp
001861r 3  48                           pha
001862r 3  A5 rr                        lda dp+1
001864r 3  48                           pha
001865r 3               
001865r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
001867r 3  48                           pha
001868r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
00186Ar 3  48                           pha
00186Br 3               
00186Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_create
00186Er 3               
00186Er 3                               ; By default, CREATE installs a subroutine jump to DOVAR, which
00186Er 3                               ; we have to replace by a jump to marker_runtime. We back up
00186Er 3                               ; two bytes and then overwrite the address
00186Er 3  A5 rr                        lda cp          ; LSB
001870r 3  38                           sec
001871r 3  E9 02                        sbc #2
001873r 3  85 rr                        sta cp
001875r 3               
001875r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1        ; MSB
001877r 3  E9 00                        sbc #0          ; we only care about the borrow
001879r 3  85 rr                        sta cp+1
00187Br 3               
00187Br 3                               ; Add the address of the runtime component
00187Br 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>marker_runtime
00187Dr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<marker_runtime
00187Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_word
001882r 3               
001882r 3                               ; Add original CP as payload
001882r 3  7A                           ply                     ; MSB
001883r 3  68                           pla                     ; LSB
001884r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_word
001887r 3               
001887r 3                               ; Add original DP as payload
001887r 3  7A                           ply                     ; MSB
001888r 3  68                           pla                     ; LSB
001889r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_word
00188Cr 3               
00188Cr 3                               ; Add the user variables for the wordlists and search order.
00188Cr 3                               ; We're compiling them in byte order.
00188Cr 3  A0 04                        ldy #4                  ; Start at CURRENT
00188Er 3               @marker_loop:
00188Er 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
001890r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_a
001893r 3  C8                           iny
001894r 3  98                           tya
001895r 3  C9 28                        cmp #40                 ; One past the end of the search order.
001897r 3  D0 F5                        bne @marker_loop
001899r 3               
001899r 3  60           z_marker:       rts
00189Ar 3               
00189Ar 3               
00189Ar 3               
00189Ar 3               marker_runtime:
00189Ar 3                       ; """Restore Dictionary and memory (DP and CP) to where the were
00189Ar 3                       ; when this marker was defined. We arrive here with the return
00189Ar 3                       ; address on the Return Stack in the usual 65c02 format
00189Ar 3                       ; """
00189Ar 3               
00189Ar 3                               ; Get the address of the string address off the stack and
00189Ar 3                               ; increase by one because of the RTS mechanics
00189Ar 3  68                           pla
00189Br 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1        ; LSB of address
00189Dr 3  68                           pla
00189Er 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1      ; MSB of address
0018A0r 3               
0018A0r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1
0018A2r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
0018A4r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1+1
0018A6r 3               @1:
0018A6r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
0018A8r 3               
0018A8r 3                               ; CP was stored first
0018A8r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
0018AAr 3  85 rr                        sta cp
0018ACr 3  C8                           iny
0018ADr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
0018AFr 3  85 rr                        sta cp+1
0018B1r 3               
0018B1r 3                               ; Next was DP
0018B1r 3  C8                           iny
0018B2r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
0018B4r 3  85 rr                        sta dp
0018B6r 3  C8                           iny
0018B7r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
0018B9r 3  85 rr                        sta dp+1
0018BBr 3               
0018BBr 3                               ; Conveniently, the offset into both tmp1 and UP is 4
0018BBr 3                               ; to start restoring the wordlists and search order.
0018BBr 3  A0 04                        ldy #4
0018BDr 3               
0018BDr 3               @marker_restore_loop:
0018BDr 3                               ; Copy from the dictionary back on top of the wordlists
0018BDr 3                               ; and search order.
0018BDr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1), y
0018BFr 3  91 rr                        sta (up), y
0018C1r 3  C8                           iny
0018C2r 3  98                           tya
0018C3r 3  C9 28                        cmp #40                 ; One past the end of the search order.
0018C5r 3  D0 F6                        bne @marker_restore_loop
0018C7r 3               
0018C7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr dp_to_current       ; Move the CURRENT DP back.
0018CAr 3               
0018CAr 3                               ; The return instruction takes us back to the original caller
0018CAr 3  60                           rts
0018CBr 3               
0018CBr 3               
0018CBr 3               
0018CBr 3               ; ## MAX ( n n -- n ) "Keep larger of two numbers"
0018CBr 3               ; ## "max"  auto  ANS core
0018CBr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/MAX
0018CBr 3                       ; Compare TOS and NOS and keep which one is larger. Adapted from
0018CBr 3                       ; Lance A. Leventhal "6502 Assembly Language Subroutines". Negative
0018CBr 3                       ; Flag indicates which number is larger. See also
0018CBr 3                       ; http://6502.org/tutorials/compare_instructions.html and
0018CBr 3                       ; http://www.righto.com/2012/12/the-6502-overflow-flag-explained.html
0018CBr 3                       ; """
0018CBr 3               
0018CBr 3               xt_max:
0018CBr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
0018CEr 3               
0018CEr 3                               ; Compare LSB. We do this first to set the carry flag
0018CEr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB of TOS
0018D0r 3  D5 02                        cmp 2,x         ; LSB of NOS, this sets the carry
0018D2r 3               
0018D2r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB of TOS
0018D4r 3  F5 03                        sbc 3,x         ; MSB of NOS
0018D6r 3  50 02                        bvc @no_overflow
0018D8r 3               
0018D8r 3                               ; handle overflow, because we use signed numbers
0018D8r 3  49 80                        eor #$80        ; complement negative flag
0018DAr 3               
0018DAr 3               @no_overflow:
0018DAr 3                               ; if negative, NOS is larger and needs to be kept
0018DAr 3  30 08                        bmi @keep_nos
0018DCr 3               
0018DCr 3                               ; move TOS to NOS
0018DCr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0018DEr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
0018E0r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
0018E2r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
0018E4r 3               
0018E4r 3               @keep_nos:
0018E4r 3  E8                           inx
0018E5r 3  E8                           inx
0018E6r 3               
0018E6r 3  60           z_max:          rts
0018E7r 3               
0018E7r 3               
0018E7r 3               
0018E7r 3               ; ## MIN ( n n -- n ) "Keep smaller of two numbers"
0018E7r 3               ; ## "min"  auto  ANS core
0018E7r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/MIN
0018E7r 3                       ; Adapted from Lance A. Leventhal "6502 Assembly Language
0018E7r 3                       ; Subroutines." Negative Flag indicateds which number is larger. See
0018E7r 3                       ; http://www.righto.com/2012/12/the-6502-overflow-flag-explained.html
0018E7r 3                       ; """
0018E7r 3               
0018E7r 3               xt_min:
0018E7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
0018EAr 3               
0018EAr 3                               ; compare LSB. We do this first to set the carry flag
0018EAr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB of TOS
0018ECr 3  D5 02                        cmp 2,x         ; LSB of NOS, this sets carry
0018EEr 3               
0018EEr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB of TOS
0018F0r 3  F5 03                        sbc 3,x         ; MSB of NOS
0018F2r 3  50 02                        bvc @no_overflow
0018F4r 3               
0018F4r 3                               ; handle overflow because we use signed numbers
0018F4r 3  49 80                        eor #$80
0018F6r 3               
0018F6r 3               @no_overflow:
0018F6r 3                               ; if negative, NOS is larger and needs to be dumped
0018F6r 3  10 08                        bpl @keep_nos
0018F8r 3               
0018F8r 3                               ; move TOS to NOS
0018F8r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0018FAr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
0018FCr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
0018FEr 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001900r 3               
001900r 3               @keep_nos:
001900r 3  E8                           inx
001901r 3  E8                           inx
001902r 3               
001902r 3  60           z_min:          rts
001903r 3               
001903r 3               
001903r 3               
001903r 3               ; ## MINUS ( n n -- n ) "Subtract TOS from NOS"
001903r 3               ; ## "-"  auto  ANS core
001903r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Minus"""
001903r 3               xt_minus:
001903r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001906r 3               
001906r 3  38                           sec
001907r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; LSB
001909r 3  F5 00                        sbc 0,x
00190Br 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
00190Dr 3               
00190Dr 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x         ; MSB
00190Fr 3  F5 01                        sbc 1,x
001911r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001913r 3               
001913r 3  E8                           inx
001914r 3  E8                           inx
001915r 3               
001915r 3  60           z_minus:        rts
001916r 3               
001916r 3               
001916r 3               ; ## MINUS_LEADING ( addr1 u1 -- addr2 u2 ) "Remove leading spaces"
001916r 3               ; ## "-leading"  auto  Tali String
001916r 3                       ; """Remove leading whitespace. This is the reverse of -TRAILING
001916r 3                       ; """
001916r 3               
001916r 3               xt_minus_leading:
001916r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001919r 3               
001919r 3               @loop:
001919r 3                               ; Quit if we were given an empty string. This also terminates
001919r 3                               ; the main loop
001919r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
00191Br 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
00191Dr 3  F0 0F                        beq @done
00191Fr 3               
00191Fr 3  A1 02                        lda (2,x)               ; get first character
001921r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr is_whitespace
001924r 3  90 08                        bcc @done
001926r 3               
001926r 3                               ; It's whitespace, move one down
001926r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_one              ; ( addr u 1 )
001929r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_slash_string     ; ( addr+ u-1 )
00192Cr 3               
00192Cr 3  80 EB                        bra @loop
00192Er 3               @done:
00192Er 3               z_minus_leading:
00192Er 3  60                           rts
00192Fr 3               
00192Fr 3               
00192Fr 3               
00192Fr 3               ; ## MINUS_TRAILING ( addr u1 -- addr u2 ) "Remove trailing spaces"
00192Fr 3               ; ## "-trailing"  auto  ANS string
00192Fr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/string/MinusTRAILING
00192Fr 3                       ; Remove trailing spaces
00192Fr 3                       ; """
00192Fr 3               
00192Fr 3               xt_minus_trailing:
00192Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001932r 3               
001932r 3                               ; if length entry is zero, return a zero and leave the
001932r 3                               ; address part untouched
001932r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB of n
001934r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x         ; MSB of n
001936r 3  F0 33                        beq @done
001938r 3               
001938r 3                               ; Compute address of last char in tmp1 as
001938r 3                               ; addr + u1 - 1
001938r 3               
001938r 3                               ; addr + u1
001938r 3  18                           clc
001939r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; LSB of addr
00193Br 3  75 00                        adc 0,x
00193Dr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
00193Fr 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x         ; MSB of addr
001941r 3  75 01                        adc 1,x
001943r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001945r 3               
001945r 3                               ; - 1
001945r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
001947r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
001949r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1+1
00194Br 3               @1:
00194Br 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1
00194Dr 3               
00194Dr 3               @loop:
00194Dr 3                               ; While spaces are found, move tmp1 backwards and
00194Dr 3                               ; decrease the count on the data stack.
00194Dr 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp1)
00194Fr 3  C9 20                        cmp #AscSP
001951r 3  D0 18                        bne @done
001953r 3               
001953r 3                               ; Move back one address.
001953r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
001955r 3  D0 02                        bne @2
001957r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1+1
001959r 3               @2:
001959r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1
00195Br 3               
00195Br 3                               ; Decrement count by one.
00195Br 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
00195Dr 3  D0 02                        bne @3
00195Fr 3  D6 01                        dec 1,x
001961r 3               @3:
001961r 3  D6 00                        dec 0,x
001963r 3               
001963r 3                               ; Check if there are any characters left.
001963r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001965r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
001967r 3  F0 02                        beq @done       ; Count has reached zero - we're done!
001969r 3               
001969r 3  80 E2                        bra @loop
00196Br 3               
00196Br 3               @done:
00196Br 3               z_minus_trailing:
00196Br 3  60                           rts
00196Cr 3               
00196Cr 3               
00196Cr 3               
00196Cr 3               ; ## MOD ( n1 n2 -- n ) "Divide NOS by TOS and return the remainder"
00196Cr 3               ; ## "mod"  auto  ANS core
00196Cr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/MOD
00196Cr 3                       ;
00196Cr 3                       ; The Forth definition of this word is  : MOD /MOD DROP ;
00196Cr 3                       ; so we just jump to xt_slash_mod and dump the actual result.
00196Cr 3                       ; """
00196Cr 3               xt_mod:
00196Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
00196Fr 3               
00196Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_slash_mod
001972r 3               
001972r 3  E8                           inx             ; DROP
001973r 3  E8                           inx
001974r 3               z_mod:
001974r 3  60                           rts
001975r 3               
001975r 3               
001975r 3               ; ## MOVE ( addr1 addr2 u -- ) "Copy bytes"
001975r 3               ; ## "move"  auto  ANS core
001975r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/MOVE
001975r 3                       ; Copy u "address units" from addr1 to addr2. Since our address
001975r 3                       ; units are bytes, this is just a front-end for CMOVE and CMOVE>. This
001975r 3                       ; is actually the only one of these three words that is in the CORE
001975r 3                       ; set.
001975r 3                       ;
001975r 3                       ; This word must not be natively compiled.
001975r 3                       ; """
001975r 3               
001975r 3               xt_move:
001975r 3                               ; We let CMOVE and CMOVE> check if there is underflow or
001975r 3                               ; we've been told to copy zero bytes
001975r 3               
001975r 3                               ; compare MSB first
001975r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x                 ; MSB of addr2
001977r 3  D5 05                        cmp 5,x                 ; MSB of addr1
001979r 3  F0 05                        beq @lsb                ; wasn't helpful, move to LSB
00197Br 3  B0 0E                        bcs @to_move_up         ; we want CMOVE>
00197Dr 3               
00197Dr 3  4C rr rr                     jmp xt_cmove            ; JSR/RTS
001980r 3               
001980r 3               @lsb:
001980r 3                               ; MSB were equal, so do the whole thing over with LSB
001980r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x                 ; LSB of addr2
001982r 3  D5 04                        cmp 4,x                 ; LSB of addr1
001984r 3  F0 08                        beq @equal              ; LSB is equal as well
001986r 3  B0 03                        bcs @to_move_up         ; we want CMOVE>
001988r 3               
001988r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp xt_cmove            ; JSR/RTS
00198Br 3               
00198Br 3               @to_move_up:
00198Br 3  4C rr rr                     jmp xt_cmove_up         ; JSR/RTS
00198Er 3               @equal:
00198Er 3                               ; drop three entries from Data Stack
00198Er 3  8A                           txa
00198Fr 3  18                           clc
001990r 3  69 06                        adc #6
001992r 3  AA                           tax
001993r 3               
001993r 3  60           z_move:         rts
001994r 3               
001994r 3               
001994r 3               
001994r 3               ; ## NAME_TO_INT ( nt -- xt ) "Convert Name Token to Execute Token"
001994r 3               ; ## "name>int"  tested  Gforth
001994r 3                       ; """See
001994r 3                       ; https://www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Name-token.html
001994r 3                       ; """
001994r 3               
001994r 3               xt_name_to_int:
001994r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
001997r 3               
001997r 3                               ; The xt starts four bytes down from the nt
001997r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001999r 3  18                           clc
00199Ar 3  69 04                        adc #4
00199Cr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3
00199Er 3               
00199Er 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
0019A0r 3  90 01                        bcc @done
0019A2r 3  1A                           inc
0019A3r 3               @done:
0019A3r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3+1
0019A5r 3               
0019A5r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
0019A7r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp3),y
0019A9r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0019ABr 3  C8                           iny
0019ACr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp3),y
0019AEr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0019B0r 3               
0019B0r 3  60           z_name_to_int:  rts
0019B1r 3               
0019B1r 3               
0019B1r 3               
0019B1r 3               ; ## NAME_TO_STRING ( nt -- addr u ) "Given a name token, return string of word"
0019B1r 3               ; ## "name>string"  tested  Gforth
0019B1r 3                       ; """http://www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Name-token.html"""
0019B1r 3               
0019B1r 3               xt_name_to_string:
0019B1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
0019B4r 3               
0019B4r 3  CA                           dex
0019B5r 3  CA                           dex
0019B6r 3               
0019B6r 3                               ; the length of the string is the first byte of the
0019B6r 3                               ; header pointed to by nt
0019B6r 3  A1 02                        lda (2,x)
0019B8r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0019BAr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
0019BCr 3               
0019BCr 3                               ; the string itself always starts eight bytes down
0019BCr 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; LSB
0019BEr 3  18                           clc
0019BFr 3  69 08                        adc #8
0019C1r 3  A8                           tay
0019C2r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x         ; MSB
0019C4r 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; just need carry
