0019C6r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
0019C8r 3  94 02                        sty 2,x
0019CAr 3               
0019CAr 3               z_name_to_string:
0019CAr 3  60                           rts
0019CBr 3               
0019CBr 3               
0019CBr 3               ; ## NC_LIMIT ( -- addr ) "Return address where NC-LIMIT value is kept"
0019CBr 3               ; ## "nc-limit"  tested  Tali Forth
0019CBr 3               
0019CBr 3               xt_nc_limit:
0019CBr 3  CA                           dex
0019CCr 3  CA                           dex
0019CDr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<nc_limit
0019CFr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0019D1r 3  A9 rr                        lda #>nc_limit
0019D3r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0019D5r 3               
0019D5r 3  60           z_nc_limit:     rts
0019D6r 3               
0019D6r 3               
0019D6r 3               
0019D6r 3               ; ## NEGATE ( n -- n ) "Two's complement"
0019D6r 3               ; ## "negate"  auto  ANS core
0019D6r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/NEGATE"""
0019D6r 3               xt_negate:
0019D6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
0019D9r 3               
0019D9r 3  A9 00                	lda #0
0019DBr 3  38                           sec
0019DCr 3  F5 00                        sbc 0,x         ; LSB
0019DEr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0019E0r 3               
0019E0r 3  A9 00                        lda #0
0019E2r 3  F5 01                        sbc 1,x         ; MSB
0019E4r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0019E6r 3               
0019E6r 3  60           z_negate:       rts
0019E7r 3               
0019E7r 3               
0019E7r 3               ; ## NEVER_NATIVE ( -- ) "Flag last word as never natively compiled"
0019E7r 3               ; ## "never-native"  auto  Tali Forth
0019E7r 3               xt_never_native:
0019E7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr current_to_dp
0019EAr 3  A0 01                        ldy #1          ; offset for status byte
0019ECr 3  B1 rr                        lda (dp),y
0019EEr 3  09 08                        ora #NN         ; Make sure NN flag is set
0019F0r 3  29 FD                        and #$ff-AN     ; and AN flag is clear.
0019F2r 3  91 rr                        sta (dp),y
0019F4r 3               z_never_native:
0019F4r 3  60                           rts
0019F5r 3               
0019F5r 3               
0019F5r 3               ; ## NIP ( b a -- a ) "Delete NOS"
0019F5r 3               ; ## "nip"  auto  ANS core ext
0019F5r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/NIP"""
0019F5r 3               xt_nip:
0019F5r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
0019F8r 3               
0019F8r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB
0019FAr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
0019FCr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB
0019FEr 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001A00r 3               
001A00r 3  E8                           inx
001A01r 3  E8                           inx
001A02r 3               
001A02r 3  60           z_nip:          rts
001A03r 3               
001A03r 3               
001A03r 3               ; ## NOT_EQUALS ( n m -- f ) "Return a true flag if TOS != NOS"
001A03r 3               ; ## "<>"  auto  ANS core ext
001A03r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/ne
001A03r 3                       ;
001A03r 3                       ; This is just a variant of EQUAL, we code it separately
001A03r 3                       ; for speed.
001A03r 3                       ; """
001A03r 3               
001A03r 3               xt_not_equals:
001A03r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001A06r 3               
001A06r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0                  ; default is true
001A08r 3               
001A08r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x                 ; LSB
001A0Ar 3  D5 02                        cmp 2,x
001A0Cr 3  D0 0A                        bne @not_equal
001A0Er 3               
001A0Er 3                               ; LSB is equal
001A0Er 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x                 ; MSB
001A10r 3  D5 03                        cmp 3,x
001A12r 3  D0 04                        bne @not_equal
001A14r 3               
001A14r 3  A9 FF                        lda #$FF
001A16r 3  80 01                        bra @done
001A18r 3               
001A18r 3               @not_equal:
001A18r 3  88                           dey                     ; drop thru to done
001A19r 3               
001A19r 3               @done:
001A19r 3  98                           tya
001A1Ar 3  E8                           inx
001A1Br 3  E8                           inx
001A1Cr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001A1Er 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001A20r 3               
001A20r 3  60           z_not_equals:   rts
001A21r 3               
001A21r 3               
001A21r 3               
001A21r 3               ; ## NOT_ROTE ( a b c -- c a b ) "Rotate upwards"
001A21r 3               ; ## "-rot"  auto  Gforth
001A21r 3                       ; """http://www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Data-stack.html"""
001A21r 3               
001A21r 3               xt_not_rote:
001A21r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_3
001A24r 3               
001A24r 3  B4 01                        ldy 1,x         ; MSB first
001A26r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
001A28r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001A2Ar 3               
001A2Ar 3  B5 05                        lda 5,x
001A2Cr 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001A2Er 3  94 05                        sty 5,x
001A30r 3               
001A30r 3  B4 00                        ldy 0,x         ; LSB second
001A32r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
001A34r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001A36r 3               
001A36r 3  B5 04                        lda 4,x
001A38r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001A3Ar 3  94 04                        sty 4,x
001A3Cr 3               
001A3Cr 3  60           z_not_rote:     rts
001A3Dr 3               
001A3Dr 3               
001A3Dr 3               
001A3Dr 3               ; ## NUMBER ( addr u -- u | d ) "Convert a number string"
001A3Dr 3               ; ## "number"  auto  Tali Forth
001A3Dr 3                       ; """Convert a number string to a double or single cell number. This
001A3Dr 3                       ; is a wrapper for >NUMBER and follows the convention set out in the
001A3Dr 3                       ; "Forth Programmer's Handbook" (Conklin & Rather) 3rd edition p. 87.
001A3Dr 3                       ; Based in part on the "Starting Forth" code
001A3Dr 3                       ; https://www.forth.com/starting-forth/10-input-output-operators/
001A3Dr 3                       ; Gforth uses S>NUMBER? and S>UNUMBER? which return numbers and a flag
001A3Dr 3                       ; https://www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Number-Conversion.html
001A3Dr 3                       ; Another difference to Gforth is that we follow ANS Forth that the
001A3Dr 3                       ; dot to signal a double cell number is required to be the last
001A3Dr 3                       ; character of the string.
001A3Dr 3                       ;
001A3Dr 3                       ; Number calls >NUMBER which in turn calls UM*,
001A3Dr 3                       ; which uses tmp1, tmp2, and tmp3, so we can't use them here, which is
001A3Dr 3                       ; a pain.
001A3Dr 3                       ;"""
001A3Dr 3               
001A3Dr 3               xt_number:
001A3Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001A40r 3               
001A40r 3                               ; we keep the flags for sign and double in tmpdsp because
001A40r 3                               ; we've run out of temporary variables
001A40r 3  64 rr                        stz tmpdsp      ; flag for double
001A42r 3  64 rr                        stz tmpdsp+1    ; flag for minus
001A44r 3               
001A44r 3                               ; If the first character is a minus, strip it off and set
001A44r 3                               ; the flag
001A44r 3  A1 02                        lda (2,x)
001A46r 3  C9 2D                        cmp #$2D        ; ASCII for "-"
001A48r 3  D0 0A                        bne @check_dot
001A4Ar 3               
001A4Ar 3                               ; It's a minus
001A4Ar 3  C6 rr                        dec tmpdsp+1
001A4Cr 3  F6 02                        inc 2,x         ; start one character later
001A4Er 3  D0 02                        bne @1
001A50r 3  F6 03                        inc 3,x
001A52r 3               @1:
001A52r 3  D6 00                        dec 0,x         ; decrease string length by one
001A54r 3               
001A54r 3               @check_dot:
001A54r 3                               ; If the last character is a dot, strip it off and set a
001A54r 3                               ; flag. We can use tmptos as a temporary variable
001A54r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; LSB of address
001A56r 3  18                           clc
001A57r 3  75 00                        adc 0,x         ; length of string
001A59r 3  85 rr                        sta tmptos
001A5Br 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
001A5Dr 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; only need carry
001A5Fr 3  85 rr                        sta tmptos+1
001A61r 3               
001A61r 3                               ; tmptos now points to the first character after the string,
001A61r 3                               ; but we need the last character
001A61r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmptos
001A63r 3  D0 02                        bne @2
001A65r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmptos+1
001A67r 3               @2:
001A67r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmptos
001A69r 3               
001A69r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmptos)
001A6Br 3  C9 2E                        cmp #'.'
001A6Dr 3  D0 04                        bne @main
001A6Fr 3               
001A6Fr 3                               ; We have a dot, which means this is a double number. Flag
001A6Fr 3                               ; the fact and reduce string length by one
001A6Fr 3  C6 rr                        dec tmpdsp
001A71r 3  D6 00                        dec 0,x
001A73r 3               
001A73r 3               @main:
001A73r 3                               ; Set up stack for subroutine jump to >NUMBER, which means
001A73r 3                               ; we have to go ( addr u --> ud addr u )
001A73r 3  CA                           dex
001A74r 3  CA                           dex
001A75r 3  CA                           dex
001A76r 3  CA                           dex
001A77r 3               
001A77r 3  B5 04                        lda 4,x         ; LSB of length
001A79r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001A7Br 3  74 01                        stz 1,x         ; MSB, max length 255 chars
001A7Dr 3               
001A7Dr 3  B5 06                        lda 6,x         ; LSB of address
001A7Fr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001A81r 3  B5 07                        lda 7,x         ; MSB of address
001A83r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001A85r 3               
001A85r 3  74 04                        stz 4,x         ; clear space for ud
001A87r 3  74 05                        stz 5,x
001A89r 3  74 06                        stz 6,x
001A8Br 3  74 07                        stz 7,x
001A8Dr 3               
001A8Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_number        ; (ud addr u -- ud addr u )
001A90r 3               
001A90r 3                               ; test length of returned string, which should be zero
001A90r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001A92r 3  F0 15                        beq @all_converted
001A94r 3               
001A94r 3                               ; Something went wrong, we still have characters left over,
001A94r 3                               ; so we print an error and abort. If the NUMBER was called
001A94r 3                               ; by INTERPRET, we've already checked for Forth words, so
001A94r 3                               ; we're in deep trouble one way or another
001A94r 3  A9 3E                        lda #$3E        ; ASCII for ">"
001A96r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001A99r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
001A9Cr 3  A9 3C                        lda #$3C        ; ASCII for "<"
001A9Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001AA1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
001AA4r 3               
001AA4r 3  A9 08                        lda #err_syntax
001AA6r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp error
001AA9r 3               
001AA9r 3               @all_converted:
001AA9r 3                               ; We can drop the string info
001AA9r 3  E8                           inx
001AAAr 3  E8                           inx
001AABr 3  E8                           inx
001AACr 3  E8                           inx
001AADr 3               
001AADr 3                               ; We have a double-cell number on the Data Stack that might
001AADr 3                               ; actually have a minus and might actually be single-cell
001AADr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmpdsp      ; flag for double
001AAFr 3  F0 0D                        beq @single
001AB1r 3               
001AB1r 3                               ; Set status bit 5 to indicate this is a double number
001AB1r 3  A9 20                        lda #%00100000
001AB3r 3  04 rr                        tsb status
001AB5r 3               
001AB5r 3                               ; This is a double cell number. If it had a minus, we'll have
001AB5r 3                               ; to negate it
001AB5r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmpdsp+1
001AB7r 3  F0 12                        beq @done       ; no minus, all done
001AB9r 3               
001AB9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dnegate
001ABCr 3               
001ABCr 3  80 0D                        bra @done
001ABEr 3               
001ABEr 3               @single:
001ABEr 3                               ; This is a single number, so we just drop the top cell
001ABEr 3  E8                           inx
001ABFr 3  E8                           inx
001AC0r 3               
001AC0r 3                               ; Clear status bit 5 to indicate this is a single number
001AC0r 3  A9 20                        lda #%00100000
001AC2r 3  14 rr                        trb status
001AC4r 3               
001AC4r 3                               ; If we had a minus, we'll have to negate it
001AC4r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmpdsp+1
001AC6r 3  F0 03                        beq @done       ; no minus, all done
001AC8r 3               
001AC8r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_negate
001ACBr 3               @done:
001ACBr 3  60           z_number:       rts
001ACCr 3               
001ACCr 3               
001ACCr 3               
001ACCr 3               ; ## NUMBER_SIGN ( ud -- ud ) "Add character to pictured output string"
001ACCr 3               ; ## "#"  auto  ANS core
001ACCr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/num
001ACCr 3                       ; Add one char to the beginning of the pictured output string.
001ACCr 3                       ;
001ACCr 3                       ; Based on
001ACCr 3                       ; https://github.com/philburk/pforth/blob/master/fth/numberio.fth
001ACCr 3                       ; Forth code  BASE @ UD/MOD ROT 9 OVER < IF 7 + THEN [CHAR] 0 + HOLD ;
001ACCr 3                       ; """
001ACCr 3               xt_number_sign:
001ACCr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2         ; double number
001ACFr 3               
001ACFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_base
001AD2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_fetch            ; ( ud1 base )
001AD5r 3               
001AD5r 3                               ; The following code is the ancient Forth word UD/MOD, which in
001AD5r 3                               ; various Forths (including Gforth) lives on under the hood,
001AD5r 3                               ; even though it's not an ANS standard word, it doesn't appear
001AD5r 3                               ; in the docs, it's only used here, and there are no tests for
001AD5r 3                               ; it. This is why we got rid of it. We'll be converting this
001AD5r 3                               ; mess to something more sane in the long run.
001AD5r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_r             ; >r
001AD8r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero             ; 0
001ADBr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_fetch          ; r@
001ADEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_um_slash_mod     ; um/mod
001AE1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_rot              ; rot
001AE4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_rot              ; rot
001AE7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_from           ; r>
001AEAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_um_slash_mod     ; um/mod
001AEDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_rot              ; rot
001AF0r 3                               ; end of UD/MOD ( rem ud )
001AF0r 3               
001AF0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_rot              ; ( ud rem )
001AF3r 3               
001AF3r 3                               ; Convert the number that is left over to an ASCII character. We
001AF3r 3                               ; use a string lookup for speed. Use either abc_str_lower for
001AF3r 3                               ; lower case or abc_str_upper for upper case (prefered)
001AF3r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001AF5r 3  A8                           tay
001AF6r 3  B9 rr rr                     lda s_abc_upper,y
001AF9r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001AFBr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x                 ; paranoid; now ( ud char )
001AFDr 3               
001AFDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_hold
001B00r 3               
001B00r 3               z_number_sign:
001B00r 3  60                           rts
001B01r 3               
001B01r 3               
001B01r 3               ; ## NUMBER_SIGN_GREATER ( d -- addr u ) "Finish pictured number conversion"
001B01r 3               ; ## "#>"  auto  ANS core
001B01r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/num-end
001B01r 3                       ; Finish conversion of pictured number string, putting address and
001B01r 3                       ; length on the Data Stack.
001B01r 3                       ;
001B01r 3                       ; Original Fort is  2DROP HLD @ PAD OVER -
001B01r 3                       ; Based on
001B01r 3                       ; https://github.com/philburk/pforth/blob/master/fth/numberio.fth
001B01r 3                       ; """
001B01r 3               xt_number_sign_greater:
001B01r 3               
001B01r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2         ; double number
001B04r 3               
001B04r 3                               ; The start address lives in tohold
001B04r 3  A5 rr                        lda tohold
001B06r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x         ; LSB of tohold
001B08r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001B0Ar 3  A5 rr                        lda tohold+1
001B0Cr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x         ; MSB of addr
001B0Er 3  95 03                        sta 3,x         ; ( addr addr )
001B10r 3               
001B10r 3                               ; The length of the string is pad - addr
001B10r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_pad      ; ( addr addr pad )
001B13r 3               
001B13r 3  38                           sec
001B14r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB of pad address
001B16r 3  F5 02                        sbc 2,x
001B18r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001B1Ar 3               
001B1Ar 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB, which should always be zero
001B1Cr 3  F5 03                        sbc 3,x
001B1Er 3  95 03                        sta 3,x         ; ( addr u pad )
001B20r 3               
001B20r 3  E8                           inx
001B21r 3  E8                           inx
001B22r 3               
001B22r 3               z_number_sign_greater:
001B22r 3  60                           rts
001B23r 3               
001B23r 3               
001B23r 3               ; ## NUMBER_SIGN_S ( d -- addr u ) "Completely convert pictured output"
001B23r 3               ; ## "#s"  auto  ANS core
001B23r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/numS
001B23r 3                       ; Completely convert number for pictured numerical output.
001B23r 3                       ;
001B23r 3                       ; Based on
001B23r 3                       ; https://github.com/philburk/pforth/blob/master/fth/system.fth
001B23r 3                       ; Original Forth code  BEGIN # 2DUP OR 0= UNTIL
001B23r 3                       ; """
001B23r 3               
001B23r 3               xt_number_sign_s:
001B23r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001B26r 3               @loop:
001B26r 3                               ; convert a single number ("#")
001B26r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign
001B29r 3               
001B29r 3                               ; stop when double-celled number in TOS is zero:
001B29r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001B2Br 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
001B2Dr 3  15 02                        ora 2,x
001B2Fr 3  15 03                        ora 3,x
001B31r 3  D0 F3                        bne @loop
001B33r 3               
001B33r 3               z_number_sign_s:
001B33r 3  60                           rts
001B34r 3               
001B34r 3               
001B34r 3               
001B34r 3               ; ## OF (C: -- of-sys) (x1 x2 -- |x1) "Conditional flow control"
001B34r 3               ; ## "of"  auto  ANS core ext
001B34r 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/OF"""
001B34r 3               
001B34r 3               xt_of:
001B34r 3                               ; Check if value is equal to this case.
001B34r 3                               ; Postpone over (eg. compile a jsr to it)
001B34r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>xt_over
001B36r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<xt_over
001B38r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
001B3Br 3               
001B3Br 3                               ; Postpone = (EQUAL), that is, compile a jsr to it
001B3Br 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>xt_equal
001B3Dr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<xt_equal
001B3Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
001B42r 3               
001B42r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_if
001B45r 3               
001B45r 3                               ; If it's true, consume the original value.
001B45r 3                               ; Postpone DROP (eg. compile a jsr to it)
001B45r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>xt_drop
001B47r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<xt_drop
001B49r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
001B4Cr 3               
001B4Cr 3  60           z_of:           rts
001B4Dr 3               
001B4Dr 3               
001B4Dr 3               
001B4Dr 3               ; ## ONE ( -- n ) "Push the number 1 to the Data Stack"
001B4Dr 3               ; ## "1"  auto  Tali Forth
001B4Dr 3                       ; """This is also the code for EDITOR-WORDLIST"""
001B4Dr 3               xt_editor_wordlist:
001B4Dr 3               xt_one:
001B4Dr 3  CA                           dex
001B4Er 3  CA                           dex
001B4Fr 3  A9 01                        lda #1
001B51r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001B53r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001B55r 3               
001B55r 3               z_editor_wordlist:
001B55r 3               z_one:
001B55r 3  60                           rts
001B56r 3               
001B56r 3               
001B56r 3               ; ## ONE_MINUS ( u -- u-1 ) "Decrease TOS by one"
001B56r 3               ; ## "1-"  auto  ANS core
001B56r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/OneMinus"""
001B56r 3               
001B56r 3               xt_one_minus:
001B56r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
001B59r 3               
001B59r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001B5Br 3  D0 02                        bne @1
001B5Dr 3  D6 01                        dec 1,x
001B5Fr 3               @1:
001B5Fr 3  D6 00                        dec 0,x
001B61r 3               
001B61r 3  60           z_one_minus:    rts
001B62r 3               
001B62r 3               
001B62r 3               
001B62r 3               ; ## ONE_PLUS ( u -- u+1 ) "Increase TOS by one"
001B62r 3               ; ## "1+"  auto  ANS core
001B62r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/OnePlus
001B62r 3                       ;
001B62r 3                       ; Code is shared with CHAR-PLUS
001B62r 3                       ; """
001B62r 3               
001B62r 3               xt_char_plus:
001B62r 3               xt_one_plus:
001B62r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
001B65r 3               
001B65r 3  F6 00                        inc 0,x
001B67r 3  D0 02                        bne @done
001B69r 3  F6 01                        inc 1,x
001B6Br 3               
001B6Br 3               @done:
001B6Br 3               z_char_plus:
001B6Br 3  60           z_one_plus:     rts
001B6Cr 3               
001B6Cr 3               
001B6Cr 3               
001B6Cr 3               ; ## ONLY ( -- ) "Set earch order to minimum wordlist"
001B6Cr 3               ; ## "only"  auto  ANS search ext
001B6Cr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/search/ONLY"""
001B6Cr 3               
001B6Cr 3               xt_only:
001B6Cr 3                               ; Put -1 on data stack.
001B6Cr 3  CA                           dex
001B6Dr 3  CA                           dex
001B6Er 3  A9 FF                        lda #$FF
001B70r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001B72r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001B74r 3               
001B74r 3                               ; Invoke set-order to set the minimum search order.
001B74r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_set_order
001B77r 3               
001B77r 3  60           z_only:         rts
001B78r 3               
001B78r 3               
001B78r 3               
001B78r 3               ; ## OR ( m n -- n ) "Logically OR TOS and NOS"
001B78r 3               ; ## "or"  auto  ANS core
001B78r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/OR"
001B78r 3               xt_or:
001B78r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001B7Br 3               
001B7Br 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001B7Dr 3  15 02                        ora 2,x
001B7Fr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001B81r 3               
001B81r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
001B83r 3  15 03                        ora 3,x
001B85r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001B87r 3               
001B87r 3  E8                           inx
001B88r 3  E8                           inx
001B89r 3               
001B89r 3  60           z_or:           rts
001B8Ar 3               
001B8Ar 3               
001B8Ar 3               ; ## ORDER ( -- ) "Print current word order list and current WID"
001B8Ar 3               ; ## "order"  auto  ANS core
001B8Ar 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/search/ORDER
001B8Ar 3                       ; Note the search order is displayed from first search to last
001B8Ar 3                       ; searched and is therefore exactly the reverse of the order in which
001B8Ar 3                       ; Forth stacks are displayed.
001B8Ar 3                       ;
001B8Ar 3                       ; A Forth implementation of this word is:
001B8Ar 3                       ;
001B8Ar 3                       ; 	: .wid ( wid -- )
001B8Ar 3                       ; 	dup 0=  if ." Forth "  drop    else
001B8Ar 3                       ; 	dup 1 = if ." Editor " drop    else
001B8Ar 3                       ; 	dup 2 = if ." Assembler " drop else
001B8Ar 3                       ; 	dup 3 = if ." Root " drop      else
001B8Ar 3                       ; 	           . ( just print the number )
001B8Ar 3                       ; 	then then then then ;
001B8Ar 3                       ;
001B8Ar 3                       ; : ORDER ( -- )
001B8Ar 3                       ; 	cr get-order 0 ?do .wid loop
001B8Ar 3                       ; 	space space get-current .wid ;
001B8Ar 3                       ;
001B8Ar 3                       ; This is an interactive program, so speed
001B8Ar 3                       ; is not as important as size. We assume we do not have more than 255
001B8Ar 3                       ; wordlists.
001B8Ar 3                       ; """
001B8Ar 3               
001B8Ar 3               xt_order:
001B8Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
001B8Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_get_order        ; ( wid_n ... wid_1 n )
001B90r 3               
001B90r 3                               ; Paranoid: Check if there are no wordlists, a rather
001B90r 3                               ; pathological case. this would mean ( 0 ) on the stack. In
001B90r 3                               ; that case, we just drop n and run
001B90r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x                 ; assumes no more than 255 wordlists
001B92r 3  F0 1E                        beq @drop_done
001B94r 3               
001B94r 3               @have_wordlists:
001B94r 3                               ; We arrive here with the LSB of TOS in A, the number of WIDs
001B94r 3                               ; on the stack
001B94r 3  A8                           tay
001B95r 3               @loop:
001B95r 3  E8                           inx
001B96r 3  E8                           inx                     ; DROP, now ( wid_n ... wid_1 )
001B97r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001B99r 3               
001B99r 3  5A                           phy
001B9Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr _print_wid_string   ; internal helper function
001B9Dr 3  7A                           ply
001B9Er 3               
001B9Er 3  88                           dey
001B9Fr 3  D0 F4                        bne @loop
001BA1r 3               
001BA1r 3                               ; We've printed the wordlists, now we add the current wordlist.
001BA1r 3                               ; This follows the convention of Gforth
001BA1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
001BA4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
001BA7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_get_current      ; ( wid )
001BAAr 3               
001BAAr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001BACr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr _print_wid_string
001BAFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
001BB2r 3               
001BB2r 3               @drop_done:
001BB2r 3  E8                           inx
001BB3r 3  E8                           inx
001BB4r 3               z_order:
001BB4r 3  60                           rts
001BB5r 3               
001BB5r 3               _print_wid_string:
001BB5r 3                       ; """Helper function for ORDER: Given a WID in A, print the
001BB5r 3                       ; corresponding string. If there is no such word list defined, just
001BB5r 3                       ; print the number. Assumes we will not have more than 256 WIDs; also
001BB5r 3                       ; assumes we have just loaded A so Z reflects status of byte.  In
001BB5r 3                       ; theory, we could speed this up by having the WID be the same as the
001BB5r 3                       ; number of the strings. However, ORDER is used rather infrequently and
001BB5r 3                       ; this would make changes to the strings.asm file very dangerous, so we
001BB5r 3                       ; follow the slightly more complicated route with a translation table.
001BB5r 3                       ; """
001BB5r 3                               ; If the WID is larger than 3, we have no string avaliable and
001BB5r 3                               ; just print the number.
001BB5r 3                               ; See http://6502.org/tutorials/compare_instructions.html
001BB5r 3                               ; for details
001BB5r 3  C9 04                        cmp #4
001BB7r 3  90 09                        bcc @output_string      ; less than 4, print a real string
001BB9r 3               
001BB9r 3                               ; Our WID is not less than 4, that is, 4 or larger. We just
001BB9r 3                               ; print the number
001BB9r 3  CA                           dex
001BBAr 3  CA                           dex
001BBBr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001BBDr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001BBFr 3  4C rr rr                     jmp xt_u_dot            ; JSR/RTS as this routine is not compiled
001BC2r 3               
001BC2r 3               @output_string:
001BC2r 3                               ; Get the string number based on WID 0 to 3
001BC2r 3  A8                           tay
001BC3r 3  B9 rr rr                     lda @wid_data,y
001BC6r 3               
001BC6r 3                               ; Print without a line feed
001BC6r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp print_string_no_lf  ; JSR/RTS as this routine is not compiled
001BC9r 3               
001BC9r 3               @wid_data:
001BC9r 3                       ; Table of string numbers (see strings.asm) indexed by the WID if
001BC9r 3                       ; less than 4.
001BC9r 3  03                   .byte str_wid_forth            ; WID 0: "Forth"
001BCAr 3  06                   .byte str_wid_editor           ; WID 1: "Editor"
001BCBr 3  07                   .byte str_wid_assembler        ; WID 2: "Assembler"
001BCCr 3  08                   .byte str_wid_root             ; WID 3: "Root"
001BCDr 3               
001BCDr 3               
001BCDr 3               
001BCDr 3               ; ## OUTPUT ( -- addr ) "Return the address of the EMIT vector address"
001BCDr 3               ; ## "output"  tested  Tali Forth
001BCDr 3               xt_output:
001BCDr 3                       ; """Return the address where the jump target for EMIT is stored (but
001BCDr 3                       ; not the vector itself). By default, this will hold the value of
001BCDr 3                       ; kernel_putc routine, but this can be changed by the user, hence this
001BCDr 3                       ; routine.
001BCDr 3                       ; """
001BCDr 3  CA                           dex
001BCEr 3  CA                           dex
001BCFr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<output
001BD1r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001BD3r 3  A9 rr                        lda #>output
001BD5r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001BD7r 3               
001BD7r 3  60           z_output:       rts
001BD8r 3               
001BD8r 3               
001BD8r 3               ; ## OVER ( b a -- b a b ) "Copy NOS to TOS"
001BD8r 3               ; ## "over"  auto  ANS core
001BD8r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/OVER"""
001BD8r 3               xt_over:
001BD8r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001BDBr 3               
001BDBr 3  CA                           dex
001BDCr 3  CA                           dex
001BDDr 3               
001BDDr 3  B5 04                        lda 4,x         ; LSB
001BDFr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001BE1r 3  B5 05                        lda 5,x         ; MSB
001BE3r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001BE5r 3               
001BE5r 3  60           z_over:         rts
001BE6r 3               
001BE6r 3               
001BE6r 3               ; ## PAD ( -- addr ) "Return address of user scratchpad"
001BE6r 3               ; ## "pad"  auto  ANS core ext
001BE6r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/PAD
001BE6r 3                       ; Return address to a temporary area in free memory for user. Must
001BE6r 3                       ; be at least 84 bytes in size (says ANS). It is located relative to
001BE6r 3                       ; the compile area pointer (CP) and therefore varies in position.
001BE6r 3                       ; This area is reserved for the user and not used by the system
001BE6r 3                       ; """
001BE6r 3               xt_pad:
001BE6r 3  CA                           dex
001BE7r 3  CA                           dex
001BE8r 3               
001BE8r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
001BEAr 3  18                           clc
001BEBr 3  69 FF                        adc #padoffset  ; assumes padoffset one byte in size
001BEDr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001BEFr 3               
001BEFr 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
001BF1r 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; only need carry
001BF3r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001BF5r 3               
001BF5r 3  60           z_pad:          rts
001BF6r 3               
001BF6r 3               
001BF6r 3               ; ## PAGE ( -- ) "Clear the screen"
001BF6r 3               ; ## "page"  tested  ANS facility
001BF6r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/facility/PAGE
001BF6r 3                       ; Clears a page if supported by ANS terminal codes. This is
001BF6r 3                       ; Clear Screen ("ESC[2J") plus moving the cursor to the top
001BF6r 3                       ; left of the screen
001BF6r 3                       ; """
001BF6r 3               xt_page:
001BF6r 3  A9 1B                        lda #AscESC
001BF8r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001BFBr 3  A9 5B                        lda #$5B        ; ASCII for "["
001BFDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001C00r 3  A9 32                        lda #'2'
001C02r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001C05r 3  A9 4A                        lda #'J'
001C07r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001C0Ar 3               
001C0Ar 3                               ; move cursor to top left of screen
001C0Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero
001C0Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero
001C10r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_at_xy
001C13r 3               
001C13r 3  60           z_page:         rts
001C14r 3               
001C14r 3               
001C14r 3               ; ## PAREN ( -- ) "Discard input up to close paren ( comment )"
001C14r 3               ; ## "("  auto  ANS core
001C14r 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/p"""
001C14r 3               
001C14r 3               xt_paren:
001C14r 3                               ; Put a right paren on the stack.
001C14r 3  CA                           dex
001C15r 3  CA                           dex
001C16r 3  A9 29                        lda #41     ; Right parenthesis
001C18r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001C1Ar 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001C1Cr 3               
001C1Cr 3                               ; Call parse.
001C1Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_parse
001C1Fr 3               
001C1Fr 3                               ; Throw away the result.
001C1Fr 3  E8                           inx
001C20r 3  E8                           inx
001C21r 3  E8                           inx
001C22r 3  E8                           inx
001C23r 3               
001C23r 3  60           z_paren:        rts
001C24r 3               
001C24r 3               
001C24r 3               
001C24r 3               ; ## PARSE_NAME ( "name" -- addr u ) "Parse the input"
001C24r 3               ; ## "parse-name"  auto  ANS core ext
001C24r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/PARSE-NAME
001C24r 3                       ; Find next word in input string, skipping leading whitespace. This is
001C24r 3                       ; a special form of PARSE and drops through to that word. See PARSE
001C24r 3                       ; for more detail. We use this word internally for the interpreter
001C24r 3                       ; because it is a lot easier to use. Reference implementations at
001C24r 3                       ; http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/PARSE-NAME and
001C24r 3                       ; http://www.forth200x.org/reference-implementations/parse-name.fs
001C24r 3                       ; Roughly, the word is comparable to BL WORD COUNT. -- Note that
001C24r 3                       ; though the ANS standard talks about skipping "spaces", whitespace
001C24r 3                       ; is actually perfectly legal (see for example
001C24r 3                       ; http://forth-standard.org/standard/usage#subsubsection.3.4.1.1).
001C24r 3                       ; Otherwise, PARSE-NAME chokes on tabs.
001C24r 3                       ; """
001C24r 3               
001C24r 3               xt_parse_name:
001C24r 3                               ; To enable the compilation of the high-level Forth words
001C24r 3                               ; in forth-words.asm and user-words.asm at boot time,
001C24r 3                               ; PARSE-NAME and PARSE must be able to deal with 16-bit string
001C24r 3                               ; lengths. This is a pain on an 8-bit machine. The pointer
001C24r 3                               ; to the current location is in toin (>IN). We need to check,
001C24r 3                               ; worst case, the characters from cib+toin to cib+ciblen, and
001C24r 3                               ; we can't just use Y as an index.
001C24r 3               
001C24r 3                               ; The counter is CIBLEN-TOIN and stored in tmp1
001C24r 3  A5 rr                        lda ciblen              ; LSB of counter
001C26r 3  38                           sec
001C27r 3  E5 rr                        sbc toin
001C29r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001C2Br 3  A5 rr                        lda ciblen+1            ; MSB
001C2Dr 3  E5 rr                        sbc toin+1
001C2Fr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001C31r 3               
001C31r 3                               ; Check the result for zero (TOIN is equal to CIBLEN)
001C31r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
001C33r 3  05 rr                        ora tmp1+1
001C35r 3  F0 28                        beq @empty_line
001C37r 3               
001C37r 3                               ; We walk through the characters starting at CIB+TOIN, so we
001C37r 3                               ; save a temp version of that in tmp2
001C37r 3  A5 rr                        lda cib
001C39r 3  18                           clc
001C3Ar 3  65 rr                        adc toin
001C3Cr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2                ; LSB of first character
001C3Er 3  A5 rr                        lda cib+1
001C40r 3  65 rr                        adc toin+1
001C42r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1              ; MSB
001C44r 3               
001C44r 3               @skip_loop:
001C44r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp2)              ; work copy of cib
001C46r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr is_whitespace
001C49r 3  90 1F                        bcc @char_found
001C4Br 3               
001C4Br 3                               ; Char is still whitespace, continue
001C4Br 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp2
001C4Dr 3  D0 02                        bne @2
001C4Fr 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp2+1
001C51r 3               @2:
001C51r 3                               ; Adjust counter
001C51r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
001C53r 3  D0 02                        bne @3
001C55r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1+1
001C57r 3               @3:
001C57r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1
001C59r 3               
001C59r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
001C5Br 3  05 rr                        ora tmp1+1
001C5Dr 3  D0 E5                        bne @skip_loop          ; fall through if empty line
001C5Fr 3               
001C5Fr 3               @empty_line:
001C5Fr 3                               ; Neither the ANS Forth nor the Gforth documentation say
001C5Fr 3                               ; what to return as an address if a string with only
001C5Fr 3                               ; spaces is given. For speed reasons, we just return junk
001C5Fr 3                               ; NOS, with the TOS zero as per standard
001C5Fr 3  CA                           dex
001C60r 3  CA                           dex
001C61r 3  CA                           dex
001C62r 3  CA                           dex
001C63r 3               
001C63r 3  74 00                        stz 0,x                 ; TOS is zero
001C65r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001C67r 3               
001C67r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp z_parse_name        ; skip over PARSE
001C6Ar 3               
001C6Ar 3               @char_found:
001C6Ar 3                               ; We arrive here with tmp2 pointing to the first non-space
001C6Ar 3                               ; character. This is where the word really starts, so
001C6Ar 3                               ; we use it to calculate the new >IN by subtracting
001C6Ar 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
001C6Cr 3  38                           sec
001C6Dr 3  E5 rr                        sbc cib
001C6Fr 3  85 rr                        sta toin
001C71r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1
001C73r 3  E5 rr                        sbc cib+1
001C75r 3  85 rr                        sta toin+1
001C77r 3               
001C77r 3                               ; prepare Data Stack for PARSE by adding space
001C77r 3                               ; as the delimiter
001C77r 3  CA                           dex
001C78r 3  CA                           dex
001C79r 3               
001C79r 3  A9 20                        lda #AscSP
001C7Br 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001C7Dr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x                 ; paranoid, now ( "name" c )
001C7Fr 3               
001C7Fr 3               
001C7Fr 3               ; ## PARSE ( "name" c -- addr u ) "Parse input with delimiter character"
001C7Fr 3               ; ## "parse"  tested  ANS core ext
001C7Fr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/PARSE
001C7Fr 3                       ; Find word in input string delimited by character given. Do not
001C7Fr 3                       ; skip leading delimiters -- this is the main difference to PARSE-NAME.
001C7Fr 3                       ; PARSE and PARSE-NAME replace WORD in modern systems. ANS discussion
001C7Fr 3                       ; http://www.forth200x.org/documents/html3/rationale.html#rat:core:PARSE
001C7Fr 3                       ;
001C7Fr 3                       ;
001C7Fr 3                       ;     cib  cib+toin   cib+ciblen
001C7Fr 3                       ;      v      v            v
001C7Fr 3                       ;     |###################|
001C7Fr 3                       ;
001C7Fr 3                       ;     |------>|  toin (>IN)
001C7Fr 3                       ;     |------------------->|  ciblen
001C7Fr 3                       ;
001C7Fr 3                       ; The input string is stored starting at the address in the Current
001C7Fr 3                       ; Input Buffer (CIB), the length of which is in CIBLEN. While searching
001C7Fr 3                       ; for the delimiter, TOIN (>IN) points to the where we currently are.
001C7Fr 3                       ; Since PARSE does not skip leading delimiters, we assume we are on a
001C7Fr 3                       ; useful string if there are any characters at all. As with
001C7Fr 3                       ; PARSE-NAME, we must be able to handle strings with a length of
001C7Fr 3                       ; 16-bit for EVALUTE, which is a pain on an 8-bit machine.
001C7Fr 3                       ; """
001C7Fr 3               
001C7Fr 3               xt_parse:
001C7Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
001C82r 3               
001C82r 3                               ; If the input buffer is empty, we just return
001C82r 3  A5 rr                        lda ciblen
001C84r 3  05 rr                        ora ciblen+1
001C86r 3  F0 0C                        beq @abort_parse
001C88r 3               
001C88r 3                               ; If the pointer >IN is larger or equal to the length of
001C88r 3                               ; the input buffer (CIBLEN), the line is done. Put
001C88r 3                               ; differently, we only continue if >IN is smaller than
001C88r 3                               ; CIBLEN
001C88r 3  A5 rr                        lda toin+1              ; MSB
001C8Ar 3  C5 rr                        cmp ciblen+1
001C8Cr 3  90 0E                        bcc @go_parse           ; unsigned comparison
001C8Er 3               
001C8Er 3  A5 rr                        lda toin                ; LSB
001C90r 3  C5 rr                        cmp ciblen
001C92r 3  90 08                        bcc @go_parse
001C94r 3               
001C94r 3               @abort_parse:
001C94r 3                               ; Sorry, this line is over
001C94r 3  CA                           dex
001C95r 3  CA                           dex
001C96r 3  74 00                        stz 0,x
001C98r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001C9Ar 3               
001C9Ar 3  80 7A                        bra @done
001C9Cr 3               @go_parse:
001C9Cr 3                               ; We actually have work to do. Save the delimiter in
001C9Cr 3                               ; tmptos.
001C9Cr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001C9Er 3  85 rr                        sta tmptos
001CA0r 3               
001CA0r 3                               ; We can now prepare the Data Stack for the return value
001CA0r 3  CA                           dex
001CA1r 3  CA                           dex
001CA2r 3               
001CA2r 3                               ; tmp1 is CIB+TOIN, the beginning of the current string
001CA2r 3                               ; tmp2 is initially the same as tmp1, then the work index
001CA2r 3                               ; tmp3 is CIB+CIBLEN, one char past the end of the string
001CA2r 3               
001CA2r 3                               ; Calculate the beginning of the string, which is also the
001CA2r 3                               ; address to return
001CA2r 3  A5 rr                        lda cib
001CA4r 3  18                           clc
001CA5r 3  65 rr                        adc toin        ; LSB
001CA7r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001CA9r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2
001CABr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001CADr 3               
001CADr 3  A5 rr                        lda cib+1
001CAFr 3  65 rr                        adc toin+1      ; MSB
001CB1r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001CB3r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1
001CB5r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001CB7r 3               
001CB7r 3                               ; Calculate the address where the input buffer ends plus 1, so
001CB7r 3                               ; we can compare it with TOIN, which is an index
001CB7r 3  A5 rr                        lda cib
001CB9r 3  18                           clc
001CBAr 3  65 rr                        adc ciblen
001CBCr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3
001CBEr 3  A5 rr                        lda cib+1
001CC0r 3  65 rr                        adc ciblen+1
001CC2r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3+1
001CC4r 3               
001CC4r 3                               ; Initialize the offset we use to adjust EOL or found delimiter
001CC4r 3  64 rr                        stz tmptos+1
001CC6r 3               @loop:
001CC6r 3                               ; If we are at the end of the string, quit
001CC6r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
001CC8r 3  C5 rr                        cmp tmp3
001CCAr 3  D0 06                        bne @not_empty
001CCCr 3               
001CCCr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1
001CCEr 3  C5 rr                        cmp tmp3+1
001CD0r 3  F0 1D                        beq @eol
001CD2r 3               @not_empty:
001CD2r 3                               ; We have to do this the hard way. In fact, it's really
001CD2r 3                               ; hard since if we are dealing with a SPACE, the standard
001CD2r 3                               ; wants us to skip all whitespace, not just spaces. Otherwise,
001CD2r 3                               ; Tali would choke on tabs between words. For details, see
001CD2r 3                               ; http://forth-standard.org/standard/file#subsection.11.3.5
001CD2r 3                               ; In theory, we could make this faster by defining a delimiter
001CD2r 3                               ; that is 00 as the sign that we skip all whitespace, thereby
001CD2r 3                               ; avoiding having to test every time. However, somebody,
001CD2r 3                               ; somewhere might want to parse a zero-delimited list. Since
001CD2r 3                               ; any byte value could be chosen for that, we just test for
001CD2r 3                               ; a space every single time for the moment.
001CD2r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp2)
001CD4r 3               
001CD4r 3  A4 rr                        ldy tmptos
001CD6r 3  C0 20                        cpy #AscSP
001CD8r 3  D0 07                        bne @not_whitespace
001CDAr 3               
001CDAr 3                               ; The delimiter is a space, so we're looking for all
001CDAr 3                               ; whitespace
001CDAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr is_whitespace
001CDDr 3  90 02                        bcc @not_whitespace
001CDFr 3  80 0C                        bra @found_delimiter
001CE1r 3               
001CE1r 3               @not_whitespace:
001CE1r 3                               ; The delimiter is not a space, so we're looking for
001CE1r 3                               ; whatever it is
001CE1r 3  C5 rr                        cmp tmptos
001CE3r 3  F0 08                        beq @found_delimiter
001CE5r 3               
001CE5r 3                               ; Not a delimiter, next character
001CE5r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp2
001CE7r 3  D0 DD                        bne @loop
001CE9r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp2+1
001CEBr 3  80 D9                        bra @loop
001CEDr 3               
001CEDr 3               @found_delimiter:
001CEDr 3                               ; Increase the offset: If we've found a delimiter, we want
001CEDr 3                               ; TOIN to point to the character after it, not the delimiter
001CEDr 3                               ; itself
001CEDr 3  E6 rr                        inc tmptos+1
001CEFr 3               @eol:
001CEFr 3                               ; The length of the new string is tmp2-tmp1
001CEFr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
001CF1r 3  38                           sec
001CF2r 3  E5 rr                        sbc tmp1
001CF4r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001CF6r 3               
001CF6r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1
001CF8r 3  E5 rr                        sbc tmp1+1
001CFAr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001CFCr 3               
001CFCr 3                               ; The new offset is tmp2-cib
001CFCr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
001CFEr 3  38                           sec
001CFFr 3  E5 rr                        sbc cib
001D01r 3  85 rr                        sta toin
001D03r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1
001D05r 3  E5 rr                        sbc cib+1
001D07r 3  85 rr                        sta toin+1
001D09r 3               
001D09r 3                               ; Add in the delimiter
001D09r 3  A5 rr                        lda toin
001D0Br 3  18                           clc
001D0Cr 3  65 rr                        adc tmptos+1
001D0Er 3  85 rr                        sta toin
001D10r 3  A5 rr                        lda toin+1
001D12r 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; we only need the carry
001D14r 3  85 rr                        sta toin+1
001D16r 3               @done:
001D16r 3               z_parse_name:
001D16r 3  60           z_parse:        rts
001D17r 3               
001D17r 3               
001D17r 3               
001D17r 3               ; ## PICK ( n n u -- n n n ) "Move element u of the stack to TOS"
001D17r 3               ; ## "pick"  auto  ANS core ext
001D17r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/PICK
001D17r 3                       ; Take the u-th element out of the stack and put it on TOS,
001D17r 3                       ; overwriting the original TOS. 0 PICK is equivalent to DUP, 1 PICK to
001D17r 3                       ; OVER. Note that using PICK is considered poor coding form. Also note
001D17r 3                       ; that FIG Forth has a different behavior for PICK than ANS Forth.
001D17r 3                       ; """
001D17r 3               
001D17r 3               xt_pick:
001D17r 3                               ; Checking for underflow is difficult because it depends on
001D17r 3                               ; which element we want to grab. We could probably figure
001D17r 3                               ; something out, but it wouldn't work with underflow stripping
001D17r 3                               ; Since using PICK is considered poor form anyway, we just
001D17r 3                               ; leave it as it is
001D17r 3  16 00                        asl 0,x         ; we assume u < 128 (stack is small)
001D19r 3  8A                           txa
001D1Ar 3  75 00                        adc 0,x
001D1Cr 3  A8                           tay
001D1Dr 3               
001D1Dr 3  B9 02 00                     lda 0002,y
001D20r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001D22r 3  B9 03 00                     lda 0003,y
001D25r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001D27r 3               
001D27r 3  60           z_pick:         rts
001D28r 3               
001D28r 3               
001D28r 3               
001D28r 3               ; ## PLUS ( n n -- n ) "Add TOS and NOS"
001D28r 3               ; ## "+"  auto  ANS core
001D28r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Plus"""
001D28r 3               xt_plus:
001D28r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001D2Br 3               
001D2Br 3  18                           clc
001D2Cr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB
001D2Er 3  75 02                        adc 2,x
001D30r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001D32r 3               
001D32r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB. No CLC, conserve carry bit
001D34r 3  75 03                        adc 3,x
001D36r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001D38r 3               
001D38r 3  E8                           inx
001D39r 3  E8                           inx
001D3Ar 3               
001D3Ar 3  60           z_plus:         rts
001D3Br 3               
001D3Br 3               
001D3Br 3               ; ## PLUS_STORE ( n addr -- ) "Add number to value at given address"
001D3Br 3               ; ## "+!"  auto  ANS core
001D3Br 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/PlusStore"""
001D3Br 3               xt_plus_store:
001D3Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001D3Er 3               
001D3Er 3                               ; move address to tmp1 so we can work with it
001D3Er 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001D40r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001D42r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
001D44r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001D46r 3               
001D46r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0          ; LSB
001D48r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
001D4Ar 3  18                           clc
001D4Br 3  75 02                        adc 2,x
001D4Dr 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
001D4Fr 3               
001D4Fr 3  C8                           iny             ; MSB
001D50r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
001D52r 3  75 03                        adc 3,x
001D54r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
001D56r 3               
001D56r 3  E8                           inx
001D57r 3  E8                           inx
001D58r 3  E8                           inx
001D59r 3  E8                           inx
001D5Ar 3               
001D5Ar 3  60           z_plus_store:   rts
001D5Br 3               
001D5Br 3               
001D5Br 3               ; ## POSTPONE ( -- ) "Change IMMEDIATE status (it's complicated)"
001D5Br 3               ; ## "postpone"  auto   ANS core
001D5Br 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/POSTPONE
001D5Br 3                       ; Add the compilation behavior of a word to a new word at
001D5Br 3                       ; compile time. If the word that follows it is immediate, include
001D5Br 3                       ; it so that it will be compiled when the word being defined is
001D5Br 3                       ; itself used for a new word. Tricky, but very useful.
001D5Br 3                       ;
001D5Br 3                       ; Because POSTPONE expects a word (not an xt) in the input stream (not
001D5Br 3                       ; on the Data Stack). This means we cannot build words with
001D5Br 3                       ; "jsr xt_postpone, jsr <word>" directly.
001D5Br 3                       ; """
001D5Br 3               
001D5Br 3               xt_postpone:
001D5Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_parse_name               ; ( -- addr n )
001D5Er 3               
001D5Er 3                               ; if there was no word provided, complain and quit
001D5Er 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001D60r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
001D62r 3  D0 05                        bne @1
001D64r 3               
001D64r 3  A9 05                        lda #err_noname
001D66r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp error
001D69r 3               @1:
001D69r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_find_name                ; ( -- nt | 0 )
001D6Cr 3               
001D6Cr 3                               ; if word not in Dictionary, complain and quit
001D6Cr 3  D0 05                        bne @2
001D6Er 3  A9 05                        lda #err_noname
001D70r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp error
001D73r 3               
001D73r 3               @2:
001D73r 3                               ; keep a copy of nt for later
001D73r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001D75r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001D77r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
001D79r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001D7Br 3               
001D7Br 3                               ; We need the xt instead of the nt
001D7Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_name_to_int              ; ( nt -- xt )
001D7Er 3               
001D7Er 3                               ; See if this is an immediate word. This is easier
001D7Er 3                               ; with nt than with xt. The status byte of the word
001D7Er 3                               ; is nt+1
001D7Er 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1
001D80r 3  D0 02                        bne @3
001D82r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1+1
001D84r 3               @3:
001D84r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp1)
001D86r 3  29 04                        and #IM         ; mask all but Intermediate flag
001D88r 3  F0 05                        beq @not_immediate
001D8Ar 3               
001D8Ar 3                               ; We're immediate, so instead of executing it right now, we
001D8Ar 3                               ; compile it. xt is TOS, so this is easy. The RTS at the end
001D8Ar 3                               ; takes us back to the original caller
001D8Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_compile_comma
001D8Dr 3  80 0A                        bra @done
001D8Fr 3               
001D8Fr 3               @not_immediate:
001D8Fr 3                               ; This is not an immediate word, so we enact "deferred
001D8Fr 3                               ; compilation" by including ' <NAME> COMPILE, which we do by
001D8Fr 3                               ; compiling the run-time routine of LITERAL, the xt itself, and
001D8Fr 3                               ; a subroutine jump to COMPILE,
001D8Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_literal
001D92r 3               
001D92r 3                               ; Last, compile COMPILE,
001D92r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>xt_compile_comma
001D94r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<xt_compile_comma
001D96r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
001D99r 3               @done:
001D99r 3  60           z_postpone:     rts
001D9Ar 3               
001D9Ar 3               
001D9Ar 3               
001D9Ar 3               ; ## PREVIOUS ( -- ) "Remove the first wordlist in the search order"
001D9Ar 3               ; ## "previous"  auto  ANS search ext
001D9Ar 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/search/PREVIOUS"""
001D9Ar 3               
001D9Ar 3               xt_previous:
001D9Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_get_order
001D9Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_nip
001DA0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_one_minus
001DA3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_set_order
001DA6r 3               
001DA6r 3  60           z_previous:     rts
001DA7r 3               
001DA7r 3               
001DA7r 3               
001DA7r 3               ; ## QUESTION ( addr -- ) "Print content of a variable"
001DA7r 3               ; ## "?"  tested  ANS tools
001DA7r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/tools/q
001DA7r 3                       ;
001DA7r 3                       ; Only used interactively. Since humans are so slow, we
001DA7r 3                       ; save size and just go for the subroutine jumps
001DA7r 3                       ; """
001DA7r 3               xt_question:
001DA7r 3                               ; FETCH takes care of underflow check
001DA7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_fetch
001DAAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dot
001DADr 3               
001DADr 3  60           z_question:     rts
001DAEr 3               
001DAEr 3               
001DAEr 3               ; ## QUESTION_DUP ( n -- 0 | n n ) "Duplicate TOS non-zero"
001DAEr 3               ; ## "?dup"  auto  ANS core
001DAEr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/qDUP"""
001DAEr 3               
001DAEr 3               xt_question_dup:
001DAEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
001DB1r 3               
001DB1r 3                               ; Check if TOS is zero
001DB1r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001DB3r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
001DB5r 3  F0 0A                        beq @done
001DB7r 3               
001DB7r 3                               ; not zero, duplicate
001DB7r 3  CA                           dex
001DB8r 3  CA                           dex
001DB9r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
001DBBr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001DBDr 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
001DBFr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001DC1r 3               @done:
001DC1r 3  60           z_question_dup: rts
001DC2r 3               
001DC2r 3               
001DC2r 3               
001DC2r 3               ; ## R_FETCH ( -- n ) "Get copy of top of Return Stack"
001DC2r 3               ; ## "r@"  auto  ANS core
001DC2r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/RFetch
001DC2r 3                       ; This word is Compile Only in Tali Forth, though Gforth has it
001DC2r 3                       ; work normally as well
001DC2r 3                       ;
001DC2r 3                       ; An alternative way to write this word
001DC2r 3                       ; would be to access the elements on the stack directly like 2R@
001DC2r 3                       ; does, these versions should be compared at some point.
001DC2r 3                       ; """
001DC2r 3               xt_r_fetch:
001DC2r 3                               ; get the return address
001DC2r 3  7A                           ply             ; LSB
001DC3r 3  84 rr                        sty tmp1
001DC5r 3  7A                           ply             ; MSB
001DC6r 3               
001DC6r 3                               ; --- CUT FOR NATIVE COMPILE ---
001DC6r 3               
001DC6r 3                               ; get the actual top of Return Stack
001DC6r 3  CA                           dex
001DC7r 3  CA                           dex
001DC8r 3               
001DC8r 3  68                           pla             ; LSB
001DC9r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001DCBr 3  68                           pla             ; MSB
001DCCr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001DCEr 3               
001DCEr 3                               ; now we have to put that value back
001DCEr 3  48                           pha
001DCFr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001DD1r 3  48                           pha
001DD2r 3               
001DD2r 3                               ; --- CUT FOR NATIVE COMPILE ---
001DD2r 3               
001DD2r 3                               ; restore return value
001DD2r 3  5A                           phy             ; MSB
001DD3r 3  A4 rr                        ldy tmp1
001DD5r 3  5A                           phy             ; LSB
001DD6r 3               
001DD6r 3  60           z_r_fetch:      rts
001DD7r 3               
001DD7r 3               
001DD7r 3               ; ## R_FROM ( -- n )(R: n --) "Move top of Return Stack to TOS"
001DD7r 3               ; ## "r>"  auto  ANS core
001DD7r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Rfrom
001DD7r 3                       ; Move Top of Return Stack to Top of Data Stack.
001DD7r 3                       ;
001DD7r 3                       ; We have to move
001DD7r 3                       ; the RTS address out of the way first. This word is handled
001DD7r 3                       ; differently for native and and subroutine compilation, see COMPILE,
001DD7r 3                       ; This is a compile-only word
001DD7r 3                       ; """
001DD7r 3               
001DD7r 3               xt_r_from:
001DD7r 3                               ; Rescue the address of the return jump that is currently
001DD7r 3                               ; on top of the Return Stack. If this word is natively
001DD7r 3                               ; compiled, this is a total waste of time
001DD7r 3  68                           pla             ; LSB
001DD8r 3  85 rr                        sta tmptos
001DDAr 3  7A                           ply             ; MSB
001DDBr 3               
001DDBr 3                               ; --- CUT FOR NATIVE CODING ---
001DDBr 3               
001DDBr 3  CA                           dex
001DDCr 3  CA                           dex
001DDDr 3               
001DDDr 3                               ; now we can access the actual data
001DDDr 3               
001DDDr 3  68                           pla             ; LSB
001DDEr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001DE0r 3  68                           pla             ; MSB
001DE1r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001DE3r 3               
001DE3r 3                               ; --- CUT FOR NATIVE CODING ---
001DE3r 3               
001DE3r 3                               ; restore the return address
001DE3r 3  5A                           phy             ; MSB
001DE4r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmptos
001DE6r 3  48                           pha             ; LSB
001DE7r 3               
001DE7r 3  60           z_r_from:       rts
001DE8r 3               
001DE8r 3               
001DE8r 3               ; ## R_TO_INPUT ( -- ) ( R: n n n n -- ) "Restore input state from Return Stack"
001DE8r 3               ; ## "r>input"  tested  Tali Forth
001DE8r 3                       ; """Restore the current input state as defined by insrc, cib, ciblen,
001DE8r 3                       ; and toin from the Return Stack.
001DE8r 3                       ;
001DE8r 3                       ; See INPUT_TO_R for a discussion of this word. Uses tmp1
001DE8r 3                       ; """
001DE8r 3               
001DE8r 3               xt_r_to_input:
001DE8r 3               
001DE8r 3                               ; We arrive here with the return address on the top of the
001DE8r 3                               ; 65c02's stack. We need to move it out of the way first
001DE8r 3  68                           pla
001DE9r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001DEBr 3  68                           pla
001DECr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001DEEr 3               
001DEEr 3                               ; This assumes that insrc is the first of eight bytes and
001DEEr 3                               ; toin+1 the last in the sequence we want to save from the Zero
001DEEr 3                               ; Page. Since we went in reverse order, insrc is now on the top
001DEEr 3                               ; of the Return Stack.
001DEEr 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
001DF0r 3               @loop:
001DF0r 3  68                           pla
001DF1r 3  99 rr rr                     sta insrc,y
001DF4r 3  C8                           iny
001DF5r 3  C0 08                        cpy #8
001DF7r 3  D0 F7                        bne @loop
001DF9r 3               
001DF9r 3                               ; Restore address for return jump
001DF9r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
001DFBr 3  48                           pha
001DFCr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
001DFEr 3  48                           pha
001DFFr 3               
001DFFr 3  60           z_r_to_input: 	rts
001E00r 3               
001E00r 3               
001E00r 3               
001E00r 3               ; ## RECURSE ( -- ) "Copy recursive call to word being defined"
001E00r 3               ; ## "recurse"  auto  ANS core
001E00r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/RECURSE
001E00r 3                       ;
001E00r 3                       ; This word may not be natively compiled
001E00r 3                       ; """
001E00r 3               
001E00r 3               xt_recurse:
001E00r 3                               ; The whole routine amounts to compiling a reference to
001E00r 3                               ; the word that is being compiled. First, we save the JSR
001E00r 3                               ; instruction
001E00r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
001E02r 3               
001E02r 3  A9 20                        lda #$20        ; opcode for JSR
001E04r 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
001E06r 3  C8                           iny
001E07r 3               
001E07r 3                               ; Next, we save the LSB and MSB of the xt of the word
001E07r 3                               ; we are currently working on. We first need to see if
001E07r 3                               ; WORKWORD has the nt (: started the word) or the
001E07r 3                               ; xt (:NONAME started the word). Bit 6 in status tells us.
001E07r 3  24 rr                        bit status
001E09r 3  70 0C                        bvs @nt_in_workword
001E0Br 3               
001E0Br 3                               ; This is a special :NONAME word. Just copy the xt
001E0Br 3                               ; from WORKWORD into the dictionary.
001E0Br 3  A5 rr                        lda workword
001E0Dr 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
001E0Fr 3  C8                           iny
001E10r 3  A5 rr                        lda workword+1
001E12r 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
001E14r 3  C8                           iny
001E15r 3  80 1B                        bra @update_cp
001E17r 3               
001E17r 3               @nt_in_workword:
001E17r 3                               ; This is a regular : word, so the xt is four bytes down
001E17r 3                               ; from the nt which we saved in WORKWORD. We could probably
001E17r 3                               ; use NAME>INT here but this is going to be faster, and
001E17r 3                               ; fast counts with recursion
001E17r 3  A5 rr                        lda workword            ; LSB
001E19r 3  18                           clc
001E1Ar 3  69 04                        adc #4
001E1Cr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001E1Er 3  A5 rr                        lda workword+1          ; MSB
001E20r 3  69 00                        adc #0
001E22r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001E24r 3               
001E24r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp1)
001E26r 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
001E28r 3  5A                           phy
001E29r 3  A0 01                        ldy #1
001E2Br 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
001E2Dr 3  7A                           ply
001E2Er 3  C8                           iny
001E2Fr 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
001E31r 3  C8                           iny
001E32r 3               
001E32r 3               @update_cp:
001E32r 3  98                           tya
001E33r 3  18                           clc
001E34r 3  65 rr                        adc cp
001E36r 3  85 rr                        sta cp
001E38r 3  90 02                        bcc @done
001E3Ar 3  E6 rr                        inc cp+1
001E3Cr 3               @done:
001E3Cr 3  60           z_recurse:      rts
001E3Dr 3               
001E3Dr 3               
001E3Dr 3               
001E3Dr 3               ; ## REFILL ( -- f ) "Refill the input buffer"
001E3Dr 3               ; ## "refill"  tested  ANS core ext
001E3Dr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/REFILL
001E3Dr 3                       ; Attempt to fill the input buffer from the input source, returning
001E3Dr 3                       ; a true flag if successful. When the input source is the user input
001E3Dr 3                       ; device, attempt to receive input into the terminal input buffer. If
001E3Dr 3                       ; successful, make the result the input buffer, set >IN to zero, and
001E3Dr 3                       ; return true. Receipt of a line containing no characters is considered
001E3Dr 3                       ; successful. If there is no input available from the current input
001E3Dr 3                       ; source, return false. When the input source is a string from EVALUATE,
001E3Dr 3                       ; return false and perform no other action." See
001E3Dr 3                       ; https://www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/The-Input-Stream.html
001E3Dr 3                       ; and Conklin & Rather p. 156. Note we don't have to care about blocks
001E3Dr 3                       ; because REFILL is never used on blocks - Tali is able to evaluate the
001E3Dr 3                       ; entire block as a 1024 byte string.
001E3Dr 3                       ; """"
001E3Dr 3               
001E3Dr 3               xt_refill:
001E3Dr 3                               ; Get input source from SOURCE-ID. This is an
001E3Dr 3                               ; optimized version of a subroutine jump to SOURCE-ID
