002842r 3               
002842r 3               ; ## TYPE ( addr u -- ) "Print string"
002842r 3               ; ## "type"  auto  ANS core
002842r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TYPE
002842r 3                       ; Works through EMIT to allow OUTPUT revectoring.
002842r 3                       ; """
002842r 3               
002842r 3               xt_type:
002842r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
002845r 3               
002845r 3                               ; Save the starting address into tmp1
002845r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
002847r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
002849r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
00284Br 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
00284Dr 3               @loop:
00284Dr 3                               ; done if length is zero
00284Dr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
00284Fr 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002851r 3  F0 15                        beq @done
002853r 3               
002853r 3                               ; Send the current character
002853r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp1)
002855r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a      ; avoids stack foolery
002858r 3               
002858r 3                               ; Move the address along (in tmp1)
002858r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1
00285Ar 3  D0 02                        bne @1
00285Cr 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1+1
00285Er 3               @1:
00285Er 3                               ; Reduce the count (on the data stack)
00285Er 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002860r 3  D0 02                        bne @2
002862r 3  D6 01                        dec 1,x
002864r 3               @2:
002864r 3  D6 00                        dec 0,x
002866r 3               
002866r 3  80 E5                        bra @loop
002868r 3               @done:
002868r 3  E8                           inx
002869r 3  E8                           inx
00286Ar 3  E8                           inx
00286Br 3  E8                           inx
00286Cr 3               
00286Cr 3  60           z_type:         rts
00286Dr 3               
00286Dr 3               
00286Dr 3               
00286Dr 3               ; ## U_DOT ( u -- ) "Print TOS as unsigned number"
00286Dr 3               ; ## "u."  tested  ANS core
00286Dr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Ud
00286Dr 3                       ;
00286Dr 3                       ; This is : U. 0 <# #S #> TYPE SPACE ; in Forth
00286Dr 3                       ; We use the internal assembler function print_u followed
00286Dr 3                       ; by a single space
00286Dr 3                       ; """
00286Dr 3               xt_u_dot:
00286Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002870r 3               
002870r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr print_u
002873r 3  A9 20                        lda #AscSP
002875r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
002878r 3               
002878r 3  60           z_u_dot:        rts
002879r 3               
002879r 3               
002879r 3               ; ## U_DOT_R ( u u -- ) "Print NOS as unsigned number right-justified with TOS width"

002879r 3               xt_u_dot_r:

00287Cr 3

00287Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero
002882r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_less_number_sign
002885r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_s
002888r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_greater
00288Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_from
00288Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_over
002891r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_minus
002894r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_spaces
002897r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type

00289Br 3               
00289Br 3               ; ## U_GREATER_THAN ( n m -- f ) "Return true if NOS > TOS (unsigned)"
00289Br 3               ; ## "u>"  auto  ANS core ext
00289Br 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Umore"""
00289Br 3               xt_u_greater_than:
00289Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
00289Er 3               
00289Er 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0028A0r 3  D5 02                        cmp 2,x
0028A2r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
0028A4r 3  F5 03                        sbc 3,x
0028A6r 3  E8                           inx
0028A7r 3  E8                           inx
0028A8r 3               
0028A8r 3  A9 00                        lda #0
0028AAr 3  69 FF                        adc #$ff
0028ACr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x         ; store flag
0028AEr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0028B0r 3               
0028B0r 3  60           z_u_greater_than:    rts
0028B1r 3               
0028B1r 3               ; ## U_LESS_THAN ( n m -- f ) "Return true if NOS < TOS (unsigned)"

0028B1r 3               xt_u_less_than:

0028B4r 3

0028B6r 3  D5 00                        cmp 0,x
0028B8r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
0028BAr 3  F5 01                        sbc 1,x
0028BCr 3  E8                           inx
0028BDr 3  E8                           inx
0028BEr 3               
0028BEr 3  A9 00                        lda #0
0028C0r 3  69 FF                        adc #$ff
0028C2r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x         ; store flag
0028C4r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0028C6r 3

0028D0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_greater

0028DAr 3               ; ## "ud.r"  auto  Tali double

0028DAr 3                       ; """
0028DAr 3               xt_ud_dot_r:

0028F9r 3               
0028F9r 3               
0028F9r 3               ; ## UM_SLASH_MOD ( ud u -- ur u ) "32/16 -> 16 division"
0028F9r 3               ; ## "um/mod"  auto  ANS core
0028F9r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/UMDivMOD
0028F9r 3                       ; Divide double cell number by single cell number, returning the
0028F9r 3                       ; quotient as TOS and any remainder as NOS. All numbers are unsigned.
0028F9r 3                       ; This is the basic division operation all others use. Based on FIG
0028F9r 3                       ; Forth code, modified by Garth Wilson, see
0028F9r 3                       ; http://6502.org/source/integers/ummodfix/ummodfix.htm
0028F9r 3                       ;
0028F9r 3                       ; This uses tmp1, tmp1+1, and tmptos
0028F9r 3                       ; """
0028F9r 3               
0028F9r 3               xt_um_slash_mod:
0028F9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_3
0028FCr 3               
0028FCr 3                               ; catch division by zero
0028FCr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0028FEr 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002900r 3  D0 05                        bne @not_zero
002902r 3               
002902r 3  A9 04                        lda #err_divzero
002904r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp error
002907r 3               
002907r 3               @not_zero:
002907r 3                               ; We loop 17 times
002907r 3  A9 11                        lda #17
002909r 3  85 rr                        sta tmptos
00290Br 3               
00290Br 3               @loop:
00290Br 3                               ; rotate low cell of dividend one bit left (LSB)
00290Br 3  36 04                        rol 4,x
00290Dr 3  36 05                        rol 5,x
00290Fr 3               
00290Fr 3                               ; loop control
00290Fr 3  C6 rr                        dec tmptos
002911r 3  F0 22                        beq @done
002913r 3               
002913r 3                               ; rotate high cell of dividend one bit left (MSB)
002913r 3  36 02                        rol 2,x
002915r 3  36 03                        rol 3,x
002917r 3               
002917r 3  64 rr                        stz tmp1        ; store the bit we got from hi cell (MSB)
002919r 3  26 rr                        rol tmp1
00291Br 3               
00291Br 3                               ; subtract dividend hi cell minus divisor
00291Br 3  38                           sec
00291Cr 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
00291Er 3  F5 00                        sbc 0,x
002920r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
002922r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
002924r 3  F5 01                        sbc 1,x
002926r 3               
002926r 3  A8                           tay
002927r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
002929r 3  E9 00                        sbc #0
00292Br 3  90 DE                        bcc @loop
00292Dr 3               
00292Dr 3                               ; make result new dividend high cell
00292Dr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
00292Fr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
002931r 3  94 03                        sty 3,x         ; used as temp storage
002933r 3               
002933r 3  80 D6                        bra @loop
002935r 3               @done:
002935r 3  E8                           inx
002936r 3  E8                           inx
002937r 3               
002937r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_swap
00293Ar 3               
00293Ar 3  60           z_um_slash_mod: rts
00293Br 3               
00293Br 3               
00293Br 3               
00293Br 3               ; ## UM_STAR ( u u -- ud ) "Multiply 16 x 16 -> 32"
00293Br 3               ; ## "um*"  auto  ANS core
00293Br 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/UMTimes
00293Br 3                       ; Multiply two unsigned 16 bit numbers, producing a 32 bit result.
00293Br 3                       ; Old Forth versions such as FIG Forth call this U*
00293Br 3                       ;
00293Br 3                       ; This is based on modified FIG Forth code by Dr. Jefyll, see
00293Br 3                       ; http://forum.6502.org/viewtopic.php?f=9&t=689 for a detailed
00293Br 3                       ; discussion.
00293Br 3                       ;
00293Br 3                       ; We don't use the system scratch pad (SYSPAD) for temp
00293Br 3                       ; storage because >NUMBER uses it as well, but instead tmp1 to
00293Br 3                       ; tmp3 (tmp1 is N in the original code, tmp1+1 is N+1, etc).
00293Br 3                       ;
00293Br 3                       ; Consider switching to a table-supported version based on
00293Br 3                       ; http://codebase64.org/doku.php?id=base:seriously_fast_multiplication
00293Br 3                       ; http://codebase64.org/doku.php?id=magazines:chacking16#d_graphics_for_the_masseslib3d>
00293Br 3                       ; http://forum.6502.org/viewtopic.php?p=205#p205
00293Br 3                       ; http://forum.6502.org/viewtopic.php?f=9&t=689
00293Br 3                       ; """
00293Br 3               
00293Br 3               xt_um_star:
00293Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
00293Er 3               
00293Er 3                               ; to eliminate clc inside the loop, the value at
00293Er 3                               ; tmp1 is reduced by 1 in advance
00293Er 3  18                           clc
00293Fr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; copy TOS to tmp2
002941r 3  E9 00                        sbc #0
002943r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2
002945r 3               
002945r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
002947r 3  E9 00                        sbc #0
002949r 3  90 31                        bcc @zero       ; is TOS zero?
00294Br 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1
00294Dr 3               
00294Dr 3  A9 00                        lda #0
00294Fr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
002951r 3  86 rr                        stx tmp3        ; tested for exit from outer loop
002953r 3  CA                           dex
002954r 3  CA                           dex
002955r 3               
002955r 3               @outer_loop:
002955r 3  A0 08                        ldy #8          ; counter inner loop
002957r 3  56 04                        lsr 4,x         ; think "2,x" then later "3,x"
002959r 3               
002959r 3               @inner_loop:
002959r 3  90 0C                        bcc @no_add
00295Br 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1      ; save time, don't CLC
00295Dr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
00295Fr 3  65 rr                        adc tmp2
002961r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
002963r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
002965r 3  65 rr                        adc tmp2+1
002967r 3               
002967r 3               @no_add:
002967r 3  6A                           ror
002968r 3  66 rr                        ror tmp1
00296Ar 3  76 04                        ror 4,x         ; think "2,x" then later "3,x"
00296Cr 3               
00296Cr 3  88                           dey
00296Dr 3  D0 EA                        bne @inner_loop ; go back for one more shift?
00296Fr 3               
00296Fr 3  E8                           inx
002970r 3  E4 rr                        cpx tmp3
002972r 3  D0 E1                        bne @outer_loop ; go back for eight more shifts?
002974r 3               
002974r 3                               ; all done, store high word of result
002974r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002976r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
002978r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
00297Ar 3  80 04                        bra @done
00297Cr 3               
00297Cr 3               @zero:
00297Cr 3  74 02                        stz 2,x
00297Er 3  74 03                        stz 3,x
002980r 3               @done:
002980r 3  60           z_um_star:      rts
002981r 3               
002981r 3               
002981r 3               
002981r 3               ; ## UNLOOP ( -- )(R: n1 n2 n3 ---) "Drop loop control from Return stack"
002981r 3               ; ## "unloop"  auto  ANS core
002981r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/UNLOOP
002981r 3                       ;
002981r 3                       ; Note that 6xPLA uses just as many bytes as a loop would
002981r 3                       ; """
002981r 3               xt_unloop:
002981r 3                               ; Drop fudge number (limit/start from DO/?DO off the
002981r 3                               ; return stack
002981r 3  68                           pla
002982r 3  68                           pla
002983r 3  68                           pla
002984r 3  68                           pla
002985r 3               
002985r 3                               ; Now drop the LEAVE address that was below them off
002985r 3                               ; the Return Stack as well
002985r 3  68                           pla
002986r 3  68                           pla
002987r 3               
002987r 3  60           z_unloop:       rts
002988r 3               
002988r 3               
002988r 3               ; ## UNTIL (C: dest -- ) ( -- ) "Loop flow control"
002988r 3               ; ## "until"  auto  ANS core
002988r 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/UNTIL"""
002988r 3               xt_until:
002988r 3                               ; Compile a 0BRANCH
002988r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>zero_branch_runtime
00298Ar 3  A9 rr                        lda #<zero_branch_runtime
00298Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
00298Fr 3               
00298Fr 3                               ; The address to loop back to is on the stack.
00298Fr 3                               ; Just compile it as the destination for the
00298Fr 3                               ; 0branch.
00298Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_comma
002992r 3               
002992r 3  60           z_until:        rts
002993r 3               
002993r 3               
002993r 3               ; ## UNUSED ( -- u ) "Return size of space available to Dictionary"
002993r 3               ; ## "unused"  auto  ANS core ext
002993r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/UNUSED
002993r 3                       ; UNUSED does not include the ACCEPT history buffers. Total RAM
002993r 3                       ; should be HERE + UNUSED + <history buffer size>, the last of which
002993r 3                       ; defaults to $400
002993r 3                       ; """
002993r 3               xt_unused:
002993r 3  CA                           dex
002994r 3  CA                           dex
002995r 3               
002995r 3  A9 FF                        lda #<cp_end
002997r 3  38                           sec
002998r 3  E5 rr                        sbc cp
00299Ar 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
00299Cr 3               
00299Cr 3  A9 7F                        lda #>cp_end
00299Er 3  E5 rr                        sbc cp+1
0029A0r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0029A2r 3               
0029A2r 3  60           z_unused:       rts
0029A3r 3               
0029A3r 3               
0029A3r 3               ; ## UPDATE ( -- ) "Mark current block as dirty"
0029A3r 3               ; ## "update"  auto  ANS block
0029A3r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/block/UPDATE"""
0029A3r 3               xt_update:
0029A3r 3                               ; Turn on the dirty bit. We can't use TSB here because it only
0029A3r 3                               ; has Absolute and Direct Pages addressing modes
0029A3r 3  A0 2C                        ldy #buffstatus_offset
0029A5r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
0029A7r 3  09 02                        ora #2          ; Turn on dirty flag (bit 2)
0029A9r 3  91 rr                        sta (up),y
0029ABr 3               
0029ABr 3  60           z_update:       rts
0029ACr 3               
0029ACr 3               
0029ACr 3               ; ## USERADDR ( -- addr ) "Push address of base address of user variables"
0029ACr 3               ; ## "useraddr"  tested  Tali Forth
0029ACr 3               xt_useraddr:
0029ACr 3  CA                           dex
0029ADr 3  CA                           dex
0029AEr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<up
0029B0r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0029B2r 3  A9 rr                        lda #>up
0029B4r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0029B6r 3               
0029B6r 3  60           z_useraddr:     rts
0029B7r 3               
0029B7r 3               
0029B7r 3               ; ## VALUE ( n "name" -- ) "Define a value"
0029B7r 3               ; ## "value"  auto  ANS core
0029B7r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/VALUE
0029B7r 3                       ;
0029B7r 3                       ; This is a dummy header for the WORDLIST. The actual code is
0029B7r 3                       ; identical to that of CONSTANT
0029B7r 3                       ; """
0029B7r 3               
0029B7r 3               
0029B7r 3               ; ## VARIABLE ( "name" -- ) "Define a variable"
0029B7r 3               ; ## "variable"  auto  ANS core
0029B7r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/VARIABLE
0029B7r 3                       ; There are various Forth definitions for this word, such as
0029B7r 3                       ; `CREATE 1 CELLS ALLOT`  or  `CREATE 0 ,`  We use a variant of the
0029B7r 3                       ; second one so the variable is initialized to zero
0029B7r 3                       ; """
0029B7r 3               xt_variable:
0029B7r 3                               ; we let CREATE do the heavy lifting
0029B7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_create
0029BAr 3               
0029BAr 3                               ; there is no "STZ (CP)" so we have to do this the hard
0029BAr 3                               ; way
0029BAr 3  A9 00                        lda #0
0029BCr 3               
0029BCr 3  92 rr                        sta (cp)
0029BEr 3  E6 rr                        inc cp
0029C0r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
0029C2r 3  E6 rr                        inc cp+1
0029C4r 3               @1:
0029C4r 3  92 rr                        sta (cp)
0029C6r 3  E6 rr                        inc cp
0029C8r 3  D0 02                        bne @2
0029CAr 3  E6 rr                        inc cp+1
0029CCr 3               @2:
0029CCr 3                               ; Now we need to adjust the length of the complete word by two
0029CCr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr adjust_z
0029CFr 3               
0029CFr 3  60           z_variable:     rts
0029D0r 3               
0029D0r 3               
0029D0r 3               ; ## WHILE ( C: dest -- orig dest ) ( x -- ) "Loop flow control"
0029D0r 3               ; ## "while"  auto  ANS core
0029D0r 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/WHILE"""
0029D0r 3               xt_while:
0029D0r 3                               ; Compile a 0branch
0029D0r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>zero_branch_runtime
0029D2r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<zero_branch_runtime
0029D4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
0029D7r 3               
0029D7r 3                               ; Put the address (here) where the destination
0029D7r 3                               ; address needs to go so it can be put there later.
0029D7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_here
0029DAr 3               
0029DAr 3                               ; Fill in the destination address with 0 for now.
0029DAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero
0029DDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_comma
0029E0r 3               
0029E0r 3                               ; Swap the two addresses on the stack.
0029E0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_swap
0029E3r 3               
0029E3r 3  60           z_while:        rts
0029E4r 3               
0029E4r 3               
0029E4r 3               ; ## WITHIN ( n1 n2 n3 -- ) "See if within a range"
0029E4r 3               ; ## "within"  auto  ANS core ext
0029E4r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/WITHIN
0029E4r 3                       ;
0029E4r 3                       ; This an assembler version of the ANS Forth implementation
0029E4r 3                       ; at https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/WITHIN which is
0029E4r 3                       ; OVER - >R - R> U<  note there is an alternative high-level version
0029E4r 3                       ; ROT TUCK > -ROT > INVERT AND
0029E4r 3                       ; """"
0029E4r 3               xt_within:
0029E4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_3
0029E7r 3               
0029E7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_over
0029EAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_minus
0029EDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_r
0029F0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_minus
0029F3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_from
0029F6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_u_less_than
0029F9r 3               
0029F9r 3  60           z_within:       rts
0029FAr 3               
0029FAr 3               
0029FAr 3               ; ## WORD ( char "name " -- caddr ) "Parse input stream"
0029FAr 3               ; ## "word"  auto  ANS core
0029FAr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/WORD
0029FAr 3                       ; Obsolete parsing word included for backwards compatibility only.
0029FAr 3                       ; Do not use this, use `PARSE` or `PARSE-NAME`. Skips leading delimiters
0029FAr 3                       ; and copies word to storage area for a maximum size of 255 bytes.
0029FAr 3                       ; Returns the result as a counted string (requires COUNT to convert
0029FAr 3                       ; to modern format), and inserts a space after the string. See "Forth
0029FAr 3                       ; Programmer's Handbook" 3rd edition p. 159 and
0029FAr 3                       ; http://www.forth200x.org/documents/html/rationale.html#rat:core:PARSE
0029FAr 3                       ; for discussions of why you shouldn't be using WORD anymore.
0029FAr 3                       ;
0029FAr 3                       ; Forth
0029FAr 3                       ; would be   PARSE DUP BUFFER1 C! OUTPUT 1+ SWAP MOVE BUFFER1
0029FAr 3                       ; We only allow input of 255 chars. Seriously, use PARSE-NAME.
0029FAr 3                       ; """
0029FAr 3               
0029FAr 3               xt_word:
0029FAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
0029FDr 3               
0029FDr 3                               ; Skip over leading delimiters - this is like PARSE-NAME,
0029FDr 3                               ; but unlike PARSE
0029FDr 3  A4 rr                        ldy toin                ; >IN
0029FFr 3               @loop:
0029FFr 3  C4 rr                        cpy ciblen              ; quit if end of input
002A01r 3  F0 09                        beq @found_char
002A03r 3  B1 rr                        lda (cib),y
002A05r 3  D5 00                        cmp 0,x                 ; ASCII of delimiter
002A07r 3  D0 03                        bne @found_char
002A09r 3               
002A09r 3  C8                           iny
002A0Ar 3  80 F3                        bra @loop
002A0Cr 3               @found_char:
002A0Cr 3                               ; Save index of where word starts
002A0Cr 3  84 rr                        sty toin
002A0Er 3               
002A0Er 3                               ; The real work is done by parse
002A0Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_parse            ; Returns ( addr u )
002A11r 3               
002A11r 3                               ; Convert the modern ( addr u ) string format to obsolete
002A11r 3                               ; ( caddr ) format. We just do this in the Dictionary
002A11r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002A13r 3  92 rr                        sta (cp)                ; Save length of string
002A15r 3  48                           pha                     ; Keep copy of length for later
002A16r 3               
002A16r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup              ; ( addr u u )
002A19r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
002A1Br 3  18                           clc
002A1Cr 3  69 01                        adc #1
002A1Er 3  95 02                        sta 2,x                 ; LSB of CP
002A20r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
002A22r 3  69 00                        adc #0
002A24r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x                 ; ( addr cp+1 u )
002A26r 3               
002A26r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_move
002A29r 3               
002A29r 3                               ; Return caddr
002A29r 3  CA                           dex
002A2Ar 3  CA                           dex
002A2Br 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
002A2Dr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002A2Fr 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
002A31r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002A33r 3               
002A33r 3                               ; Adjust CP
002A33r 3  68                           pla                     ; length of string
002A34r 3  18                           clc
002A35r 3  65 rr                        adc cp
002A37r 3  85 rr                        sta cp
002A39r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
002A3Br 3  69 00                        adc #0                  ; we only need the carry
002A3Dr 3  85 rr                        sta cp+1
002A3Fr 3  60           z_word:         rts
002A40r 3               
002A40r 3               
002A40r 3               ; ## WORDLIST ( -- wid ) "Create new wordlist (from pool of 8)"
002A40r 3               ; ## "wordlist" auto ANS search
002A40r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/search/WORDLIST
002A40r 3                       ; See the tutorial on Wordlists and the Search Order for
002A40r 3                       ; more information.
002A40r 3                       ; """
002A40r 3               
002A40r 3               xt_wordlist:
002A40r 3                               ; Get the current number of wordlists
002A40r 3  A0 05                        ldy #num_wordlists_offset
002A42r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y      ; This is a byte variable, so only
002A44r 3                                               ; the LSB needs to be checked.
002A44r 3               
002A44r 3                               ; See if we are already at the max.
002A44r 3  C9 0C                        cmp #max_wordlists
002A46r 3  D0 05                        bne @ok
002A48r 3               
002A48r 3                               ; Print an error message if all wordlists used.
002A48r 3  A9 0B                        lda #err_wordlist
002A4Ar 3  4C rr rr                     jmp error
002A4Dr 3               
002A4Dr 3               @ok:
002A4Dr 3  1A                           inc             ; Increment the wordlist#
002A4Er 3  91 rr                        sta (up),y      ; Save it into byte variable #wordlists
002A50r 3  CA                           dex             ; and put it on the stack.
002A51r 3  CA                           dex
002A52r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002A54r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x         ; 12 is the max, so upper byte is always zero.
002A56r 3               
002A56r 3  60           z_wordlist:     rts
002A57r 3               
002A57r 3               
002A57r 3               
002A57r 3               ; ## WORDS ( -- ) "Print known words from Dictionary"
002A57r 3               ; ## "words"  tested  ANS tools
002A57r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/tools/WORDS
002A57r 3                       ; This is pretty much only used at the command line so we can
002A57r 3                       ; be slow and try to save space.
002A57r 3                       ; """
002A57r 3               
002A57r 3               xt_words:
002A57r 3                               ; we follow Gforth by starting on the next
002A57r 3                               ; line
002A57r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
002A5Ar 3               
002A5Ar 3                               ; We pretty-format the output by inserting a line break
002A5Ar 3                               ; before the end of the line. We can get away with pushing
002A5Ar 3                               ; the counter to the stack because this is usually an
002A5Ar 3                               ; interactive word and speed is not that important
002A5Ar 3  A9 00                        lda #0
002A5Cr 3  48                           pha
002A5Dr 3               
002A5Dr 3                               ; Set up for traversing the wordlist search order.
002A5Dr 3  CA                           dex                     ; Make room on the stack for
002A5Er 3  CA                           dex                     ; a dictionary pointer.
002A5Fr 3  64 rr                        stz tmp3                ; Start at the beginning of
002A61r 3                                                       ; the search order.
002A61r 3               @wordlist_loop:
002A61r 3  A0 1E                        ldy #num_order_offset   ; Check against byte variable #ORDER.
002A63r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp3
002A65r 3  D1 rr                        cmp (up),y              ; See if we are done.
002A67r 3  D0 02                        bne @have_wordlist
002A69r 3               
002A69r 3                               ; We ran out of wordlists to search.
002A69r 3  80 44                        bra @words_done
002A6Br 3               
002A6Br 3               @have_wordlist:
002A6Br 3                               ; start with last word in Dictionary
002A6Br 3                               ; Get the current wordlist id
002A6Br 3  18                           clc                     ; Index into byte array SEARCH-ORDER.
002A6Cr 3  69 1F                        adc #search_order_offset
002A6Er 3  A8                           tay
002A6Fr 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y              ; Get the index into array WORDLISTS
002A71r 3               
002A71r 3                               ; Get the DP for that wordlist.
002A71r 3  0A                           asl                     ; Turn offset into cells offset.
002A72r 3  18                           clc
002A73r 3  69 06                        adc #wordlists_offset
002A75r 3  A8                           tay
002A76r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y              ; Save the DP for this wordlist
002A78r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x                 ; on the stack. ( nt )
002A7Ar 3  C8                           iny
002A7Br 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
002A7Dr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002A7Fr 3               
002A7Fr 3               @loop:
002A7Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup              ; ( nt nt )
002A82r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_name_to_string   ; ( nt addr u )
002A85r 3               
002A85r 3                               ; Insert line break if we're about to go past the end of the
002A85r 3                               ; line
002A85r 3  68                           pla
002A86r 3  18                           clc
002A87r 3  75 00                        adc 0,x
002A89r 3  1A                           inc                     ; don't forget the space between words
002A8Ar 3  C9 4F                        cmp #MAX_LINE_LENGTH    ; usually 79
002A8Cr 3  90 05                        bcc @1
002A8Er 3               
002A8Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
002A91r 3  A9 00                        lda #0
002A93r 3               @1:
002A93r 3  48                           pha
002A94r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type             ; ( nt )
002A97r 3               
002A97r 3  A9 20                        lda #AscSP
002A99r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
002A9Cr 3               
002A9Cr 3                               ; get next word, which begins two down
002A9Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_one_plus         ; 1+
002A9Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_one_plus         ; 1+
002AA2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_fetch            ; @ ( nt+1 )
002AA5r 3               
002AA5r 3                               ; if next address is zero, we're done
002AA5r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002AA7r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002AA9r 3  D0 D4                        bne @loop
002AABr 3               
002AABr 3                               ; Move on to the next wordlist in the search order.
002AABr 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp3
002AADr 3  80 B2                        bra @wordlist_loop
002AAFr 3               
002AAFr 3               @words_done:
002AAFr 3  68                           pla                     ; dump counter
002AB0r 3               
002AB0r 3  E8                           inx
002AB1r 3  E8                           inx
002AB2r 3               
002AB2r 3  60           z_words:        rts
002AB3r 3               
002AB3r 3               
002AB3r 3               
002AB3r 3               ; ## WORDSIZE ( nt -- u ) "Get size of word in bytes"
002AB3r 3               ; ## "wordsize"  auto  Tali Forth
002AB3r 3                       ; """Given an word's name token (nt), return the size of the
002AB3r 3                       ; word's payload size in bytes (CFA plus PFA) in bytes. Does not
002AB3r 3                       ; count the final RTS.
002AB3r 3                       ; """
002AB3r 3               xt_wordsize:
002AB3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002AB6r 3               
002AB6r 3                               ; We get the start address of the word from its header entry
002AB6r 3                               ; for the start of the actual code (execution token, xt)
002AB6r 3                               ; which is four bytes down, and the pointer to the end of the
002AB6r 3                               ; code (z_word, six bytes down)
002AB6r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002AB8r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
002ABAr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
002ABCr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
002ABEr 3               
002ABEr 3  A0 06                        ldy #6
002AC0r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y    ; LSB of z
002AC2r 3  88                           dey
002AC3r 3  88                           dey
002AC4r 3               
002AC4r 3  38                           sec
002AC5r 3  F1 rr                        sbc (tmp1),y    ; LSB of xt
002AC7r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002AC9r 3               
002AC9r 3  A0 07                        ldy #7
002ACBr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y    ; MSB of z
002ACDr 3  88                           dey
002ACEr 3  88                           dey
002ACFr 3               
002ACFr 3  F1 rr                        sbc (tmp1),y    ; MSB of xt
002AD1r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002AD3r 3               
002AD3r 3  60           z_wordsize:     rts
002AD4r 3               
002AD4r 3               
002AD4r 3               ; ## XOR ( n n -- n ) "Logically XOR TOS and NOS"
002AD4r 3               ; ## "xor"  auto  ANS core
002AD4r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/XOR"""
002AD4r 3               xt_xor:
002AD4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
002AD7r 3               
002AD7r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002AD9r 3  55 02                        eor 2,x
002ADBr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
002ADDr 3               
002ADDr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
002ADFr 3  55 03                        eor 3,x
002AE1r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
002AE3r 3               
002AE3r 3  E8                           inx
002AE4r 3  E8                           inx
002AE5r 3               
002AE5r 3  60           z_xor:          rts
002AE6r 3               
002AE6r 3               
002AE6r 3               ; ## ZERO ( -- 0 ) "Push 0 to Data Stack"
002AE6r 3               ; ## "0"  auto  Tali Forth
002AE6r 3                       ; """The disassembler assumes that this routine does not use Y. Note
002AE6r 3                       ; that CASE and FORTH-WORDLIST use the same routine, as the WD for Forth
002AE6r 3                       ; is 0."""
002AE6r 3               xt_case:
002AE6r 3               xt_forth_wordlist:
002AE6r 3               xt_zero:
002AE6r 3  CA                           dex             ; push
002AE7r 3  CA                           dex
002AE8r 3  74 00                        stz 0,x
002AEAr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002AECr 3               z_case:
002AECr 3               z_forth_wordlist:
002AECr 3               z_zero:
002AECr 3  60                           rts
002AEDr 3               
002AEDr 3               
002AEDr 3               ; ## ZERO_EQUAL ( n -- f ) "Check if TOS is zero"
002AEDr 3               ; ## "0="  auto  ANS core
002AEDr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/ZeroEqual"""
002AEDr 3               
002AEDr 3               xt_zero_equal:
002AEDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002AF0r 3               
002AF0r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002AF2r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002AF4r 3  F0 04                        beq @zero
002AF6r 3               
002AF6r 3                               ; not a zero, so we need a FALSE flag (0)
002AF6r 3  A9 00                        lda #0
002AF8r 3  80 02                        bra @store
002AFAr 3               @zero:
002AFAr 3                               ; We have a zero, so we need a TRUE flag (-1)
002AFAr 3  A9 FF                        lda #$ff
002AFCr 3               @store:
002AFCr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002AFEr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002B00r 3               
002B00r 3  60           z_zero_equal:   rts
002B01r 3               
002B01r 3               
002B01r 3               
002B01r 3               ; ## ZERO_GREATER ( n -- f ) "Return a TRUE flag if TOS is positive"
002B01r 3               ; ## "0>"  auto  ANS core ext
002B01r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Zeromore"""
002B01r 3               
002B01r 3               xt_zero_greater:
002B01r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002B04r 3               
002B04r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0          ; Default is FALSE (TOS is negative)
002B06r 3               
002B06r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB
002B08r 3  30 05                        bmi @done       ; TOS is negative, keep FLASE
002B0Ar 3  15 00                        ora 0,x
002B0Cr 3  F0 01                        beq @done       ; TOS is zero, keep FALSE
002B0Er 3               
002B0Er 3  88                           dey             ; TOS is postive, make true
002B0Fr 3               @done:
002B0Fr 3  98                           tya
002B10r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002B12r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002B14r 3               
002B14r 3  60           z_zero_greater: rts
002B15r 3               
002B15r 3               
002B15r 3               
002B15r 3               ; ## ZERO_LESS ( n -- f ) "Return a TRUE flag if TOS negative"
002B15r 3               ; ## "0<"  auto  ANS core
002B15r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Zeroless"""
002B15r 3               
002B15r 3               xt_zero_less:
002B15r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002B18r 3               
002B18r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0          ; Default is FALSE (TOS positive)
002B1Ar 3               
002B1Ar 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB
002B1Cr 3  10 01                        bpl @done       ; TOS is positive, so keep FALSE
002B1Er 3               
002B1Er 3  88                           dey             ; TOS is negative, make TRUE
002B1Fr 3               @done:
002B1Fr 3  98                           tya
002B20r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002B22r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002B24r 3               
002B24r 3  60           z_zero_less:    rts
002B25r 3               
002B25r 3               
002B25r 3               
002B25r 3               ; ## ZERO_UNEQUAL ( m -- f ) "Return TRUE flag if not zero"
002B25r 3               ; ## "0<>"  auto  ANS core ext
002B25r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Zerone"""
002B25r 3               
002B25r 3               xt_zero_unequal:
002B25r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002B28r 3               
002B28r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0          ; default false
002B2Ar 3               
002B2Ar 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002B2Cr 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002B2Er 3  F0 01                        beq @got_zero
002B30r 3               
002B30r 3  88                           dey
002B31r 3               @got_zero:
002B31r 3  98                           tya
002B32r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002B34r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002B36r 3               
002B36r 3  60           z_zero_unequal: rts
002B37r 3               
002B37r 3               
002B37r 3               
002B37r 3               ; ==========================================================
002B37r 3               ; EDITOR words
002B37r 3               
002B37r 3               ; This routine is used by both enter-screen and erase-screen
002B37r 3               ; to get a buffer for the given screen number and set SCR to
002B37r 3               ; the given screen number.  This word is not in the dictionary.
002B37r 3               xt_editor_screen_helper:
002B37r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup
002B3Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_scr
002B3Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_store
002B40r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_buffer
002B43r 3               z_editor_screen_helper:
002B43r 3  60                           rts
002B44r 3               
002B44r 3               
002B44r 3               ; ## EDITOR_ENTER_SCREEN ( scr# -- ) "Enter all lines for given screen"
002B44r 3               ; ## "enter-screen"  auto  Tali Editor
002B44r 3               
002B44r 3               xt_editor_enter_screen:
002B44r 3                               ; Set the variable SCR and get a buffer for the
002B44r 3                               ; given screen number.
002B44r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_editor_screen_helper
002B47r 3               
002B47r 3                               ; Drop the buffer address.
002B47r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_drop
002B4Ar 3               
002B4Ar 3                               ; Overwrite the lines one at a time.
002B4Ar 3  64 rr                        stz editor1
002B4Cr 3               @prompt_loop:
002B4Cr 3                               ; Put the current line number on the stack.
002B4Cr 3  CA                           dex
002B4Dr 3  CA                           dex
002B4Er 3  A5 rr                        lda editor1
002B50r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002B52r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002B54r 3               
002B54r 3                               ; Use the O word to prompt for overwrite.
002B54r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_editor_o
002B57r 3               
002B57r 3                               ; Move on to the next line.
002B57r 3  E6 rr                        inc editor1
002B59r 3  A9 10                        lda #16
002B5Br 3  C5 rr                        cmp editor1
002B5Dr 3  D0 ED                        bne @prompt_loop
002B5Fr 3               
002B5Fr 3               z_editor_enter_screen:
002B5Fr 3  60                           rts
002B60r 3               
002B60r 3               
002B60r 3               
002B60r 3               ; ## EDITOR_ERASE_SCREEN ( scr# -- ) "Erase all lines for given screen"
002B60r 3               ; ## "erase-screen"  tested  Tali Editor
002B60r 3               xt_editor_erase_screen:
002B60r 3                               ; Set the variable SCR and get a buffer for the
002B60r 3                               ; given screen number.
002B60r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_editor_screen_helper
002B63r 3               
002B63r 3                               ; Put 1024 (chars/screen) on stack.
002B63r 3  CA                           dex
002B64r 3  CA                           dex
002B65r 3  74 00                        stz 0,x
002B67r 3  A9 04                        lda #4          ; 4 in MSB makes 1024 ($400).
002B69r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002B6Br 3               
002B6Br 3                               ; Erase the entire block (fill with spaces).
002B6Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_blank
002B6Er 3               
002B6Er 3                               ; Mark buffer as updated.
002B6Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_update
002B71r 3               
002B71r 3               z_editor_erase_screen:
002B71r 3  60                           rts
002B72r 3               
002B72r 3               
002B72r 3               ; ## EDITOR_EL ( line# -- ) "Erase the given line number"
002B72r 3               ; ## "el"  tested  Tali Editor
002B72r 3               xt_editor_el:
002B72r 3                               ; Turn the line number into buffer offset.
002B72r 3                               ; This also loads the block into the buffer if it's
002B72r 3                               ; not there for some reason.
002B72r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_editor_line
002B75r 3               
002B75r 3                               ; Put 64 (# of chars/line) on the stack.
002B75r 3  CA                           dex
002B76r 3  CA                           dex
002B77r 3  A9 40                        lda #64
002B79r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002B7Br 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002B7Dr 3               
002B7Dr 3                               ; Fill with spaces.
002B7Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_blank
002B80r 3               
002B80r 3                               ; Mark buffer as updated.
002B80r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_update
002B83r 3               
002B83r 3  60           z_editor_el:    rts
002B84r 3               
002B84r 3               
002B84r 3               ; ## EDITOR_L ( -- ) "List the current screen"
002B84r 3               ; ## "l"  tested  Tali Editor
002B84r 3               
002B84r 3               xt_editor_l:
002B84r 3                               ; Load the current screen
002B84r 3  CA                           dex             ; Put SCR on the stack.
002B85r 3  CA                           dex
002B86r 3  A0 02                        ldy #scr_offset
002B88r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
002B8Ar 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002B8Cr 3  C8                           iny
002B8Dr 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
002B8Fr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002B91r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_block    ; Get the current screen.
002B94r 3               
002B94r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
002B97r 3               
002B97r 3                               ; Print the screen number.
002B97r 3                               ; We're using sliteral, so we need to set up the
002B97r 3                               ; appropriate data structure (see sliteral)
002B97r 3  80 08                        bra @after_screen_msg
002B99r 3               
002B99r 3               @screen_msg:
002B99r 3  53 63 72 65                  .byte "Screen #"
002B9Dr 3  65 6E 20 23  
002BA1r 3               
002BA1r 3               @after_screen_msg:
002BA1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr sliteral_runtime
002BA4r 3  rr rr 08 00                  .word @screen_msg, @after_screen_msg-@screen_msg
002BA8r 3               
002BA8r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
002BABr 3               
002BABr 3                               ; Put the screen number and printed size for u.r on the stack.
002BABr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_scr
002BAEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_fetch
002BB1r 3  CA                           dex
002BB2r 3  CA                           dex
002BB3r 3  A9 04                        lda #4          ; four spaces
002BB5r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002BB7r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002BB9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_u_dot_r
002BBCr 3               
002BBCr 3                               ; The address of the buffer is currently on the stack.
002BBCr 3                               ; Print 64 chars at a time. TYPE uses tmp1, so we'll
002BBCr 3                               ; keep track of the line number in tmp3.
002BBCr 3  64 rr                        stz tmp3
002BBEr 3               
002BBEr 3               @line_loop:
002BBEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
002BC1r 3               
002BC1r 3                               ; Print the line number (2-space fixed width)
002BC1r 3  CA                           dex
002BC2r 3  CA                           dex
002BC3r 3  CA                           dex
002BC4r 3  CA                           dex
002BC5r 3  74 03                        stz 3,x
002BC7r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp3
002BC9r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
002BCBr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002BCDr 3  A9 02                        lda #2
002BCFr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002BD1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_u_dot_r
002BD4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
002BD7r 3               
002BD7r 3                               ; Print one line using the address on the stack.
002BD7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup
002BDAr 3  CA                           dex
002BDBr 3  CA                           dex
002BDCr 3  A9 40                        lda #64
002BDEr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002BE0r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002BE2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
002BE5r 3               
002BE5r 3                               ; Add 64 to the address on the stack to move to the next line.
002BE5r 3  18                           clc
002BE6r 3  A9 40                        lda #64
002BE8r 3  75 00                        adc 0,x
002BEAr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002BECr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
002BEEr 3  69 00                        adc #0      ; Add carry
002BF0r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002BF2r 3               
002BF2r 3                               ; Increment the line number (held in tmp3)
002BF2r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp3
002BF4r 3               
002BF4r 3                               ; See if we are done.
002BF4r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp3
002BF6r 3  C9 10                        cmp #16
002BF8r 3  D0 C4                        bne @line_loop
002BFAr 3               
002BFAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
002BFDr 3                               ; Drop the address on the stack.
002BFDr 3  E8                           inx
002BFEr 3  E8                           inx
002BFFr 3               
002BFFr 3  60           z_editor_l:            rts
002C00r 3               
002C00r 3               
002C00r 3               
002C00r 3               ; ## EDITOR_LINE ( line# -- c-addr ) "Turn a line number into address in current screen"
002C00r 3               ; ## "line"  tested  Tali Editor
002C00r 3               
002C00r 3               xt_editor_line:
002C00r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002C03r 3               
002C03r 3                               ; Multiply the TOS by 64 (chars/line) to compute offset.
002C03r 3  A0 06                        ldy #6          ; *64 is same as left shift 6 times.
002C05r 3               @shift_tos_left:
002C05r 3  16 00                        asl 0,x         ; Shift TOS to the left
002C07r 3  36 01                        rol 1,x         ; ROL brings MSb from lower byte.
002C09r 3  88                           dey
002C0Ar 3  D0 F9                        bne @shift_tos_left
002C0Cr 3                               ; Load the current screen into a buffer
002C0Cr 3                               ; and get the buffer address
002C0Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_scr
002C0Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_fetch
002C12r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_block
002C15r 3               
002C15r 3                               ; Add the offset to the buffer base address.
002C15r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_plus
002C18r 3               
002C18r 3  60           z_editor_line:  rts
002C19r 3               
002C19r 3               
002C19r 3               
002C19r 3               ; ## EDITOR_O ( line# -- ) "Overwrite the given line"
002C19r 3               ; ## "o"  tested  Tali Editor
002C19r 3               xt_editor_o:
002C19r 3                               ; Print prompt
002C19r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
002C1Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup
002C1Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_two
002C22r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_u_dot_r
002C25r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
002C28r 3  A9 2A                        lda #42         ; ASCII for *
002C2Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
002C2Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
002C30r 3               
002C30r 3                               ; Accept new input (directly into the buffer)
002C30r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_editor_line
002C33r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup      ; Save a copy of the line address for later.
002C36r 3  CA                           dex
002C37r 3  CA                           dex
002C38r 3  A9 40                        lda #64         ; chars/line
002C3Ar 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002C3Cr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002C3Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_accept
002C41r 3               
002C41r 3                               ; Fill the rest with spaces.
002C41r 3                               ; Stack is currently ( line_address numchars_from_accept )
002C41r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup
002C44r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_not_rote ; -rot
002C47r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_plus
002C4Ar 3  CA                           dex
002C4Br 3  CA                           dex
002C4Cr 3  A9 40                        lda #64         ; chars/line
002C4Er 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002C50r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002C52r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_rot
002C55r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_minus
002C58r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_blank
002C5Br 3               
002C5Br 3                               ; Mark buffer as updated.
002C5Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_update
002C5Er 3               
002C5Er 3  60           z_editor_o:     rts
002C5Fr 3               
002C5Fr 3               ; ## LCDPUT ( s -- ) "Print single character to LCD"
002C5Fr 3               ; ## "lcdput" coded Custom
002C5Fr 3               xt_lcdput:
002C5Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1

002C62r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x

002C64r 3                               jsr lcd_print
002C64r 3                       .endif

002C67r 3               
002C67r 3               
002C67r 3               ; ## LCDPRINT ( addr u -- ) "Print string to LCD"
002C67r 3               ; ## "lcdprint"  coded Custom
002C67r 3               
002C67r 3               xt_lcdprint:
002C67r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
002C6Ar 3               
002C6Ar 3                               ; Save the starting address into tmp1
002C6Ar 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
002C6Cr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
002C6Er 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
002C70r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
002C72r 3               @loop:
002C72r 3                               ; done if length is zero
002C72r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002C74r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002C76r 3  F0 12                        beq @done
002C78r 3               
002C78r 3                               ; Send the current character
002C78r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp1)
002C7Ar 3                       .ifdef lcd_print
002C7Ar 3                               jsr lcd_print      ; avoids stack foolery
002C7Ar 3                       .endif
002C7Ar 3                               ; Move the address along (in tmp1)
002C7Ar 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1
002C7Cr 3  D0 02                        bne @1
002C7Er 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1+1
002C80r 3               @1:
002C80r 3                               ; Reduce the count (on the data stack)
002C80r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002C82r 3  D0 02                        bne @2
002C84r 3  D6 01                        dec 1,x
002C86r 3               @2:
002C86r 3  D6 00                        dec 0,x
002C88r 3               
002C88r 3  80 E8                        bra @loop
002C8Ar 3               @done:
002C8Ar 3  E8                           inx
002C8Br 3  E8                           inx
002C8Cr 3  E8                           inx
002C8Dr 3  E8                           inx
002C8Er 3               
002C8Er 3  60           z_lcdprint:         rts

002CAEr 3               ; ## "sd_readsector" coded Custom
002CAEr 3               xt_sd_readsector:

002CB1r 3                       .ifdef sd_readsector
002CB1r 3                               ; get and save storage address
002CB1r 3                               lda 0,x
002CB1r 3                               sta sd_buffer_address
002CB1r 3                               lda 1, x
002CB1r 3                               sta sd_buffer_address + 1

002CB1r 3                       .endif

002CF8r 3  C9 55                cmp #$55

003000r 3               ; ## cf_readsector ( double -- addr ) "Set LBA block and read to buffer"
003000r 3               ; ## "cf_readsector" coded Custom
003000r 3               xt_cf_readsector:
003000r 3               .ifdef cf_init
003000r 3  20 rr rr             jsr underflow_2
003003r 3                       ; most significant part is TOS
003003r 3  B5 00                lda 0, x
003005r 3  8D rr rr             sta CF_LBA + 2
003008r 3  B5 01                lda 1, x
00300Ar 3  8D rr rr             sta CF_LBA + 3
00300Dr 3                       ; least significant part is NOS
00300Dr 3  B5 02                lda 2, x
00300Fr 3  8D rr rr             sta CF_LBA + 0
003012r 3  B5 03                lda 3, x
003014r 3  8D rr rr             sta CF_LBA + 1
003017r 3                       ; LBA is set, now read sector
003017r 3  20 rr rr             jsr cf_init
00301Ar 3               
00301Ar 3  A9 rr                lda #<FAT_BUFFER
00301Cr 3  95 02                sta 2, x
00301Er 3               
00301Er 3  A9 rr                lda #>FAT_BUFFER
003020r 3               
003020r 3  95 03                sta 3, x
003022r 3               
003022r 3  20 rr rr             jsr cf_read_sector
003025r 3               
003025r 3                       ; return buffer address
003025r 3  E8                   inx
003026r 3  E8                   inx
003027r 3               .endif
003027r 3               z_cf_readsector:
003027r 3  60                   rts
003028r 3               
003028r 3               
003028r 3               
003028r 3               ; END
003028r 3               
003028r 3               
003028r 2                   .include "headers.s"          ; Headers of native words
003028r 3               ; Dictionary Headers for Tali Forth 2
003028r 3               ; Scot W. Stevenson <scot.stevenson@gmail.com>
003028r 3               ; First version: 05. Dec 2016 (Liara Forth)
003028r 3               ; This version: 29. Dec 2018
003028r 3               
003028r 3               ; Dictionary headers are kept separately from the code, which allows various
003028r 3               ; tricks in the code. We roughly follow the Gforth terminology: The Execution
003028r 3               ; Token (xt) is the address of the first byte of a word's code that can be, uh,
003028r 3               ; executed; the Name Token (nt) is a pointer to the beginning of the word's
003028r 3               ; header in the Dictionary. There the link to the next word in the Dictionary
003028r 3               ; is always one cell down from the current word's own nt. In the code itself,
003028r 3               ; we use "nt_<WORD>" for the nt and "xt_<WORD>" for the xt.
003028r 3               
003028r 3               ; This gives us the following header structure:
003028r 3               
003028r 3               ;              8 bit     8 bit
003028r 3               ;               LSB       MSB
003028r 3               ; nt_word ->  +--------+--------+
003028r 3               ;          +0 | Length | Status |
003028r 3               ;             +--------+--------+
003028r 3               ;          +2 | Next Header     | -> nt_next_word
003028r 3               ;             +-----------------+
003028r 3               ;          +4 | Start of Code   | -> xt_word
003028r 3               ;             +-----------------+
003028r 3               ;          +6 | End of Code     | -> z_word
003028r 3               ;             +--------+--------+
003028r 3               ;          +8 | Name   |        |
003028r 3               ;             +--------+--------+
003028r 3               ;             |        |        |
003028r 3               ;             +--------+--------+
003028r 3               ;             |        |  ...   | (name string does not end with a zero)
003028r 3               ;          +n +--------+--------+
003028r 3               
003028r 3               ; The Status Byte is created by adding the flags defined in definitions.asm,
003028r 3               ; which are:
003028r 3               
003028r 3               ;       CO - Compile Only
003028r 3               ;       IM - Immediate Word
003028r 3               ;       NN - Never Native Compile (must always be called by JSR)
003028r 3               ;       AN - Always Native Compile (may not be called by JSR)
003028r 3               ;       UF - Contains underflow check
003028r 3               ;       HC - Has CFA (words created by CREATE and DOES> only)
003028r 3               
003028r 3               ; Note there are currently two bits unused.
003028r 3               
003028r 3               ; By default, all existing words can be natively compiled (compiled inline) or
003028r 3               ; as a subroutine jump target; the system decides which variant to use based on
003028r 3               ; a threshold the user can set. By default, all user-created words are flagged
003028r 3               ; never-native. The user can override this by using the always-native word
003028r 3               ; just after defining their new word.  The NN flag forbids native compiling,
003028r 3               ; the AN flag forces it.
003028r 3               
003028r 3               ; The last word (top word in code) is always BYE. It is marked as the last word
003028r 3               ; by its value of 0000 in its Next Header field. The words are sorted with the
003028r 3               ; more common ones first (further down in code) so they are found earlier.
003028r 3               ; Anything to do with output comes later (further up) because things will
003028r 3               ; always be slow if there is a human involved.
003028r 3               
003028r 3               ; The initial skeleton of this list was automatically generated by a script
003028r 3               ; in the tools folder and then sorted by hand.
003028r 3               
003028r 3               nt_bye:
003028r 3  03                   .byte 3         ; length of word strings
003029r 3  00                   .byte 0         ; status byte
00302Ar 3  00 00                .word 0000      ; next word in Dictionary, 0000 signals end
00302Cr 3  rr rr                .word xt_bye    ; start of code block (xt of this word)
00302Er 3  rr rr                .word z_bye     ; end of code (RTS)
003030r 3  62 79 65             .byte "bye"     ; word name, always lower case, not zero-terminated
003033r 3               
003033r 3

003F2Ar 3               ; ; ASSEMBLER-WORDLIST
003F2Ar 3               
003F2Ar 3               ; ; Labels for the opcodes have the format "nt_asm_<OPC>" where a futher
003F2Ar 3               ; ; underscore replaces any dot present in the SAN mnemonic. The hash sign for
003F2Ar 3               ; ; immediate addressing is replaced by an "h" (for example, the label code for
003F2Ar 3               ; ; "lda.#" is "xt_adm_lda_h"). All opcodes are immediate.
003F2Ar 3               assembler_dictionary_start:
003F2Ar 3               ; nt_asm_adc_h:
003F2Ar 3               ; 		.byte 5, IM
003F2Ar 3               ;                 .word nt_asm_adc_x

003F2Ar 3               ; 		.byte "adc.#"

003F2Ar 3               ;                 .word nt_asm_adc_y

003F2Ar 3               ; 		.byte "adc.x"

003F2Ar 3               ;                 .word nt_asm_adc_z

003F2Ar 3               ; 		.byte "adc.y"

003F2Ar 3               
003F2Ar 3               ; All general strings must be zero-terminated, names start with "s_",
003F2Ar 3               ; aliases with "str_"
003F2Ar 3               
003F2Ar 3               str_ok =              0
003F2Ar 3               str_compile =         1
003F2Ar 3               str_redefined =       2
003F2Ar 3               str_wid_forth =       3
003F2Ar 3               str_abc_lower =       4
003F2Ar 3               str_abc_upper =       5
003F2Ar 3               str_wid_editor =      6

003F2Ar 3               str_wid_root =        8
003F2Ar 3               str_see_flags =       9
003F2Ar 3               str_see_nt =         10
003F2Ar 3               str_see_xt =         11
003F2Ar 3               str_see_size =       12
003F2Ar 3               
003F2Ar 3               ; Since we can't fit a 16-bit address in a register, we use indexes as offsets
003F2Ar 3               ; to tables as error and string numbers.

00418Dr 3               
00418Dr 3               ; These are used by the ENVIRONMENT? word and stored in the old string format:
00418Dr 3               ; Length byte first, then the string itself that is not rpt. not
00418Dr 3               ; zero-terminated. Note these are uppercase by ANS defintion. All start with
00418Dr 3               ; "envs_".
00418Dr 3               
00418Dr 3               ; These return a single-cell number

0041DBr 3  55 52 4E 2D  
0041DFr 3  53 54 41 43  
0041EAr 3  0B 53 54 41  envs_sc:        .byte 11, "STACK-CELLS"
0041EEr 3  43 4B 2D 43  
0041F2r 3  45 4C 4C 53  
0041F6r 3  09 57 4F 52  envs_wl:        .byte 9, "WORDLISTS"
0041FAr 3  44 4C 49 53  
0041FEr 3  54 53        
004200r 3               
004200r 3               ; These return a double-cell number
004200r 3  05 4D 41 58  envs_max_d:     .byte 5, "MAX-D"
004204r 3  2D 44        
004206r 3  06 4D 41 58  envs_max_ud:    .byte 6, "MAX-UD"
00420Ar 3  2D 55 44     
00420Dr 3               
00420Dr 3               ; END
00420Dr 3               
00420Dr 2               
00420Dr 2               ; High-level Forth words, see forth_code/README.md
00420Dr 2               forth_words_start:
00420Dr 2  20 63 72 20  .incbin "forth_code/forth_words.asc"
004211r 2  2E 28 20 52  
004215r 2  65 61 64 79
